------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Xhosa Bible: Psalms

<span id="an_1:1">1:1</span> Hayi, uyolo lomntu ongahambiyo ngecebo
labangendawo, Ongemiyo endleleni yaboni, Ongahlaliyo embuthweni
yabagxeki!

<span id="an_1:2">1:2</span> Yena unonelela umyalelo kaYehova; Ucamanga
ngomyalelo wakhe imini nobusuku:

<span id="an_1:3">1:3</span> Unjengomthi omiliselwe phezu kwemijelo
yamanzi, Onika isiqhamo sawo ngexesha lawo, Ogqabi lawo lingabuniyo;
Konke akwenzayo kophumelela.

<span id="an_1:4">1:4</span> Abanjalo abangendawo; Bona banjengomququ
ophetshethwa ngumoya.

<span id="an_1:5">1:5</span> Ngenxa yoko abangendawo abanakuma
emgwebeni, Naboni ebandleni lamalungisa.

<span id="an_1:6">1:6</span> Ngokuba uYehova uyayazi indlela
yamalungisa; Ke yona indlela yabangendawo iya kudaka.

<span id="an_2:1">2:1</span> Yini na ukuba iintlanga zenze
imbuthumbuthu, Izizwe zicamange into engeyakonto?

<span id="an_2:2">2:2</span> Ookumkani behlabathi bazimisile,
Izidwangube zabhunga NgoYehova nangoMthanjiswa wakhe;

<span id="an_2:3">2:3</span> Besithi, Masiziqhawule iimbophelelo zabo,
Sizilahle izintya zabo kuthi.

<span id="an_2:4">2:4</span> Ohleli emazulwini uyahleka, INkosi
iyabagculela.

<span id="an_2:5">2:5</span> Iya kwandula ithethe kubo ngomsindo wayo,
Ibakhwankqise ngokuvutha kwayo.

<span id="an_2:6">2:6</span> Ithi, Mna ke ndimmisile ukumkani wam Phezu
kweZiyon, intaba yam engcwele.

<span id="an_2:7">2:7</span> Athi yena, Ndiya kuwuvakalisa ummiselo:
UYehova uthe kum, UnguNyana wam wena; Mna namhla ndikuzele.

<span id="an_2:8">2:8</span> Cela kum, ndikunike iintlanga zibe lilifa
lakho, Iziphelo zehlabathi zibe zezakho.

<span id="an_2:9">2:9</span> Uya kuzivikiva ngentonga yentsimbi,
Uzihlekeze, zinge zizitya zodongwe.

<span id="an_2:10">2:10</span> Ngoko ke, nina bokumkani, qiqani; Bagwebi
basehlabathini, yalekani.

<span id="an_2:11">2:11</span> Mkhonzeni uYehova nisoyika, Gcobani
nithuthumela.

<span id="an_2:12">2:12</span> Mangeni uNyana, hleze aqumbe,
nitshabalale endleleni, Ngokuba ungahle uvuthe umsindo wakhe. Hayi,
uyolo lwabo bonke abazimela ngaye!

<span id="an_3:1">3:1</span> Umhobe kaDavide, ekubalekeni kwakhe
kuAbhisalom unyana wakhe. Yehova, hayi, ukuba baninzi
kwabandibandezelayo! Baninzi abasukela phezulu kum.

<span id="an_3:2">3:2</span> Baninzi abathi kumphefumlo wam,
Akunalusindiso kuThixo. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_3:3">3:3</span> Ke wena, Yehova, uyingweletshetshe kum,
Uluzuko lwam, umphakamisi wentloko yam.

<span id="an_3:4">3:4</span> Ndidanduluka kuYehova ngezwi lam,
Andiphendule entabeni yakhe engcwele. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_3:5">3:5</span> Ndalala phantsi, ndalala ubuthongo;
Ndavuka, ngokuba uYehova endixhasa.

<span id="an_3:6">3:6</span> Andizoyiki izigidi zabantu Abakhe uluhlu
lokulwa ngeenxa zonke kum.

<span id="an_3:7">3:7</span> Khawusuk’ ume, Yehova; ndisindise, Thixo
wam; Ngokuba uzibetha zonke iintshaba zam emhlathini; Amazinyo
abangendawo uyawaphula.

<span id="an_3:8">3:8</span> Usindiso lolukaYehova: Mayibe phezu
kwabantu bakho intsikelelo yakho. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_4:1">4:1</span> Kumongameli wokubethelwa izinto
ezineentambo. Umhobe kaDavide. Ekudandulukeni kwam ndiphendule, Thixo
wobulungisa bam; Embandezelweni yam wandenzela indawo ebanzi; Ndibabale,
uwuve umthandazo wam.

<span id="an_4:2">4:2</span> Nina, nyana babantu, kunini na uzuko lwam
niluhlazisa, Ningxamele into engeyakonto, nithanda amanga?
(Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_4:3">4:3</span> Yazini ke ukuba uYehova uzibalulele
owenceba; UYehova uyaphulaphula ndakudanduluka kuye.

<span id="an_4:4">4:4</span> Qumbani, ningoni; Thethani neentliziyo zenu
ezinkukweni zenu, nithi cwaka. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_4:5">4:5</span> Bingelelani imibingelelo yobulungisa,
Nikholose ngoYehova.

<span id="an_4:6">4:6</span> Baninzi abathi, Ngubani na owosibonisa
okulungileyo? Siphakamisele ukukhanya kobuso bakho, Yehova.

<span id="an_4:7">4:7</span> Uyivuyisile intliziyo yam, Kunexesha
lobuninzi bengqolowa yabo, newayini yabo entsha.

<span id="an_4:8">4:8</span> Ndiya kulala phantsi, ndilale ubuthongo
kwangoku, ndixolile, Ngokuba wena, Yehova, undihlalisa ndikholosile,
noko ndindedwa.

<span id="an_5:1">5:1</span> Kumongameli: ngogwali. Umhobe kaDavide.
Wabekele indlebe amazwi am, Yehova, Kuqonde ukucamanga kwam.

<span id="an_5:2">5:2</span> Libazele indlebe izwi lokuzibika kwam,
Kumkani wam, Thixo wam; Ngokuba ndithandaza kuwe.

<span id="an_5:3">5:3</span> Yehova, uya kuliva izwi lam kwakusasa,
Kwakusasa ndiya kuwusingisa kuwe umthandazo wam, ndibonisele.

<span id="an_5:4">5:4</span> Ngokuba wena akunguThixo onanze
okungendawo, Akanakuphambukela kuwe onobubi.

<span id="an_5:5">5:5</span> Abanakuma abaqhayisi phambi kwamehlo akho;
Uyabathiya bonke abasebenzi bobutshinga.

<span id="an_5:6">5:6</span> Uyabatshabalalisa abathetha amanga; Indoda
enegazi nenkohliso ilisikizi kuYehova.

<span id="an_5:7">5:7</span> Ke mna, ndinokungena endlwini yakho
ngenceba yakho eninzi, Ndiqubude, ndibhekise etempileni yakho engcwele
ngokukoyika.

<span id="an_5:8">5:8</span> Yehova, ndikhaphe ngobulungisa bakho ngenxa
yabandilaleleyo; Yilungelelanise indlela yakho phambi kwam.

<span id="an_5:9">5:9</span> Ngokuba emlonyeni wabo akukho nto imiyo,
Umbilini wabo ngumeyeliselo; Lingcwaba elivuliweyo umqala wabo; Bathetha
okugudileyo ngolwimi lwabo.

<span id="an_5:10">5:10</span> Bathwalise ityala, Thixo; Makatshitshe
amaqhinga abo; Elukreqweni lwabo oluninzi batyhale, Ngokuba
bakuphikisile.

<span id="an_5:11">5:11</span> Mabavuye bonke abazimela ngawe,
Bamemelele ngonaphakade, ubakhusele; Badlamke ngawe abalithandayo igama
lakho.

<span id="an_5:12">5:12</span> Ngokuba wena uyalisikelela ilungisa,
Yehova, Ulihlanganisele ngenkoliseko njengekhaka.

<span id="an_6:1">6:1</span> Kumongameli wokubethelwa izinto
ezineentambo: ngelamadoda ilizwi. Umhobe kaDavide. Yehova, musa
ukundohlwaya unomsindo, Ungandithethisi unobushushu.

<span id="an_6:2">6:2</span> Ndibabale, Yehova, ngokuba ndintshwenyile;
Ndiphilise, Yehova, ngokuba ekhwankqisiwe amathambo am.

<span id="an_6:3">6:3</span> Umphefumlo wam ukhwankqiswe kakhulu; Ke
wena, Yehova, koda kube nini na?

<span id="an_6:4">6:4</span> Buya, Yehova, uwuhlangule umphefumlo wam;
Ndisindise ngenxa yenceba yakho.

<span id="an_6:5">6:5</span> Ngokuba ekufeni akusekho kukukhumbula;
Kwelabafileyo ngubani na osenokubulela kuwe?

<span id="an_6:6">6:6</span> Ndidiniwe kukugcuma kwam; Ndiludadisa
ubusuku bonke ukhuko lwam, Ndiwenza manzi umandlalo wam ngeenyembezi
zam.

<span id="an_6:7">6:7</span> Lonakele kukukhathazeka iliso lam;
Laluphele ngenxa yababandezeli bam bonke.

<span id="an_6:8">6:8</span> Sukani kum, nina nonke basebenzi
bobutshinga; Ngokuba uYehova ulivile ilizwi lokulila kwam.

<span id="an_6:9">6:9</span> Ukuvile uYehova ukutarhuzisa kwam; UYehova
umthandazo wam uyawamkela.

<span id="an_6:10">6:10</span> Ziya kudana, zikhwankqe kakhulu, zonke
iintshaba zam; Ziya kubuyiswa zidanile ngephanyazo.

<span id="an_7:1">7:1</span> Ishigayon kaDavide, awayivumayo kuYehova
ngenxa yamazwi kaKushi, umBhenjamin. Yehova, Thixo wam, ndizimela ngawe;
Ndisindise kubo bonke abandisukelayo, undihlangule,

<span id="an_7:2">7:2</span> Hleze bawuqwenge njengengonyama umphefumlo
wam, Bawudlavule, kungekho mhlanguli.

<span id="an_7:3">7:3</span> Yehova, Thixo wam, ukuba ndithe ndenza oku,
Ukuba kukho ubugqwetha ezandleni zam,

<span id="an_7:4">7:4</span> Ukuba ndimphethe kakubi obexolelene nam,
Ndambhunyula ondibandezele kungekho sizathu:

<span id="an_7:5">7:5</span> Maluwusukele utshaba umphefumlo wam,
luwufumane, Lubunyashele phantsi ubomi bam, Uzuko lwam lululalise
eluthulini. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_7:6">7:6</span> Khawusuk’ ume, Yehova, unomsindo,
Kuphakamele ukuphuphuma komsindo wabandibandezelayo; Uvuke,
undikhawulele; wena umise umgwebo.

<span id="an_7:7">7:7</span> Ibandla lezizwe malikungqonge; Ubuyele
phezulu phezu kwalo.

<span id="an_7:8">7:8</span> UYehova uya kugweba phakathi kwezizwe.
Lithethe ityala lam, Yehova, ngobulungisa bam, nangokugqibelela kwam
okukum.

<span id="an_7:9">7:9</span> Mabuphele ububi babangendawo, ulizimase
ilungisa; Ungumcikidi weentliziyo nezintso, Thixo wobulungisa.

<span id="an_7:10">7:10</span> Ingweletshetshe yam inoThixo, Umsindisi
wabantliziyo zithe tye.

<span id="an_7:11">7:11</span> UThixo ngumgwebi olilungisa; UnguThixo
obhavuma yonke imihla.

<span id="an_7:12">7:12</span> Ukuba ongendawo uthe akabuya, ulilolile
ikrele lakhe; Usityedile isaphetha sakhe, wasilungisa.

<span id="an_7:13">7:13</span> Uzibhekise kuye izixhobo zokufa, Uzenze
zanomlilo iintolo zakhe.

<span id="an_7:14">7:14</span> Yabona, yena unenimba yobutshinga;
Ukhawule ububi, wazala ubuxoki;

<span id="an_7:15">7:15</span> Umbe umhadi, wawugomba; Weyela esihogweni
awasisebenzayo.

<span id="an_7:16">7:16</span> Ububi bakhe bobuyela entlokweni yakhe,
Naselukakayini lwakhe kufike ukugonyamela kwakhe.

<span id="an_7:17">7:17</span> Ndiya kubulela kuYehova ngokobulungisa
bakhe, Ndivume ngendumiso kwigama likaYehova ophezu konke.

<span id="an_8:1">8:1</span> Kumongameli: ngolwaseGati. Umhobe kaDavide.
Yehova, Nkosi yethu, Hayi, ubungangamsha begama lakho ehlabathini lonke!
Wena uwambathise amazulu ngendili yakho.

<span id="an_8:2">8:2</span> Emlonyeni wabantwana nabanyayo useke
amandla, Ngenxa yababandezeli bakho, Ukuze udambise utshaba
nophindezelayo.

<span id="an_8:3">8:3</span> Xa ndilikhangelayo izulu lakho, umsebenzi
weminwe yakho, Inyanga neenkwenkwezi ozimisileyo:

<span id="an_8:4">8:4</span> Uyintoni na umntu lo, le nto
umkhumbulelayo? Unyana womntu, le nto umvelelayo?

<span id="an_8:5">8:5</span> Umsilelise kancinane ebuThixweni, Wamthi
jize ngobuqaqawuli nangobungangamela.

<span id="an_8:6">8:6</span> Umphathise ubukhosi phezu kwemisebenzi
yezandla zakho, Zonke izinto uzibeke phantsi kweenyawo zakhe:

<span id="an_8:7">8:7</span> Impahla emfutshane, neenkomo zonke
ziphelele, Kwaneenyamakazi zonke;

<span id="an_8:8">8:8</span> Iintaka zezulu, neentlanzi zolwandle, Into
ehamba ngeendlela zolwandle.

<span id="an_8:9">8:9</span> Yehova, Nkosi yethu, Hayi, ubungangamsha
begama lakho ehlabathini lonke!

<span id="an_9:1">9:1</span> Kumongameli: ngemute-labhen, Umhobe
kaDavide. Ndiya kubulela kuYehova ngentliziyo yam yonke; Ndiya
kuyibalisa yonke imisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo.

<span id="an_9:2">9:2</span> Ndiya kuvuya ndidlamke ngawe; Ndiya
kulibethela uhadi igama lakho, Wena usenyangweni.

<span id="an_9:3">9:3</span> Ekubuyeni kweentshaba zam umva, Ziyawa,
zibhubhe ebusweni bakho.

<span id="an_9:4">9:4</span> Ngokuba ulifezile ityala lam nebango lam:
Uhleli etroneni ungumgwebi olilungisa.

<span id="an_9:5">9:5</span> Uzikhalimele iintlanga, wabatshabalalisa
abangendawo; Igama lazo ulicimile ngonaphakade kanaphakade.

<span id="an_9:6">9:6</span> Iintshaba zona zigqibele, yangamanxuwa
kwaphela; Imizi uyinyothule, Yadaka inkumbulo yayo yona.

<span id="an_9:7">9:7</span> Ke yena uYehova uhleli ngonaphakade,
Uyizinzisele ugwebo itrone yakhe.

<span id="an_9:8">9:8</span> Uya kugweba yena kwelimiweyo ngobulungisa,
Agwebe phakathi kwezizwe ngokuthe tye.

<span id="an_9:9">9:9</span> UYehova makabe yingxonde kotyunyuziweyo,
Ingxonde ngamaxesha engxingongo;

<span id="an_9:10">9:10</span> Bakholose ngawe abalaziyo igama lakho;
Ngokuba akubashiyanga abakuquqelayo wena, Yehova.

<span id="an_9:11">9:11</span> Vumani ngendumiso kuYehova ohlala eZiyon;
Xelani ezizweni izenzo zakhe ezincamisileyo;

<span id="an_9:12">9:12</span> Ukuba umphindezeli wamagazi ubakhumbule,
Akakulibalanga ukukhala kwabalulamileyo.

<span id="an_9:13">9:13</span> Ndibabale, Yehova; Zibone iintsizi zam
ezikhoyo ngabandithiyayo, Mphakamisi wam emasangweni okufa;

<span id="an_9:14">9:14</span> Ukuze ndibalise yonke indumiso yakho,
Emasangweni entombi uZiyon, Ndigcobe ngosindiso lwakho.

<span id="an_9:15">9:15</span> Iintlanga zitshone esihogweni ezasenzayo,
Emnatheni ezawugqumelayo kubanjiswe kwaolwazo unyawo.

<span id="an_9:16">9:16</span> Uzazisile uYehova; wenza umgwebo,
Emthiyela ngomsebenzi wezandla zakhe ongendawo. (Bethani uhadi ngofefe.
Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_9:17">9:17</span> Baya kubuyela kwelabafileyo abangendawo,
Kwaiintlanga zonke ezimlibalayo uThixo;

<span id="an_9:18">9:18</span> Ngokuba aliyi kuhlala lilityalwa
ihlwempu, Ithemba leentsizana aliyi kudaka ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_9:19">9:19</span> Khawusuk’ ume, Yehova; malungangcwangushi
uluntu, Mazigwetywe iintlanga phambi kwakho,

<span id="an_9:20">9:20</span> Zimisele ukoyika, Yehova, Zazi iintlanga
ukuba ziluluntu kuphela. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_10:1">10:1</span> Yini na ukuba umele mgama, Yehova,
Uzifihle ngamaxesha engxingongo?

<span id="an_10:2">10:2</span> Ngokukratsha kwabangendawo bayatsha
abaziintsizana; Babanjiswa ngamayelenqe abawacingileyo.

<span id="an_10:3">10:3</span> Ngokuba ongendawo uyaqhayisa ngeminqweno
yomphefumlo wakhe. Nolibawa wahlukene noYehova, wamgiba.

<span id="an_10:4">10:4</span> Ongendawo ngobuchi bakhe uthi, Akasayi
kubuza. Yonke iminkqangiyelo yakhe ithi, Akukho Thixo.

<span id="an_10:5">10:5</span> Ziqinile iindlela zakhe ngamaxesha onke;
Ziphakamile izigwebo zakho, zikude kuye; Bonke ababandezeli bakhe
uyabafuthela.

<span id="an_10:6">10:6</span> Uthi entliziyweni yakhe, Andisayi
kushukunyiswa; Izizukulwana ngezizukulwana, ndingongayi kuba sebubini.

<span id="an_10:7">10:7</span> Umlomo wakhe uzele kukushwabula
nokukhohlisa nokuxinezela. Ngaphantsi kolwimi lwakhe bububi nobutshinga.

<span id="an_10:8">10:8</span> Uhlala emilaleleni yeengqili, Agwinte
omsulwa entsithelweni; Amehlo akhe azonda oludwayi.

<span id="an_10:9">10:9</span> Ulalela entsithelweni njengengonyama
eludadeni wayo; Ulalela ukuba axwile emke nosizana; Uxwila emke
nolusizana, elutsala ngomnatha wakhe.

<span id="an_10:10">10:10</span> Uyabuthuma, uyabunguzela, Bawele
ezinzitsheni zakhe abaziindwayi.

<span id="an_10:11">10:11</span> Uthi entliziyweni yakhe, UThixo
ulibele, Ubusithelisile ubuso bakhe, akabonanga nento.

<span id="an_10:12">10:12</span> Khawusuk’ ume, Yehova, phakamisa
isandla sakho, Thixo. Musa ukubalibala abalulamileyo.

<span id="an_10:13">10:13</span> Kungenxa yani na ukuba ongendawo amgibe
uThixo, Athi entliziyweni yakhe, Akuyi kubuza?

<span id="an_10:14">10:14</span> Ubonile wena; ngokuba uyabubona ububi
nenkathazo, ububeke esandleni sakho; Uzinikela kuwe oludwayi; Ungumncedi
weenkedama wena.

<span id="an_10:15">10:15</span> Yaphula ingalo yongendawo; Onobubi,
mbuze okungendawo kwakhe, kungasali nento.

<span id="an_10:16">10:16</span> UYehova nguKumkani ngonaphakade
kanaphakade; Zitshabalele iintlanga, azabakho ehlabathini lakhe.

<span id="an_10:17">10:17</span> Umnqweno wabalulamileyo uwuvile,
Yehova; Wazizimasa iintliziyo zabo, wayibaza indlebe yakho,

<span id="an_10:18">10:18</span> Ukuba ugwebe ityala lenkedama
noxinzelelweyo, Angabi sabangcangcazelisa umntu wasehlabathini.

<span id="an_11:1">11:1</span> Kumongameli. EkaDavide. Ndizimela
ngoYehova; Ningathini na ukuthi kumphefumlo wam, Balekela entabeni yakho
njengentaka?

<span id="an_11:2">11:2</span> Ngokuba nabo abangendawo begoba
isaphetha, Bezilungisile iintolo zabo entanjeni, Ukuba batole besithele
kwabantliziyo zithe tye.

<span id="an_11:3">11:3</span> Xa iziseko zithe zagungxulwa, Ilungisa
linokuthini na?

<span id="an_11:4">11:4</span> UYehova, ulotempile yakhe iyingcwele,
UYehova, ulotrone yakhe isemazulwini, Amehlo akhe ayababona, iinkophe
zakhe ziyabacikida oonyana babantu.

<span id="an_11:5">11:5</span> UYehova uyalicikida ilungisa; Ke yena
ongendawo nothanda ukugonyamela, umthiyile umphefumlo wakhe.

<span id="an_11:6">11:6</span> Uya kubanisela abangendawo imigibe;
Umlilo, nesulfure, nomoya olulophu, yindebe yabo abayabelweyo;

<span id="an_11:7">11:7</span> Ngokuba lilungisa uYehova; uthanda
imisebenzi yobulungisa; Othe tye uya kububona ubuso bakhe.

<span id="an_12:1">12:1</span> Kumongameli: ngelamadoda ilizwi. Umhobe
kaDavide. Sindisa, Yehova, ngokuba uphelile owenceba, Ngokuba bathe
shwaka abanyanisileyo koonyana babantu.

<span id="an_12:2">12:2</span> Bathetha inkohlakalo omnye nomnye;
Bathetha ngomlomo ogudileyo, nangentliziyo embaxa.

<span id="an_12:3">12:3</span> Ngamana uYehova angayinqumla yonke
imilebe yomlomo ogudileyo, Ulwimi oluthetha izinto ezinkulu;

<span id="an_12:4">12:4</span> Abathe, Ulwimi lwethu siyalupheza;
Imilomo yethu yeyethu; ngubani na oyinkosi kuthi?

<span id="an_12:5">12:5</span> Ngenxa yokubhuqwa kweentsizana, ngenxa
yokuncwina kwamahlwempu, Ndiya kusuka ndime ngoku, utsho uYehova; Ndiya
kumbeka elusindisweni lowo ululangazelelayo.

<span id="an_12:6">12:6</span> Amazwi kaYehova ngamazwi acocekileyo,
Yisilivere enyibilikiselwe eziko, yela emhlabeni, Ehluzwe kasixhenxe.

<span id="an_12:7">12:7</span> Wena, Yehova, uya kubagcina, Uya
kubalondoloza kwesi sizukulwana ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_12:8">12:8</span> Abangendawo bahambahamba ngeenxa zonke,
Xa kuphakanyiswe abangeni phakathi koonyana babantu.

<span id="an_13:1">13:1</span> Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide. Kunini na,
Yehova, undilibele kwaphela? Kunini na ubusithelisa ubuso bakho kum?

<span id="an_13:2">13:2</span> Kunini na ndicebacebisana nomphefumlo
wam, Ndinesingqala entliziyweni yam imini le? Kunini na lundiphakamele
utshaba lwam?

<span id="an_13:3">13:3</span> Bheka undiphendule, Yehova, Thixo wam;
Khanyisa amehlo am, hleze ndilale ukufa;

<span id="an_13:4">13:4</span> Hleze utshaba lwam luthi, Ndimeyisile;
Bagcobe abandibandezelayo, xa ndithe ndashukunyiswa.

<span id="an_13:5">13:5</span> Mna ndikholose ngenceba yakho, Mayigcobe
intliziyo yam ngosindiso lwakho.

<span id="an_13:6">13:6</span> Ndiya kuvuma kuYehova, Ngokuba endiphethe
kakuhle.

<span id="an_14:1">14:1</span> Kumongameli. EkaDavide. Sithi isidenge
entliziyweni yaso, Akukho Thixo. Bonakalisile, balisikizi ngeentlondi
zabo; Akukho wenza okulungileyo.

<span id="an_14:2">14:2</span> UYehova esemazulwini uqondele koonyana
babantu, Ukubona ukuba ukho na oqiqayo, Oquqela kuThixo.

<span id="an_14:3">14:3</span> Bonke batyekile, bayimbozisa bephelele;
Akukho wenza okulungileyo, Akukho nokuba abe mnye.

<span id="an_14:4">14:4</span> Abanakwazi na bonke abasebenzi
bobutshinga, Abathi, bebadla abantu bam, bathi badla isonka, Bangamnquli
uYehova?

<span id="an_14:5">14:5</span> Apho bankwantya benkwantyile; Ngokuba
uThixo usesizukulwaneni samalungisa.

<span id="an_14:6">14:6</span> Icebo losizana ningalidanisa, Kodwa
uYehova ulihlathi lalo.

<span id="an_14:7">14:7</span> Akwaba bekuvela eZiyon ukusindiswa
kwamaSirayeli! Ekubabuyiseni kukaYehova abantu bakhe ekuthinjweni,
Wogcoba uYakobi, avuye uSirayeli.

<span id="an_15:1">15:1</span> Umhobe kaDavide. Yehova, ngubani na
owophambukela ententeni yakho? Ngubani na owohlala entabeni yakho
engcwele?

<span id="an_15:2">15:2</span> Ngohamba ngokugqibeleleyo, esenza
ubulungisa, Othetha inyaniso ngentliziyo yakhe.

<span id="an_15:3">15:3</span> Ngongahlebiyo ngolwimi lwakhe,
Ongamenziyo into embi uwabo, Ongamngcikiviyo ummelwane wakhe;

<span id="an_15:4">15:4</span> Odelekileyo, ecekiseka, kwawakhe amehlo,
Obazukisayo ke bona abamoyikayo uYehova; Ofunga, angajiki, nokuba kubi
kuye,

<span id="an_15:5">15:5</span> Ongayinikeliyo imali yakhe ukuba adle
abantu ngayo, Ongenakugaqelwa ngaye omsulwa. Okwenzayo oko akayi kuza
ashukunyiswe naphakade.

<span id="an_16:1">16:1</span> Eyona iligugu likaDavide. Ndigcine,
Thixo, ngokuba ndizimela ngawe.

<span id="an_16:2">16:2</span> Ndithe kuYehova, UyiNkosi yam, Andinanto
indilungeleyo ngaphezu kwakho.

<span id="an_16:3">16:3</span> Ndithe kwabangcwele abasehlabathini, Bona
bazizinhanha apho, kukhona konke endikunanzileyo.

<span id="an_16:4">16:4</span> Ziya kwanda iimbulaleko zabo bamananisa
ngathixo wumbi uYehova. Andiyi kuyithulula iminikelo yabo ethululwayo
yegazi; Andiyi kuwaphatha amagama abo ngomlomo wam.

<span id="an_16:5">16:5</span> NguYehova isahlulo endasabelwayo, nendebe
endayabelwayo; Ulenze banzi ilifa lam.

<span id="an_16:6">16:6</span> Amacandelo andiwele ezindaweni ezimnandi;
Hee! Ndide ndaba nelifa elihle.

<span id="an_16:7">16:7</span> Ndiya kumbonga uYehova ondinike icebo;
Nasebusuku ziyandithethisa izintso zam.

<span id="an_16:8">16:8</span> Ndimmisile uYehova phambi kwam amaxesha
onke; Ngokuba esekunene kum nje, andiyi kushukunyiswa.

<span id="an_16:9">16:9</span> Ngako oko iyavuya intliziyo yam,
luyagcoba uzuko lwam: Nenyama yam iya kuhlala ikholosile.

<span id="an_16:10">16:10</span> Ngokuba akuyi kuwushiya umphefumlo wam
kwelabafileyo; Akuyi kumyekela owakho wenceba ukuba abonane nesihogo.

<span id="an_16:11">16:11</span> Uya kundazisa umendo wobomi; Ebusweni
bakho yinzaliseko yemivuyo; Ekunene kwakho yimihlali ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_17:1">17:1</span> Umthandazo kaDavide. Buve, Yehova,
ubulungisa; kubazele indlebe ukuhlahlamba kwam; Wubekele indlebe
umthandazo wam, ongengamlomo ukhohlisayo.

<span id="an_17:2">17:2</span> Ibango lam malivele ebusweni bakho,
Amehlo akho akhangele ngokuthe tye.

<span id="an_17:3">17:3</span> Uyicikidile intliziyo yam; undivelele
ebusuku; Undinyibilikisile, akwafumana nto; Ndiyinkqangiyele into embi,
ayiyi kuwugqitha umlomo wam.

<span id="an_17:4">17:4</span> Malunga nemisebenzi yabantu, ngelizwi
lomlomo wakho, Mna ndizigcinile, andangena kwiindlela zamanyangaza.

<span id="an_17:5">17:5</span> Imikhondo yam ibambe iindlela zakho,
Azashukuma iinyawo zam.

<span id="an_17:6">17:6</span> Mna ndinqula wena, ngokuba undiphendula,
Thixo; Ndithobele indlebe yakho, kuve ukuthetha kwam.

<span id="an_17:7">17:7</span> Zibalule iinceba zakho, wena
wabasindisayo abazimela ngawe, Ngesandla sakho sokunene, ngenxa
yabasukela phezulu kubo.

<span id="an_17:8">17:8</span> Ndigcine njengeliso, njengokhozo lwalo,
Ndisithelise ngesithunzi samaphiko akho,

<span id="an_17:9">17:9</span> Phambi kwabangendawo abandibhuqayo,
Phambi kweentshaba zam ngokwasemphefumlweni ezindingungelayo.

<span id="an_17:10">17:10</span> Zithe fithi kukutyeba; Ngomlomo wazo
zithetha ngekratshi.

<span id="an_17:11">17:11</span> Zindijikelezile ngoku ekuhambeni kwam;
Amehlo azo ziwamisele ukundinqumela emhlabeni.

<span id="an_17:12">17:12</span> Ukufana kwazo kunjengengonyama
engxamele ukuqwenga, Kunjengengonyama entsha ihleli entsithelweni.

<span id="an_17:13">17:13</span> Khawusuk’ ume, Yehova, Uyihlangabeze,
uyiwise yona; Wusindise umphefumlo wam kongendawo ngekrele lakho;

<span id="an_17:14">17:14</span> Kubafo, ngesandla sakho, Yehova, Kubafo
beli phakade, abasahlulo sikobu bomi; Osizalisileyo isisu sabo
ngeengqwebo zakho; Bakholisile ngoonyana, Ukuphuphuma kwabo bakushiya
neentsapho zabo.

<span id="an_17:15">17:15</span> Mna ndiya kububona ubuso bakho
ndisebulungiseni; Ndiya kwaneliswa sisithomo sakho ekuvukeni kwam.

<span id="an_18:1">18:1</span> Kumongameli. Eyomkhonzi kaYehova.
EkaDavide, owawathethayo kuYehova amazwi ale ngoma, mhlenikweni uYehova
wamhlangulayo esandleni seentshaba zakhe zonke nasesandleni sikaSawule;
wathi: Ndikuthanda ngembilini yam, Yehova, lomelelo lwam.

<span id="an_18:2">18:2</span> Yehova, ngxondorha yam, mboniselo yam,
msindisi wam, Thixo wam, liwa lam endizimela ngalo, Ngweletshetshe yam,
luphondo losindiso lwam, ngxonde yam!

<span id="an_18:3">18:3</span> Ndinqula uYehova ongowokudunyiswa,
Ndiyasindiswa ezintshabeni zam.

<span id="an_18:4">18:4</span> Izintya zokufa zandijikela; Imilambo
yobutshijolo yandidandathekisa.

<span id="an_18:5">18:5</span> Izintya zelabafileyo zandibhijela;
Izirhintyelo zokufa zabetha kum.

<span id="an_18:6">18:6</span> Ekubandezelekeni kwam ndanqula uYehova,
Ndazibika kuThixo wam; Waliva etempileni yakhe izwi lam, Ukuzibika kwam
kwafika phambi kwakhe ezindlebeni zakhe.

<span id="an_18:7">18:7</span> Lahexa ke lanyikima ihlabathi, Iziseko
zeentaba zagungqa, Zahexa, ngokuba enomsindo.

<span id="an_18:8">18:8</span> Kwathi thaphu umsi emathatheni akhe,
Wadla umlilo, uphuma emlonyeni wakhe, Kwavutha amalahle ephuma kuwo.

<span id="an_18:9">18:9</span> Wawathoba amazulu, wehla, Yangamafu
amnyama phantsi kweenyawo zakhe.

<span id="an_18:10">18:10</span> Wakhwela ekerubhini, waphaphazela, Wee
tshwebelele ngamaphiko omoya.

<span id="an_18:11">18:11</span> Wamisa ubumnyama baba lisithe lakhe,
umnquba wakhe ngeenxa zonke kuye; Ubumnyama bamanzi, iingqimba zamafu.

<span id="an_18:12">18:12</span> Ekukhanyeni okuphambi kwakhe,
kwatyhoboza emafini akhe Isiphango samatye, namalahle omlilo.

<span id="an_18:13">18:13</span> Wadudumisa ezulwini uYehova, Ophezu
konke walikhupha ilizwi lakhe. Yasisiphango samatye namalahle omlilo.

<span id="an_18:14">18:14</span> Wathuma iintolo zakhe,
wabaphangalalisa; Yamininzi imibane, wabadubaduba.

<span id="an_18:15">18:15</span> Imiphantsi yamanzi yabonakala,
Kwatyhileka iziseko zelimiweyo Ngokukhalima kwakho, Yehova, Ngokufutha
komoya womsindo wakho.

<span id="an_18:16">18:16</span> Wolula isandla ephezulu, wandibamba,
Wandirhola emanzini amaninzi.

<span id="an_18:17">18:17</span> Wandihlangula elutshabeni lwam
olunamandla, Kwabandithiyileyo, ngokuba bebomelele kunam.

<span id="an_18:18">18:18</span> Bandifikela ngemini yokusindeka kwam,
UYehova wandixhasa.

<span id="an_18:19">18:19</span> Wandikhuphela endaweni ebanzi,
Wandihlangula, ngokuba endithandile.

<span id="an_18:20">18:20</span> UYehova wandiphatha kakuhle
ngokobulungisa bam, Wandibuyisela ngokobunyulu bezandla zam.

<span id="an_18:21">18:21</span> Ngokuba ndizigcina iindlela zikaYehova,
Andemka ngokungendawo kuThixo wam.

<span id="an_18:22">18:22</span> Ngokuba onke amasiko akhe aphambi kwam,
Nemimiselo yakhe andiyisusi kum;

<span id="an_18:23">18:23</span> Ndaye ndingogqibeleleyo kuye,
Ndazigcina, andaba nabugwenxa,

<span id="an_18:24">18:24</span> Wandibuyisela ke uYehova ngokobulungisa
bam, Ngokobunyulu bezandla zam phambi kwamehlo akhe.

<span id="an_18:25">18:25</span> Kowenceba uzenza owenceba, Kwigorha
eligqibeleleyo uzenza ogqibeleleyo;

<span id="an_18:26">18:26</span> Kozenze nyulu uzenza onyulu,
Kojibilizayo uzenza onobuqhokolo.

<span id="an_18:27">18:27</span> Ngokuba wena uyabasindisa abantu
ababandezelekileyo, Uwathobe amehlo aqwayingileyo.

<span id="an_18:28">18:28</span> Ngokuba uyasilumeka isibane sam wena;
UYehova uThixo wam uyabukhanyisela ubumnyama bam.

<span id="an_18:29">18:29</span> Ngokuba ngawe ndigila amajarha,
NgoThixo wam ndiqabela ezindongeni.

<span id="an_18:30">18:30</span> UThixo yena, igqibelele indlela yakhe;
Ilizwi likaYehova linyibilikisiwe, Uyingweletshetshe kubo bonke
abazimela ngaye.

<span id="an_18:31">18:31</span> Ngokuba ngubani na onguThixo, ingenguye
uYehova? Ngubani na oliliwa, ingenguThixo wethu?

<span id="an_18:32">18:32</span> UloThixo undibhinqise ubukroti,
Uyigqibelelisileyo indlela yam;

<span id="an_18:33">18:33</span> Uzifanisayo iinyawo zam
nezamaxhamakazi, Undimisayo emimangweni yam:

<span id="an_18:34">18:34</span> Uzifundisayo ukulwa izandla zam,
Zityede isaphetha sobhedu iingalo zam.

<span id="an_18:35">18:35</span> Undinikileyo ingweletshetshe yosindiso
lwakho: Sandixhasa isandla sakho sokunene; Ululamo lwakho lwandikhulisa.

<span id="an_18:36">18:36</span> Wawenzela indawo ebanzi amanyathela am
phantsi kwam, Amaxhwele am akahexa.

<span id="an_18:37">18:37</span> Ndazisukela iintshaba zam, ndazifumana;
Andabuya zada zaphela.

<span id="an_18:38">18:38</span> Ndaziqoba; azaba nakuvuka, Zawa phantsi
kweenyawo zam.

<span id="an_18:39">18:39</span> Wandibhinqisa ubukroti ekulweni,
Wabaguqisa phantsi kwam abasukela phezulu kum;

<span id="an_18:40">18:40</span> Wandinika ikhosi leentshaba zam,
Abandithiyayo ndababhangisa.

<span id="an_18:41">18:41</span> Bazibika, akwabakho msindisi; Bazibika
kuYehova, akabaphendula.

<span id="an_18:42">18:42</span> Ndabacola, banjengothuli phambi komoya,
Ndabaphalaza njengodaka lwezitrato.

<span id="an_18:43">18:43</span> Wandisiza ekubambaneni kwabantu,
Wandimisa ndayintloko yeentlanga; Abantu ebe ndingabazi bandikhonza.

<span id="an_18:44">18:44</span> Besave ngeendlebe, bandithobela,
Oonyana bolunye uhlanga bahanahanisa kum;

<span id="an_18:45">18:45</span> Oonyana bolunye uhlanga bantshwenya,
Baphuma bengcangcazela ekuvingcelweni kwabo.

<span id="an_18:46">18:46</span> UYehova uhleli; lelokubongwa iliwa lam,
Aphakanyiswe uThixo ondisindisayo.

<span id="an_18:47">18:47</span> UloThixo wandinika impindezelo,
Uzikhandaniselayo izizwe phantsi kwam;

<span id="an_18:48">18:48</span> Undisiza ezintshabeni zam; Ewe, wena
undiphakamisayo kwabasukela phezulu kum, Undihlangule kumfo
ogonyamelayo.

<span id="an_18:49">18:49</span> Ngenxa yoko ndiya kubulela kuwe,
Yehova, phakathi kweentlanga, Ndivume kwigama lakho.

<span id="an_18:50">18:50</span> Ulokhulisa iintsindiso zokumkani wakhe:
Wenzayo inceba kumthanjiswa wakhe, KuDavide, nakwimbewu yakhe kude kuse
ephakadeni.

<span id="an_19:1">19:1</span> Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide. Izulu
libalisa uzuko lukaThixo, Saye isibhakabhaka sixela umsebenzi wezandla
zakhe.

<span id="an_19:2">19:2</span> Imini impompozelela imini intetho,
Ubusuku buxelela ubusuku ukwazi.

<span id="an_19:3">19:3</span> Akukho ntetho, akukho mazwi, Apho
singavakaliyo isandi sawo.

<span id="an_19:4">19:4</span> Intambo yawo yokulinganisa iphume yaya
ehlabathini lonke, Kwaba seziphelweni zelimiweyo ukukhuluma kwawo.
Ilanga ulimisele intente kuwo,

<span id="an_19:5">19:5</span> Lona linjengomyeni ke ephuma egumbini
lakhe; Linemihlali njengegorha, ukugidima ngomendo walo.

<span id="an_19:6">19:6</span> Kusesiphelweni sezulu ukuphuma kwalo,
Ukujikeleza kwalo kusa eziphelweni zalo; Akukho nto inokusithela
ebushushwini balo.

<span id="an_19:7">19:7</span> Umyalelo kaYehova ugqibelele, ubuyisa
umphefumlo; Isingqino sikaYehova sinyanisekile, sinika isiyatha
ubulumko.

<span id="an_19:8">19:8</span> Izimiselo zikaYehova zithe tye, zivuyisa
intliziyo; Umthetho kaYehova unyulu, ukhanyisela amehlo.

<span id="an_19:9">19:9</span> Ukoyika uYehova kucocekile, kumi
ngonaphakade; Izigwebo zikaYehova ziyinyaniso, zibubulungisa kwaphela.

<span id="an_19:10">19:10</span> Zinokunqweneleka kunegolide zona,
nakunengcwengiweyo eninzi; Zimnandi kunobusi, kunencindi yobusi.

<span id="an_19:11">19:11</span> Zikwamkhanyisela umkhonzi wakho;
Ekuzigcineni mkhulu umvuzo.

<span id="an_19:12">19:12</span> Ukulahleka, ngubani na okuqondayo?
Ndenze msulwa kokusitheleyo.

<span id="an_19:13">19:13</span> Kwanasekukhukhumaleni mnqande umkhonzi
wakho; Makungandilawuli; ukuze ndandule ukuba ngogqibeleleyo, Ndibe
msulwa ekukreqeni okukhulu.

<span id="an_19:14">19:14</span> Makakholeke amazwi omlomo wam,
nezicamango zentliziyo yam, Phambi kwakho, Yehova, liwa lam, mkhululi
wam.

<span id="an_20:1">20:1</span> Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide. Ngamana
wakuphendula uYehova ngemini yembandezelo, Ngamana lakusa engxondeni
igama likaThixo kaYakobi!

<span id="an_20:2">20:2</span> Wakuthumela uncedo lwasengcweleni,
Wakuxhasa eseZiyon!

<span id="an_20:3">20:3</span> Wayikhumbula yonke iminikelo yakho
yokudla, Wawafumana etyebile amadini akho anyukayo! (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_20:4">20:4</span> Wakunika ngokwentliziyo yakho, Walizalisa
lonke icebo lakho!

<span id="an_20:5">20:5</span> Singamemelela ngosindiso lwakho,
Siphakamise iibhanile zethu egameni loThixo wethu; Azizalise uYehova
zonke izicelo zakho.

<span id="an_20:6">20:6</span> Ndiyazi ngoku ukuba uYehova ngumsindisi
womthanjiswa wakhe; Uya kumphendula emazulwini akhe angcwele Ngobugorha
obusindisayo besandla sakhe sokunene.

<span id="an_20:7">20:7</span> Abanye bakhankanya iinqwelo zokulwa,
abanye bakhankanye amahashe, Ke thina sikhankanya igama likaYehova
uThixo wethu.

<span id="an_20:8">20:8</span> Bona baguqile bawa; Thina siphakamile
sema.

<span id="an_20:9">20:9</span> Yehova, sindisa; Ukumkani asiphendule
ngemini yokubiza kwethu.

<span id="an_21:1">21:1</span> Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide. Yehova,
uvuyile ngamandla akho ukumkani, Asikuko nokuba uyagcoba ngosindiso
lwakho!

<span id="an_21:2">21:2</span> Umnike umnqweno wentliziyo yakhe
Akwasilandula isicelo somlomo wakhe. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_21:3">21:3</span> Ngokuba umkhawulela ngeentsikelelo
zokulungileyo, Umthwesa isithsaba segolide engcwengekileyo.

<span id="an_21:4">21:4</span> Wacela ubomi kuwe, wampha, Wamnika imihla
emide ngonaphakade kanaphakade.

<span id="an_21:5">21:5</span> Lukhulu uzuko lwakhe ngosindiso lwakho;
Ubeka phezu kwakhe indili nobungangamela.

<span id="an_21:6">21:6</span> Ngokuba umenze waba yintsikelelo
ngonaphakade, Umvuyisa ngovuyo ebusweni bakho.

<span id="an_21:7">21:7</span> Ngokuba ukumkani ukholose ngoYehova,
Ngenceba yOsenyangweni akayi kushukunyiswa.

<span id="an_21:8">21:8</span> Isandla sakho siya kuzifumana zonke
iintshaba zakho, Esokunene sakho siya kubafumana abakuthiyayo.

<span id="an_21:9">21:9</span> Uya kubenza babe njengeziko lomlilo,
wakubonakala. UYehova uya kubaginya ngomsindo wakhe, Nomlilo ubadle.

<span id="an_21:10">21:10</span> Uya kusitshabalalisa isiqhamo sabo
emhlabeni, Imbewu yabo koonyana babantu.

<span id="an_21:11">21:11</span> Ngokuba bakuthobela ububi, Bacinga
iyelenqe; abayi kufeza nto.

<span id="an_21:12">21:12</span> Ngokuba uya kubenza bakunikele umhlana;
Ngesaphetha sakho uya kuxuna iintolo zakho ebusweni babo.

<span id="an_21:13">21:13</span> Phakama, Yehova, ngamandla akho; Siya
kuvuma sibethe uhadi ngobugorha bakho.

<span id="an_22:1">22:1</span> Kumongameli: ngeyelexhama lesifingo.
Umhobe kaDavide. Thixo wam, Thixo wam, undilahleleni na? Ukude ngani na
ekusindisweni kwam, nasemazwini okubonga kwam?

<span id="an_22:2">22:2</span> Thixo wam, ndiyabiza emini, ungaphenduli;
Nasebusuku ndiyabiza, andithozanyiswa noko.

<span id="an_22:3">22:3</span> Ungcwele ke wena, Ungulohlala
ezindumisweni zakwaSirayeli.

<span id="an_22:4">22:4</span> Oobawo bakholosa ngawe, Bakholosa,
wabasiza;

<span id="an_22:5">22:5</span> Bakhala kuwe, basinda; Bakholosa ngawe,
abadana.

<span id="an_22:6">22:6</span> Ke mna ndingumbungu, andimntu;
Ndisisingcikivo soluntu, into edelekileyo ebantwini.

<span id="an_22:7">22:7</span> Bonke abandibonayo bayandigculela;
Bayasineka, bahlunguzela intloko;

<span id="an_22:8">22:8</span> Bathi, Makazilahlele kuYehova, amsize,
Amhlangule kaloku, ngokuba emthandile.

<span id="an_22:9">22:9</span> Ewe, nguwe umtyhobozisi wam esizalweni,
Inkolosisi yam ndisemabeleni kama.

<span id="an_22:10">22:10</span> Ndalahlelwa kuwe kwasesizalweni;
Kwasembilinini kama ubunguThixo wam.

<span id="an_22:11">22:11</span> Musa ukuba kude nam, ngokuba isondele
imbandezelo, Ngokuba akukho mncedi.

<span id="an_22:12">22:12</span> Ndingqongwe ziinkunzi ezininzi,
Ndihlanganyelwe zeziziimbalasane zaseBhashan.

<span id="an_22:13">22:13</span> Zindakhamele umlomo wazo,
Njengengonyama eqwengayo, egqumayo.

<span id="an_22:14">22:14</span> Ndiphalele njengamanzi, Ahlukene onke
amathambo am; Yanjengomthwebeba intliziyo yam, Inyibilikile phakathi
kwezibilini zam.

<span id="an_22:15">22:15</span> Omile njengegophe amandla am, Ulwimi
lwam lunamathele ekhuhlangubeni lam; Undibeka eluthulini lokufa.

<span id="an_22:16">22:16</span> Ngokuba izinja zindirhawule, Ibandla
labenzi bokubi lindingungele; Bagqobhoza izandla zam neenyawo zam.

<span id="an_22:17">22:17</span> Ndinokuwabala onke amathambo am; Bona
bayandijonga, bayandibonela,

<span id="an_22:18">22:18</span> Babelana ngeengubo zam, Isambatho sam
basenzela amaqashiso.

<span id="an_22:19">22:19</span> Ke wena, Yehova, musa ukuba kude;
Mandla am, khawuleza undincede.

<span id="an_22:20">22:20</span> Wuhlangule ekreleni umphefumlo wam,
Okuphela kwawo, ethupheni lenja.

<span id="an_22:21">22:21</span> Ndisindise emlonyeni wengonyama,
Nasezimpondweni zenqu uya kundiphendula.

<span id="an_22:22">22:22</span> Ndiya kulazisa igama lakho kubazalwana
bam, Ndikudumise phakathi kwebandla, ndithi,

<span id="an_22:23">22:23</span> Nina nimoyikayo uYehova, mdumiseni;
Nonke, mbewu kaYakobi, mzukiseni, Nimhlonele nina, mbewu yonke
kaSirayeli.

<span id="an_22:24">22:24</span> Kuba azidelekanga, azibanga nazothe
kuye iintsizi zolusizana; Akabusithelisanga ubuso bakhe kuye;
Ekuzibikeni kwakhe kuye waphulaphula.

<span id="an_22:25">22:25</span> Ivela kuwe indumiso yam ebandleni
elikhulu; Nezibhambathiso zam ndiya kuzizalisa phambi kwabamoyikayo.

<span id="an_22:26">22:26</span> Baya kudla abalulamileyo, bahluthe;
Baya kudumisa uYehova abamngxamelayo. Ngamana yaphila intliziyo yenu
ngonaphakade!

<span id="an_22:27">22:27</span> Ziya kukhumbula zibuyele kuYehova zonke
iziphelo zehlabathi, Iqubude phambi kwakhe yonke imizalwane yeentlanga:

<span id="an_22:28">22:28</span> Ngokuba bobukaYehova ubukumkani, Nguye
umlawuli ezintlangeni.

<span id="an_22:29">22:29</span> Baya kudla, baqubude, bonke
abatyebileyo behlabathi; Baya kuguqa phambi kwakhe bonke abatshona
eluthulini, Abangawugciniyo umphefumlo wabo.

<span id="an_22:30">22:30</span> Imbewu iya kumkhonza; Kuya kubaliselwa
isizukulwana ngayo iNkosi.

<span id="an_22:31">22:31</span> Baya kuza baxele ubulungisa bayo
Kubantu abaza kuzalwa, ukuba oko ukwenzile.

<span id="an_23:1">23:1</span> Umhobe kaDavide. UYehova ngumalusi wam,
andisweli lutho.

<span id="an_23:2">23:2</span> Wenza ukuba mandibuthe emakriweni
aluhlaza; Undithundezela emanzini angawokuphumla.

<span id="an_23:3">23:3</span> Uyawubuyisa umphefumlo wam; Undikhaphela
ezindleleni zobulungisa ngenxa yegama lakhe.

<span id="an_23:4">23:4</span> Nokuba ndihamba emfuleni wethunzi lokufa,
Andiyi koyika bubi, ngokuba unam wena; Intonga yakho, umsimelelo wakho,
uyandithuthuzela.

<span id="an_23:5">23:5</span> Undilungisela isithebe phambi
kwababandezeli bam, Uyithambisa ngeoli intloko yam, Indebe yam
iyaphalala.

<span id="an_23:6">23:6</span> Inene, ndiya kulandelwa kokulungileyo
nenceba Yonke imihla yobomi bam, Ndihlale endlwini kaYehova Imihla
emide.

<span id="an_24:1">24:1</span> Umhobe kaDavide. LelikaYehova ihlabathi
nenzaliseko yalo, Elimiweyo, nabahleli kulo;

<span id="an_24:2">24:2</span> Ngokuba yena waliseka phezu kweelwandle,
Walizinzisa phezu kwemilambo.

<span id="an_24:3">24:3</span> Ngubani na onokunyuka aye entabeni
kaYehova? Ngubani na onokuma endaweni yakhe engcwele?

<span id="an_24:4">24:4</span> Ngozandla zimsulwa, ontliziyo inyulu,
Ongawuphakamiseli kwinkohlakalo umphefumlo wakhe, Ongafungiyo
ngenkohliso.

<span id="an_24:5">24:5</span> Uya kwamkela intsikelelo kuYehova,
Nobulungisa kuThixo ongumsindisi wakhe.

<span id="an_24:6">24:6</span> Siso eso isizukulwana sabamngxameleyo,
Sababufunayo ubuso bakho, Thixo kaYakobi.(phakamisani.)

<span id="an_24:7">24:7</span> Phakamisani iintloko zenu, masango;
Niziphakamise, minyango yaphakade, Angene uKumkani wozuko.

<span id="an_24:8">24:8</span> Ngubani na ke lo Kumkani wozuko?
NguYehova onamandla, oligorha; NguYehova, igorha emfazweni.

<span id="an_24:9">24:9</span> Phakamisani iintloko zenu, masango,
Niziphakamise, minyango yaphakade, Angene lo Kumkani wozuko.

<span id="an_24:10">24:10</span> Ngubani na ke yena uKumkani wozuko?
NguYehova wemikhosi, Nguye lo Kumkani wozuko. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_25:1">25:1</span> EkaDavide. Ndiwuphakamisela kuwe, Yehova,
umphefumlo wam.

<span id="an_25:2">25:2</span> Thixo wam, ndikholose ngawe,
Mandingadani; Mazingandivuyeleli iintshaba zam.

<span id="an_25:3">25:3</span> Ewe, bonke abo bakuthembayo abayi kudana;
Kuya kudana abo banginiza ngelize.

<span id="an_25:4">25:4</span> Ndazise iindlela zakho, Yehova,
Ndifundise umendo wakho.

<span id="an_25:5">25:5</span> Ndinyathelise enyanisweni yakho,
undifundise; Ngokuba unguThixo ongumsindisi wam; Ndithembe wena yonke
imihla.

<span id="an_25:6">25:6</span> Khumbula iimfesane zakho, Yehova,
neenceba zakho; Ngokuba kususela kwaphakade zikho.

<span id="an_25:7">25:7</span> Musa ukuzikhumbula izono zobutsha bam,
nokreqo lwam; Ndikhumbule ngokwenceba yakho wena, Ngenxa yokulunga
kwakho, Yehova.

<span id="an_25:8">25:8</span> Ulungile, uthe tye uYehova; Ngenxa yoko
uyabayalela indlela aboni.

<span id="an_25:9">25:9</span> Uyabanyathelisa abalulamileyo emasikweni
akhe, Abafundise abalulamileyo indlela yakhe.

<span id="an_25:10">25:10</span> Zonke iindlela zikaYehova ziyinceba
nenyaniso, Kwabagcina umnqophiso wakhe nezingqino zakhe.

<span id="an_25:11">25:11</span> Ngenxa yegama lakho, Yehova, xolela
ubugwenxa bam, Ngokuba bukhulu bona.

<span id="an_25:12">25:12</span> Ngubani na ke umntu omoyikayo uYehova?
Womyalela indlela aya kuyinyula.

<span id="an_25:13">25:13</span> Umphefumlo wakhe wohlala wonwabile,
Imbewu yakhe ilidle ilifa ilizwe.

<span id="an_25:14">25:14</span> Ukucweya kukaYehova kunabamoyikayo;
Ubazisa umnqophiso wakhe.

<span id="an_25:15">25:15</span> Amehlo am ahlala emi kuYehova, Ngokuba
nguye ozirholayo eluthanjeni iinyawo zam.

<span id="an_25:16">25:16</span> Ndibheke, undibabale, Ngokuba
ndindodwa, ndibandezelekile.

<span id="an_25:17">25:17</span> Iimbandezelo zentliziyo yam
ziphangalalisiwe; Ndikhuphe ekucuthekeni kwam.

<span id="an_25:18">25:18</span> Khangela ukucinezeleka kwam nokwaphuka
kwam, Uxolele zonke izono zam.

<span id="an_25:19">25:19</span> Zikhangele iintshaba zam, ngokuba
zininzi; Zindithiye ngentiyo egonyamelayo.

<span id="an_25:20">25:20</span> Wugcine umphefumlo wam, undihlangule;
Mandingadani, ngokuba ndizimela ngawe.

<span id="an_25:21">25:21</span> Ukugqibelela nokuthi tye
makundilondoloze, Ngokuba ndithembele kuwe.

<span id="an_25:22">25:22</span> Khulula uSirayeli, Thixo,
Ezimbandezelweni zakhe zonke.

<span id="an_26:1">26:1</span> EkaDavide. Lithethe ityala lam, Yehova,
ngokuba mna ndihambe engqibelelweni yam, Ndakholosa ngoYehova, andahexa.

<span id="an_26:2">26:2</span> Ndicikide, Yehova, undilinge; Nyibilikisa
izintso zam nentliziyo yam.

<span id="an_26:3">26:3</span> Ngokuba inceba yakho iphambi kwamehlo am,
Ndihamba enyanisweni yakho.

<span id="an_26:4">26:4</span> Andihlali namadoda akhohlakeleyo,
Andihambi nabanyhwalazi.

<span id="an_26:5">26:5</span> Ndilithiyile ibandla labenzi bobubi,
Andihlali nabangendawo.

<span id="an_26:6">26:6</span> Ndizihlamba kokumsulwa izandla zam,
Ndisiphahle isibingelelo sakho, Yehova,

<span id="an_26:7">26:7</span> Ukuba ndivakalise izwi lokubulela,
Ndibalise ngayo yonke imisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo.

<span id="an_26:8">26:8</span> Yehova, ndiyalithanda ikhaya eliyindlu
yakho, Nendawo yokuhlala kozuko lwakho.

<span id="an_26:9">26:9</span> Musa ukuwubuthela umphefumlo wam ndawonye
naboni, Ubomi bam ndawonye namadoda anamagazi;

<span id="an_26:10">26:10</span> Wona azandla zinamanyala, Wona
ezokunene zawo zizeleyo zizicengo.

<span id="an_26:11">26:11</span> Mna ke okwam ndihamba engqibelelweni
yam; Ndikhulule, undibabale.

<span id="an_26:12">26:12</span> Unyawo lwam lumi endaweni ebanzi;
Ndimbonga uYehova ndisemabandleni.

<span id="an_27:1">27:1</span> EkaDavide. NguYehova umkhanyiseli wam
nomsindisi wam, ndiya koyika bani na? NguYehova inqaba yobomi bam, ndiya
kunkwantya ngabani na?

<span id="an_27:2">27:2</span> Bakusondela kum abenzi bobubi ukuba badle
inyama yam, Bakuza ababandezeli bam neentshaba zam kum, bakhubeka bawa
bona.

<span id="an_27:3">27:3</span> Bendingafanelana ndirhawulwe ngumkhosi
isuka ingoyiki intliziyo yam; Bendingafanelana ndiphakanyelwe yimfazwe,
ndisuka ndithembe noko.

<span id="an_27:4">27:4</span> Ndicele nto-nye kuYehova, ndifuna yona:
Ukuba ndihlale endlwini kaYehova yonke imihla yobomi bam, Ndibone ubuhle
bukaYehova, ndiphicothe etempileni yakhe.

<span id="an_27:5">27:5</span> Ngokuba undigusha emnqubeni wakhe ngemini
yobubi, Undisithelisa esitheni lentente yakhe, Undimisa eweni.

<span id="an_27:6">27:6</span> Ngoku ke iya kuphakama intloko yam phezu
kweentshaba zam ezindijikelezayo, Ndibingelele ententeni yakhe
imibingelelo yokuduma, Ndivume, ndibethe uhadi kuYehova.

<span id="an_27:7">27:7</span> Yiva, Yehova, ndakubiza ngezwi lam;
Ndibabale, undiphendule.

<span id="an_27:8">27:8</span> Intliziyo yam ithi kuwe, kweli uthi,
Funani ubuso bam, Ubuso bakho, Yehova, ndiya kubufuna.

<span id="an_27:9">27:9</span> Musa ukubusithelisa ubuso bakho kum; Musa
ukumgila umkhonzi wakho ngomsindo; Uluncedo lwam, musa ukundilahla; Musa
ukundishiya, Thixo ondisindisayo.

<span id="an_27:10">27:10</span> Ngokuba ubawo noma bandishiyile, Wesuka
uYehova wandichola.

<span id="an_27:11">27:11</span> Ndiyalele, Yehova, indlela yakho,
Ndikhaphe emendweni othe tye, ngenxa yabandilaleleyo.

<span id="an_27:12">27:12</span> Musa ukundinikela elitheni
labandibandezelayo, Ngokuba ndiphakanyelwe ngamangqina axokayo,
nabafutha ukugonyamela.

<span id="an_27:13">27:13</span> Ndinge ndiphelelwe, koko bendikholwa
kukuba ndokubona ukulunga kukaYehova Ezweni lobu bomi.

<span id="an_27:14">27:14</span> Thembela kuYehova; Yomelela, ikhaliphe
intliziyo yakho, Uthembele kuYehova.

<span id="an_28:1">28:1</span> EkaDavide. Ndidanduluka kuwe, Yehova;
Liwa lam, musa ukuzenza isithulu; Hleze, wakuthi cwaka kum, Ndifane
nabahla baye emhadini.

<span id="an_28:2">28:2</span> Yiva izwi lokukhunga kwam ekuzibikeni
kwam kuwe, Ekuziphakamiseleni kwam izandla zam kwingcwele kangcwele.

<span id="an_28:3">28:3</span> Musa ukundiqweqwedisa nabangendawo,
Nabenzi bobutshinga; Abathetha uxolo kummelwane wabo, Benobubi
ezintliziyweni zabo.

<span id="an_28:4">28:4</span> Banike ngokwemisebenzi yabo, ngokobubi
beentlondi zabo; Banike ngokwezenzo zezandla zabo; Babuyisele
ngokwempatho yabo.

<span id="an_28:5">28:5</span> Ekubeni bengayiqondi imisebenzi kaYehova,
Nezenzo zezandla zakhe, Uya kubagungxula, angabakhi.

<span id="an_28:6">28:6</span> Makabongwe uYehova, Kuba elivile ilizwi
lokukhunga kwam.

<span id="an_28:7">28:7</span> NguYehova amandla am nengweletshetshe
yam; Yakholosa ngaye intliziyo yam, ndancedeka. Iyadlamka ke intliziyo
yam, Ndiyamdumisa ngengoma yam.

<span id="an_28:8">28:8</span> UYehova ungamandla kubo; Uligwiba
losindiso kumthanjiswa wakhe yena.

<span id="an_28:9">28:9</span> Sindisa abantu bakho, Usikelele ilifa
lakho, Ubaluse, ubathwale kude kuse ephakadeni.

<span id="an_29:1">29:1</span> Umhobe kaDavide. Mnikeni uYehova, nina
nyana bakaThixo, Mnikeni uYehova uzuko namandla.

<span id="an_29:2">29:2</span> Mnikeni uYehova uzuko lwegama lakhe;
Qubudani kuYehova nivethe ezingcwele.

<span id="an_29:3">29:3</span> Izwi likaYehova liphezu kwamanzi; UThixo
wozuko uyadudumisa, KwauYehova phezu kwamanzi amaninzi.

<span id="an_29:4">29:4</span> Izwi likaYehova linamandla, Izwi
likaYehova linobungangamela;

<span id="an_29:5">29:5</span> Izwi likaYehova laphula imisedare,
UYehova waphula imisedare yaseLebhanon.

<span id="an_29:6">29:6</span> Uyidlobisa njengenkonyana, ILebhanon
neSiriyon njengethole lenqu.

<span id="an_29:7">29:7</span> Izwi likaYehova lilenyise okwamalangatye
omlilo,

<span id="an_29:8">29:8</span> Izwi likaYehova liyenza isaqhwithi
intlango, UYehova uyenza isaqhwithi intlango yaseKadeshe.

<span id="an_29:9">29:9</span> Izwi likaYehova lizuzisa amaxhamakazi,
Lihlube amahlathi; Etempileni yakhe into yonke iphela ithi, Luzuko!

<span id="an_29:10">29:10</span> UYehova wahlala kunogumbe, UYehova
uhleli enguKumkani ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_29:11">29:11</span> UYehova uya kubanika abantu bakhe
amandla; UYehova uya kubasikelela abantu bakhe ngoxolo.

<span id="an_30:1">30:1</span> Umhobe: ingoma yokusungulwa kwayo indlu.
EkaDavide. Ndiya kukuphakamisa, Yehova, kuba undirholile wandinyusa,
Akwazivuyisa iintshaba zam ngam.

<span id="an_30:2">30:2</span> Yehova, Thixo wam, Ndazibika kuwe,
wandiphilisa;

<span id="an_30:3">30:3</span> Yehova, uwunyusile kwelabafileyo
umphefumlo wam, Wandidlisa ubomi, ukuba ndingehli ndiye emhadini.

<span id="an_30:4">30:4</span> Mbetheleni uhadi uYehova, nina bakhe
benceba, Nibulele isikhumbuzo sakhe esingcwele,

<span id="an_30:5">30:5</span> Ngokuba yinto yephanyazo umsindo wakhe,
Itarhu lakhe liyinto yobomi; Ngokuhlwa kulalisa ukulila, Kusasa kubakho
ukumemelela.

<span id="an_30:6">30:6</span> Ke mna ndathi ebunqobeni bam, Andiyi
kushukunyiswa naphakade.

<span id="an_30:7">30:7</span> Yehova, enkolosekweni yakho ubuyiqinisile
intaba yam; Ubusithelisile ubuso bakho, ndakhwankqiswa.

<span id="an_30:8">30:8</span> Ndadanduluka kuwe, Yehova, Ndakhunga
kuYehova:

<span id="an_30:9">30:9</span> Ndathi, Kukho nzuzo yani na egazini lam,
ekuhleni kwam ndiye esihogweni? Lokudumisa na uthuli? loyixela na
inyaniso yakho?

<span id="an_30:10">30:10</span> Yiva, Yehova, undibabale; Yehova, yiba
ngumncedi wam.

<span id="an_30:11">30:11</span> Wakuguqula ukulila kwam, kwaba
kukuqamba; Wandikhulula ezirhwexayo, wandibhinqisa uvuyo,

<span id="an_30:12">30:12</span> Ukuze uzuko lwam luvume ngawe, lungathi
cwaka. Yehova, Thixo wam, ndiya kubulela kuwe ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_31:1">31:1</span> Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide. Ndizimela
ngawe, Yehova, mandingaze ndidaniswe; Ndisize ngobulungisa bakho.

<span id="an_31:2">31:2</span> Ndithobele indlebe yakho, ungxame
undihlangule; Yiba liliwa eliligwiba kum, Indlu yemboniselo
yokundisindisa.

<span id="an_31:3">31:3</span> Ngokuba ingxondorha yam nemboniselo yam
nguwe; Ngenxa yegama lakho uya kundikhapha undithundeze.

<span id="an_31:4">31:4</span> Uya kundirhola esibatheni ababesigqumele
mna, Ngokuba uyinqaba yam.

<span id="an_31:5">31:5</span> Ndiwuyaleza umoya wam esandleni sakho;
Uyandikhulula, Yehova, Thixo wenyaniso.

<span id="an_31:6">31:6</span> Ndibathiyile abagcine amampunge angento
yanto. Ndikholose ngoYehova mna.

<span id="an_31:7">31:7</span> Ndiya kugcoba ndivuye ngenceba yakho,
Ngenxa enokuba uzibonile iintsizi zam, Wazazi iingxingongo zomphefumlo
wam;

<span id="an_31:8">31:8</span> Akwandivingcela ngesandla seentshaba,
Wazimisa endaweni ebanzi iinyawo zam.

<span id="an_31:9">31:9</span> Ndibabale, Yehova, ngokuba
ndibandezelekile; Lonakele kukukhathazeka iliso lam, nomphefumlo wam,
nesisu sam;

<span id="an_31:10">31:10</span> Ngokuba buphelile sisingqala ubomi bam,
Neminyaka yam kukuncwina; Ayagexa amandla am ngobugwenxa bam, Namathambo
am aluphele.

<span id="an_31:11">31:11</span> Ngenxa yababandezeli bam bonke ndaba
sisingcikivo, Ngokukodwa kubamelwane bam; ndaba yinto yokunkwantyisa
kwabandaziyo; Abandibonayo ngaphandle baya ndibaleka.

<span id="an_31:12">31:12</span> Ndilityelwe njengomfi
ongasakhunjulwayo; Ndinjengesitya esiza kulahlwa.

<span id="an_31:13">31:13</span> Ngokuba ndive intlebendwane yabaninzi,
Ukunxunguphala ngeenxa zonke. Ekugquguleni kwabo ngam, Bankqangiyela
ukuthabatha umphefumlo wam.

<span id="an_31:14">31:14</span> Ke mna ndikholose ngawe, Yehova;
Ndithi, UnguThixo wam wena.

<span id="an_31:15">31:15</span> Asesandleni sakho amaxesha am;
Ndihlangule esandleni seentshaba zam nakwabandisukelayo.

<span id="an_31:16">31:16</span> Khanyisa ubuso bakho phezu komkhonzi
wakho; Ndisindise ngenceba yakho.

<span id="an_31:17">31:17</span> Yehova, andiyi kudana, ngokuba ndinqula
wena; Makudane abangendawo, bathi cwaka kwelabafileyo.

<span id="an_31:18">31:18</span> Mawubotshwe umlomo wobuxoki, Othetha
ngelungisa ngokusa, Unekratshi, udela.

<span id="an_31:19">31:19</span> Hayi, ubukhulu bokulunga kwakho,
obuqwebele abakoyikayo, Obenzela abazimela ngawe, ebusweni boonyana
babantu!

<span id="an_31:20">31:20</span> Ubasithelisa esitheni lobuso bakho
kumayelenqe abantu; Uyabagusha emnqubeni ekubambaneni kweelwimi.

<span id="an_31:21">31:21</span> Makabongwe uYehova, Ngokuba endenzele
inceba ebalulekileyo emzini onqabileyo.

<span id="an_31:22">31:22</span> Ke mna ndathi ekuphakuzeleni kwam,
Ndinqanyulwe andabakho emehlweni akho. Waliva noko izwi lokukhunga kwam
ekuzibikeni kwam kuwe.

<span id="an_31:23">31:23</span> Thandani uYehova, nonke nina bakhe
benceba; NguYehova umlondolozi wabanyanisileyo, Umphindezeli ngokukhulu
kowenza ngekratshi.

<span id="an_31:24">31:24</span> Yomelelani, ikhaliphe intliziyo yenu
Nonke nina nithembele kuYehova.

<span id="an_32:1">32:1</span> EkaDavide. Eyokuqiqa. Hayi, uyolo lwakhe
olukreqo luxolelweyo, osono siselelweyo!

<span id="an_32:2">32:2</span> Hayi, uyolo lomntu angabubaleliyo uYehova
kuye ubugwenxa, Ekungekho kukhohlisa emoyeni wakhe!

<span id="an_32:3">32:3</span> Ndithi ndakuthi cwaka, aluphale amathambo
am Ngokubhonga kwam imihla yonke.

<span id="an_32:4">32:4</span> Ngokuba imini nobusuku, besinzima phezu
kwam isandla sakho, Baguquka ubumanzi bam, baba kukubalela
kwasehlotyeni. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_32:5">32:5</span> Ndikwazisile isono sam, ubugwenxa bam
andabugquma; Ndathi, Ndoluvuma ukreqo lwam kuYehova; Wabuxolela ke wena
ubugwenxa besono sam. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_32:6">32:6</span> Ngenxa yoko mabathandaze kuwe bonke
abenceba ngexesha lokukufumana; Inene, ekukhukuleni kwamanzi amaninzi
Akayi kufika kubo.

<span id="an_32:7">32:7</span> Wena uyindawo yokuzimela kwam;
uyandilondoloza embandezelweni, Undingqonge ngomemelelo lokusiza.
(Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_32:8">32:8</span> Ndiya kukuqiqisa ndikuyalele indlela
owohamba ngayo: Ndiya kukucebisa, iliso lam likuwe.

<span id="an_32:9">32:9</span> Musani ukuba njengamahashe,
njengoondlebende, ukungabi nangqondo; Abazivatho zingumkhala, neentambo
zokubabopha umlomo; Bengenazo abasayi kusondela kuwe.

<span id="an_32:10">32:10</span> Mkhulu umvandedwa wongendawo; Ke
okholosa ngoYehova, yena uya kumjikela ngenceba.

<span id="an_32:11">32:11</span> Vuyani kuYehova, nigcobe, nina
malungisa, Nimemelele, nina nonke bantliziyo zithe tye.

<span id="an_33:1">33:1</span> Memelelani kuYehova, nina malungisa;
Ibafanele abathe tye indumiso.

<span id="an_33:2">33:2</span> Bulelani kuYehova ngohadi, Mbetheleni
umrhubhe ontambo zilishumi.

<span id="an_33:3">33:3</span> Mvumeleni ingoma entsha, Nilungise
ukubetha ngelokuduma;

<span id="an_33:4">33:4</span> Nokuba lithe tye ilizwi likaYehova, Konke
akwenzayo kuthembekile.

<span id="an_33:5">33:5</span> Ngumthandi wobulungisa nokusesikweni,
Lizele ihlabathi yinceba kaYehova.

<span id="an_33:6">33:6</span> Lenzeka ngelizwi likaYehova izulu,
Umkhosi walo lonke ngomoya womlomo wakhe.

<span id="an_33:7">33:7</span> Ulobutha njengemfumba amanzi olwandle,
Ulobeka koovimba amanzi enzonzobila.

<span id="an_33:8">33:8</span> Malimoyike uYehova lonke ihlabathi,
Bamhlonele bonke abemi belimiweyo;

<span id="an_33:9">33:9</span> Ngokuba wathetha, kwabakho; Wawisa
umthetho yena, kwema.

<span id="an_33:10">33:10</span> UYehova ulitshitshisile icebo
leentlanga; Uzalele iingcinga zezizwe.

<span id="an_33:11">33:11</span> Icebo likaYehova limi ngonaphakade,
Iingcinga zentliziyo yakhe kwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana.

<span id="an_33:12">33:12</span> Hayi, uyolo lohlanga oluThixo walo
unguYehova; Lwabantu abanyulileyo, baba lilifa kuye.

<span id="an_33:13">33:13</span> Uqondele esemazulwini uYehova;
Uyababona bonke oonyana babantu;

<span id="an_33:14">33:14</span> Esendaweni yakhe yokuhlala, wondele
Kubemi bonke behlabathi:

<span id="an_33:15">33:15</span> Ulobumba ngakunye intliziyo yabo,
Uloqonda zonke izenzo zabo.

<span id="an_33:16">33:16</span> Akukho kumkani osindiswa yimpi enkulu;
Igorha alihlangulwa ngamandla alo amakhulu.

<span id="an_33:17">33:17</span> Liyaxoka ihashe ukuba lingasindisa,
Nangamandla alo amakhulu alinakusiza.

<span id="an_33:18">33:18</span> Yabona, iliso likaYehova likubo
abamoyikayo, Abalindele inceba yakhe,

<span id="an_33:19">33:19</span> Ukuba awuhlangule ekufeni umphefumlo
wabo, Abagcine ngexesha lendlala.

<span id="an_33:20">33:20</span> Umphefumlo wethu ulindele kuYehova;
Nguye uncedo lwethu, nengweletshetshe yethu.

<span id="an_33:21">33:21</span> Ngokuba iya kuvuya ngaye intliziyo
yethu, Sikholosile nje ngegama lakhe elingcwele.

<span id="an_33:22">33:22</span> Inceba yakho mayibe phezu kwethu,
Yehova, Njengoko sikulindeleyo kuwe.

<span id="an_34:1">34:1</span> EkaDavide; oko wazenza ophambene ingqondo
phambi koAbhimeleki, waza yena wamgxotha, wahamba. Ndiya kumbonga
uYehova ngamaxesha onke, Ihlale isemlonyeni wam indumiso yakhe.

<span id="an_34:2">34:2</span> Uya kuqhayisa umphefumlo wam ngoYehova;
Bova abalulamileyo, bavuye.

<span id="an_34:3">34:3</span> Menzeni mkhulu kunye nam uYehova,
Siliphakamise kunye igama lakhe.

<span id="an_34:4">34:4</span> Ndamfuna uYehova, wandiphendula;
Wandihlangula kwiinto zonke endinxunguphala zizo.

<span id="an_34:5">34:5</span> Babheka kuye, bakhazimla; Ubuso babo
ababa nazintloni.

<span id="an_34:6">34:6</span> Usizana lwadanduluka, weva uYehova,
Walusindisa ezimbandezelweni zalo zonke.

<span id="an_34:7">34:7</span> Isithunywa sikaYehova sibangqinga ngeenxa
zonke abamoyikayo, Sibahlangule.

<span id="an_34:8">34:8</span> Yivani, nibone ukuba ulungile uYehova.
Hayi, uyolo lomfo ozimela ngaye!

<span id="an_34:9">34:9</span> Moyikeni uYehova, nina bangcwele bakhe,
Ngokuba abanakuswela abamoyikayo.

<span id="an_34:10">34:10</span> Iingonyama ezintsha ziyaswela, zilambe;
Ke bona abamfunayo uYehova abasweli nanye into elungileyo.

<span id="an_34:11">34:11</span> Yizani, bonyana, phulaphulani kum;
Ndonifundisa ukoyika uYehova.

<span id="an_34:12">34:12</span> Ngubani na umntu obungxameleyo ubomi,
Othanda imihla yokubona okulungileyo?

<span id="an_34:13">34:13</span> Gcina ulwimi lwakho ebubini, Umlomo
wakho ungathethi nkohliso.

<span id="an_34:14">34:14</span> Suka ebubini, wenze okulungileyo; Funa
uxolo, uluphuthume.

<span id="an_34:15">34:15</span> Amehlo kaYehova akumalungisa, Iindlebe
zakhe zisekuzibikeni kwawo.

<span id="an_34:16">34:16</span> Ubuso bukaYehova bujonge abenzi bokubi,
Ukuba akunqumle ehlabathini ukukhunjulwa kwabo.

<span id="an_34:17">34:17</span> Akhala, weva uYehova; Wawahlangula
ezimbandezelweni zawo zonke.

<span id="an_34:18">34:18</span> Usondele uYehova kwabantliziyo
zaphukileyo, Abasindise abamoya utyumkileyo.

<span id="an_34:19">34:19</span> Buninzi ububi obulihlelayo ilungisa, Ke
uYehova ulihlangula kubo bonke.

<span id="an_34:20">34:20</span> Uyawagcina onke amathambo alo,
Akwaphuki nalinye kuwo.

<span id="an_34:21">34:21</span> Ububi buyambulala ongendawo; Abathiyi
belungisa bayalithwala ityala.

<span id="an_34:22">34:22</span> UYehova uyawukhulula umphefumlo
wabakhonzi bakhe, Bangathwali tyala bonke abazimela ngaye.

<span id="an_35:1">35:1</span> EkaDavide. Bambana, Yehova, nababambana
nam. Yilwa nabalwa nam.

<span id="an_35:2">35:2</span> Qubula ikhaka nengweletshetshe, Usuk’ume
undincede.

<span id="an_35:3">35:3</span> Rhola umkhonto, uvingce indlela
yabandisukelayo; Yithi kumphefumlo wam, Ndilusindiso lwakho.

<span id="an_35:4">35:4</span> Mabadane, bahlazeke, abazungula
umphefumlo wam; Mababuye umva babe neentloni abacinga ububi ngam.

<span id="an_35:5">35:5</span> Mababe njengomququ phambi komoya,
Sibatyhale isithunywa sikaYehova, bawe.

<span id="an_35:6">35:6</span> Indlela yabo mayibe mnyama, ibe
buthelezi, Sibasukele isithunywa sikaYehova.

<span id="an_35:7">35:7</span> Ngokuba basigqumele mna isibatha sabo
ngelize; Bawumbela isihogo umphefumlo wam ngelize.

<span id="an_35:8">35:8</span> Mayimfikele intshabalalo engazi;
Sibambise yena isibatha sakhe awasigqumayo, Eyele kuso ngesithonga.

<span id="an_35:9">35:9</span> Wogcoba ke umphefumlo wam kuYehova, Ube
nemihlali ngosindiso lwakhe.

<span id="an_35:10">35:10</span> Onke amathambo am aya kuthi, Yehova,
ngubani na onjengawe, Mhlanguli wosizana kowomeleleyo kunalo, Kwausizana
nehlwempu kumxhakamfuli walo?

<span id="an_35:11">35:11</span> Kusuke kwema amangqina angenakulungisa,
Andibuza into endingayaziyo,

<span id="an_35:12">35:12</span> Bandibuyekeza ngobubi esikhundleni
sokulungileyo; Uxhwalekile umphefumlo wam.

<span id="an_35:13">35:13</span> Ke mna, xa babesifa, iingubo zam
bezizezirhwexayo; Ndawucinezela umphefumlo wam ngokuzila ukudla;
Umthandazo wam wabuyela esifubeni sam.

<span id="an_35:14">35:14</span> Ndaziphatha njengokungathi unguwethu,
njengokungathi ungumzalwana kum, ukuhamba-hamba kwam; Ndanga
ndingombambazelela unina, ukuthobeka kwam, ndinezimnyama zokuzila.

<span id="an_35:15">35:15</span> Ke ekuqhwaleleni kwam avuya, ahlangana,
Ahlangana ngam amagxidolo, nendingabaziyo, Bandihlalela ngentlamba,
abayeka.

<span id="an_35:16">35:16</span> Ngokweentshembenxa ezizihiba ngenxa
yesonka, Banditshixizela amazinyo.

<span id="an_35:17">35:17</span> Nkosi, kunini na ubonela? Buyisa
umphefumlo wam kwiintshabalaliso zabo, Okuphela kwawo ezingonyameni.

<span id="an_35:18">35:18</span> Ndiya kubulela kuwe ebandleni elikhulu,
Ebantwini abaninzi ndiya kukudumisa.

<span id="an_35:19">35:19</span> Mazingandivuyeleli iintshaba zam
ngobuxoki, Bangatyandelani ngoshiyi abandithiyayo ngelize:

<span id="an_35:20">35:20</span> Ngokuba abathethi luxolo; Bacinga
amazwi enkohliso ngabanyhamnyhekileyo belizwe.

<span id="an_35:21">35:21</span> Bayandisinekela, Bathi, Tshotsho!
Tshotsho! Abonile amehlo ethu.

<span id="an_35:22">35:22</span> Ubonile, Yehova; musa ukuba sisithulu;
Nkosi, musa ukuba kude kum.

<span id="an_35:23">35:23</span> Zivuse, uphaphe ngenxa yebango lam,
Thixo wam, Nkosi yam, ngenxa yento esibambene ngayo.

<span id="an_35:24">35:24</span> Lithethe ityala lam ngokobulungisa
bakho, Yehova Thixo wam; Mabangandivuyeleli;

<span id="an_35:25">35:25</span> Mabangathi entliziyweni yabo, Tshotsho!
Nantso into ebe siyfuna! Mabangathi, Simginyile.

<span id="an_35:26">35:26</span> Mabadane, babe neentloni kunye
Abavuyela ububi bam; Bambathe ukudana nehlazo Abazikhulisayo kunam.

<span id="an_35:27">35:27</span> Mabamemelele, bavuye, abananze
ubulungisa bam, Bahlale besithi, Makabe mkhulu uYehova, Ulonanze uxolo
lomkhonzi wakhe.

<span id="an_35:28">35:28</span> Ulwimi lwam luya kuxela ubulungisa
bakho Nendumiso yakho, imihla yonke.

<span id="an_36:1">36:1</span> Kumongameli. Eyomkhonzi kaYehova.
EkaDavide. Ongendawo unezihlabo zokreqo entliziyweni yakhe ngaphakathi,
ezithi, Akukho koyika Thixo emehlweni akhe,

<span id="an_36:2">36:2</span> Ngokuba zithetha kuye ngokugudileyo
emehlweni akhe, Zide zimfumanise ubugwenxa bakhe, zimthiye.

<span id="an_36:3">36:3</span> Amazwi omlomo wakhe abubutshinga
nenkohliso; Uyekile ukwenza ngokuqiqa nangokulungisa.

<span id="an_36:4">36:4</span> Ucinga ubutshinga elukhukweni lwakhe;
Uzimisa endleleni engalungileyo; Akabucekisi ububi.

<span id="an_36:5">36:5</span> Yehova, inceba yakho ifikelela ezulwini,
Ukuthembeka kwakho esibhakabhakeni.

<span id="an_36:6">36:6</span> Ubulungisa bakho bunjengeentaba
zikaThixo; Izigwebo zakho zingamanzi enzonzobila; Usindisa umntu
neenkomo, Yehova.

<span id="an_36:7">36:7</span> Hayi, ixabiso lenceba yakho, Thixo!
Oonyana babantu bazimela ngethunzi lamaphiko akho.

<span id="an_36:8">36:8</span> Bayahluthiswa kukutyeba kwendlu yakho;
Ubaseza emlanjeni weziyolo zakho.

<span id="an_36:9">36:9</span> Ngokuba likuwe ithende lobomi;
Ekukhanyeni kwakho sibona ukukhanya.

<span id="an_36:10">36:10</span> Bolulele inceba yakho abakwaziyo,
Ubolulele ubulungisa bakho abantliziyo zithe tye.

<span id="an_36:11">36:11</span> Malungandinyatheli unyawo lonekratshi.
Singandiphekuzi isandla sabangendawo.

<span id="an_36:12">36:12</span> Nabo bewile abasebenzi bobutshinga;
Batyhalwe bawa, ababa nakuvuka.

<span id="an_37:1">37:1</span> EkaDavide. Musa ukuzivuthisa ngomsindo
ngabenzi bobubi; Musa ukubamonela abenzi bobugqwetha.

<span id="an_37:2">37:2</span> Ngokuba baya kusikwa kamsinyane
njengengca, Babune njengohlaza oluphumayo.

<span id="an_37:3">37:3</span> Kholosa ngoYehova, wenze okulungileyo;
Lime ilizwe, ulandelane nokuthembeka.

<span id="an_37:4">37:4</span> Ziyolise ngoYehova; Wokunika okunqwenelwa
yintliziyo yakho.

<span id="an_37:5">37:5</span> Yiyekele kuYehova indlela yakho, Ukholose
ngaye; wokwenzela,

<span id="an_37:6">37:6</span> Abuvelise njengokukhanya ubulungisa
bakho, Nebango lakho njengemini enkulu.

<span id="an_37:7">37:7</span> Yithi cwaka kuYehova, ulindele kuye; Musa
ukuzivuthisa ngomsindo ngonempumelelo ngendlela yakhe, Ngomntu ofeza
amayelenqe.

<span id="an_37:8">37:8</span> Lahla umsindo, ushiye ubushushu; Musa
ukuzivuthisa ngomsindo, kuba oko kusingisa ekwenzeni ububi kuphela.

<span id="an_37:9">37:9</span> Ngokuba abenzi bobubi baya kunqunyulwa;
Ke bona abamthembayo uYehova, baya kulidla ilifa ilizwe.

<span id="an_37:10">37:10</span> Kusaya kuba mzuzwana, angabikho
ongendawo; Uthi wakuyikhangela indawo yakhe, angabikho.

<span id="an_37:11">37:11</span> Ke bona abalulamileyo baya kulidla
ilifa ilizwe, Baziyolise ngobuninzi boxolo.

<span id="an_37:12">37:12</span> Ongendawo ulenzela amayelenqe ilungisa,
Ulitshixizela amazinyo akhe.

<span id="an_37:13">37:13</span> INkosi iyamhleka, Ngokuba ibona ukuba
iyeza imini yakhe.

<span id="an_37:14">37:14</span> Barhole ikrele abangendawo, bagobe
isaphetha sabo, Ukuba bawise usizana nehlwempu, Basike abandlela zithe
tye.

<span id="an_37:15">37:15</span> Ikrele labo liya kungena kwakweyabo
intliziyo, Zaphuke izaphetha zabo.

<span id="an_37:16">37:16</span> Ilungile intwana elinayo ilungisa,
Kunentabalala abanayo abangendawo abaninzi:

<span id="an_37:17">37:17</span> Ngokuba iingalo zabangendawo ziya
kwaphulwa; NguYehova umxhasi wamalungisa.

<span id="an_37:18">37:18</span> NguYehova umazi wemihla
yabagqibeleleyo, Nelifa labo liya kuba ngunaphakade.

<span id="an_37:19">37:19</span> Abayi kudana ngexesha lobubi; Baya
kuhlutha ngeemini zendlala:

<span id="an_37:20">37:20</span> Ngokuba abangendawo bayatshabalala;
Iintshaba zikaYehova zinjengobuhle bamadlelo; Ziya kuphela njengomsi,
ziphele.

<span id="an_37:21">37:21</span> Uyaboleka ongendawo, angabuyisi; Ke
lona ilungisa liyababala, liphe.

<span id="an_37:22">37:22</span> Ngokuba abasikelelweyo nguye baya
kulidla ilifa ilizwe, Banqanyulwe abatshabhisiweyo nguye.

<span id="an_37:23">37:23</span> Amanyathela omfo aqiniswa nguYehova,
Ayithande indlela yakhe.

<span id="an_37:24">37:24</span> Ewile, akayi kuqungquluza, Ngokuba
nguYehova umxhasi wesandla sakhe.

<span id="an_37:25">37:25</span> Ndaka ndamtsha, kungokunje ndimdala;
Ukanti andizanga ndilibone ilungisa lishiywa, Nembewu yalo ivukela
ukutya.

<span id="an_37:26">37:26</span> Imihla yonke liyababala, liboleke
abanye; Nembewu yalo iyintsikelelo.

<span id="an_37:27">37:27</span> Suka ebubini, wenze okulungileyo,
Uhlale ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_37:28">37:28</span> Ngokuba uYehova uthanda okusesikweni,
Angabashiyi abenceba bakhe; Bagciniwe ngonaphakade: Ke yona imbewu
yongendawo iyanqanyulwa.

<span id="an_37:29">37:29</span> Amalungisa aya kulidla ilifa ilizwe,
Ahlale kulo ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_37:30">37:30</span> Umlomo welungisa uxela ubulumko,
Nolwimi lwalo luthetha okusesikweni.

<span id="an_37:31">37:31</span> Umyalelo woThixo walo usentliziyweni
yalo; Akayi kuhexa amanyathela alo.

<span id="an_37:32">37:32</span> Ongendawo uyalilalela ilungisa, Ufuna
ukulibulala.

<span id="an_37:33">37:33</span> UYehova akalinikeli esandleni sakhe,
Angaligwebi ekuthethweni kwetyala lalo.

<span id="an_37:34">37:34</span> Thembela kuYehova, ugcine indlela
yakhe; Wokuphakamisa, ulidle ilifa ilizwe; Ekunqanyulweni kongendawo
wobonela.

<span id="an_37:35">37:35</span> Ndimbonile ongendawo,
oyingqwangangqwili, Exanda njengomthi omilileyo, uluhlaza;

<span id="an_37:36">37:36</span> Kwadlula umntu, nanko engasekho;
Ndamfuna, akafumaneka.

<span id="an_37:37">37:37</span> Gcina ogqibeleleyo, ukhangele othe tye;
Ngokuba izivela-mva zezomntu woxolo.

<span id="an_37:38">37:38</span> Ke bona abangendawo batshatyalaliswa
kuphele; Izivela-mva zongendawo ziyanqanyulwa.

<span id="an_37:39">37:39</span> Usindiso lwamalungisa luphuma kuYehova;
Uligwiba lawo ngexesha lembandezelo.

<span id="an_37:40">37:40</span> UYehova uyawanceda, awasindise,
Awasindise kongendawo, awasindise, Ngokuba azimela ngaye.

<span id="an_38:1">38:1</span> Umhobe kaDavide: eyokukhumbuza. Yehova,
musa ukundohlwaya unoburhalarhume, Ungandithethisi unobushushu:

<span id="an_38:2">38:2</span> Ngokuba iintolo zakho zitshone kum, Sehla
kanzima kum isandla sakho.

<span id="an_38:3">38:3</span> Akukho ndawo iphilileyo enyameni yam,
ngenxa yokubhavuma kwakho; Akukho kuphila emathanjeni am, ngenxa yezono
zam.

<span id="an_38:4">38:4</span> Ngokuba ubugwenxa bam bugqithile
entlokweni yam, Bundisinda njengomthwalo onzima.

<span id="an_38:5">38:5</span> Iyanuka, iyabhiqiza imivumbo yam, Ngenxa
yokumatha kwam.

<span id="an_38:6">38:6</span> Ndiyapenapena, ndisibekeke kakhulu; Yonke
imini ndihamba-hamba ngezimnyama zokuzila.

<span id="an_38:7">38:7</span> Ngokuba kuyatshisa emihlubulweni yam,
Akukho ndawo iphilileyo enyameni yam.

<span id="an_38:8">38:8</span> Ndiqobekile, ndityumkile kakhulu;
Ndibhongiswa kukugcuma kwentliziyo yam.

<span id="an_38:9">38:9</span> Nkosi yam, uphambi kwakho wonke umnqweno
wam, Nokuncwina kwam akusithele kuwe.

<span id="an_38:10">38:10</span> Iphaphu lam liyabetha, ndiphelelwe
ngamandla; Ukukhanya kwamehlo am, nako oko, akukho kum.

<span id="an_38:11">38:11</span> Abandithandayo nowethu bamele mgama
ekubethweni kwam, Nezalamane zam zimi kude.

<span id="an_38:12">38:12</span> Bandithiyele abafuna umphefumlo wam;
Abangxamele ukuba ndihlelwe bububi bathetha izinto zokweyelisela,
Bacamanga inkohliso imini yonke.

<span id="an_38:13">38:13</span> Ke mna ndinjengesithulu, andiva;
Njengesidenge esingawuvuliyo umlomo waso.

<span id="an_38:14">38:14</span> Ndinjengomntu ongeva nto, Omlomo
ungenakuthethisa.

<span id="an_38:15">38:15</span> Ngokuba ndilindele kuwe, Yehova; Kuya
kuphendula wena, Nkosi yam, Thixo wam,

<span id="an_38:16">38:16</span> Ngokuba ndithi, Hleze bandivuyelele
Bona abo bangazikhulisayo kum ekutyibilikeni konyawo lwam.

<span id="an_38:17">38:17</span> Ngokuba ndihlalele ukujingxela,
Umvandedwa wam uphambi kwam amaxesha onke.

<span id="an_38:18">38:18</span> Ngokuba ndiya kubuxela ubugwenxa bam;
Ndinesithukuthezi ngenxa yesono sam.

<span id="an_38:19">38:19</span> Ke zona iintshaba zam ziphilile,
ziziimfidi; Baninzi abandithiyileyo bexoka;

<span id="an_38:20">38:20</span> Abandibuyekeza ngobubi esikhundleni
sokulungileyo Bayandichasa, ngenxa yokuphuthuma kwam okulungileyo.

<span id="an_38:21">38:21</span> Musa ukundishiya, Yehova; Thixo wam,
musa ukuba kude nam.

<span id="an_38:22">38:22</span> Khawuleza undincede, Nkosi yam,
Msindisi wam.

<span id="an_39:1">39:1</span> Kumongameli, kuYedutun. Umhobe kaDavide.
Ndathi, Ndiya kuzigcina iindlela zam, Ndingoni ngolwimi lwam; Ndiya
kuwugcina ngokuwubopha umlomo wam, Xa ongendawo asephambi kwam.

<span id="an_39:2">39:2</span> Ndaba sisidenge, ndathozama,
Ndazisulungisa nakokulungileyo; Wagxobha-gxobheka umvandedwa wam.

<span id="an_39:3">39:3</span> Yaba nobushushu intliziyo yam phakathi
kwam, Ekucamangeni kwam wavutha umlilo. Ndathetha ke ngolwimi lwam,

<span id="an_39:4">39:4</span> Ndathi, Ndazise, Yehova, isiphelo sam,
Nomlinganiso wemihla yam, into oyiyo; Mandikwazi ukunqamka kwam, into
okuyiyo.

<span id="an_39:5">39:5</span> Yabona, uyenze imihla yam yangangobubanzi
besandla; Nobomi bam bunjengento engento phambi kwakho; Ngumphunga nje
bonke abantu, nakuba bemi. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_39:6">39:6</span> Uhamba-hamba umntu enjengesithunzi nje
kodwa; Baxokozela ngomphunga nje kodwa; Bafumba, bengazi ukuba ngubani
na oya kukuhlanganisa.

<span id="an_39:7">39:7</span> Ngoku ndiya kuthembela kwintoni na, Nkosi
yam? Ukulinda kwam kukuwe.

<span id="an_39:8">39:8</span> Ndihlangule elukreqweni lwam lonke; Musa
ukundimisela ingcikivo yesidenge.

<span id="an_39:9">39:9</span> Ndisisidenge, umlomo wam andiwuvuli,
Ngokuba oko kwenziwe nguwe.

<span id="an_39:10">39:10</span> Sisuse kum isibetho sakho; Mna
ndiyaphela kukutyundyutha kwesandla sakho.

<span id="an_39:11">39:11</span> Wakumthethisa umntu ngezohlwayo ngenxa
yobugwenxa, Uyasonakalisa njengenundu isoya sakhe; Bangumphunga nje
kodwa bonke abantu. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_39:12">39:12</span> Yiva umthandazo wam, Yehova, Kubekele
indlebe ukuzibika kwam. Musa ukuthi tu ezinyembezini zam; Ngokuba
ndingumphambukeli kuwe, Undwendwe, njengoobawo bonke.

<span id="an_39:13">39:13</span> Bheka phaya, ungandikhangeli,
khendincumeze, Ndingekemki ndingabi sabakho.

<span id="an_40:1">40:1</span> Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide.
Ndathembela, ndithembele kuYehova, Wathoba, wakuva ukuzibika kwam.

<span id="an_40:2">40:2</span> Wandirhola emhadini wentshabalalo,
naseludakeni lomgxobhozo, Wazimisa eliweni iinyawo zam, wakuqinisa
ukunyathela kwam.

<span id="an_40:3">40:3</span> Wabeka emlonyeni wam ingoma entsha,
indumiso kuThixo wethu; Abaninzi bayabona, boyike, Bakholose ngoYehova.

<span id="an_40:4">40:4</span> Hayi, uyolo lwendoda emenze uYehova
inkoloseko yayo, Ingabheki kwabagwagwisayo, nakubanxaxhi abanamanga!

<span id="an_40:5">40:5</span> Yehova, Thixo wam, wena wenze okuninzi
ngemisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo, Nangeengcinga zakho kuthi; Akukho nto
inokulinganiswa nawe; Okanye bendiya kuyixela, ndithethe ngayo; Ke
ziyinkohla engenakubalwa.

<span id="an_40:6">40:6</span> Akunanze mbingelelo namnikelo wakudla;
Iindlebe zam uzivulile; Akubizi dini linyukayo nadini lasono.

<span id="an_40:7">40:7</span> Ndaza ndathi, Yabona, Ndiyeza; encwadini
esongwayo kubhaliwe ngam.

<span id="an_40:8">40:8</span> Ukwenza okulikholo kuwe, Thixo wam,
ndikunanzile; Nomyalelo wakho usezibilinini zam ngaphakathi.

<span id="an_40:9">40:9</span> Ndashumayela iindaba ezilungileyo
zobulungisa ebandleni elikhulu; Yabona, andiwuthintelanga umlomo wam;
Yehova, wena uyazi.

<span id="an_40:10">40:10</span> Ubulungisa bakho andibugqumanga
phakathi kwentliziyo yam; Ndakukhankanya ukuthembeka kwakho nosindiso
lwakho; Andiyikhanyelanga inceba yakho nenyaniso yakho ebandleni
elikhulu.

<span id="an_40:11">40:11</span> Wena, Yehova, akuyi kuzithintela
iimfesane zakho kum; Inceba yakho nenyaniso yakho iya kuhlala
indilondoloza.

<span id="an_40:12">40:12</span> Ngokuba zindijikele izinto ezimbi,
ezide azaba nakubalwa; Bundifikele ubugwenxa bam, andinakubukhangela;
Buninzi kuneenwele zentloko yam; Ndimkelwe yintliziyo.

<span id="an_40:13">40:13</span> Ngamana, Yehova, wandihlangula; Yehova,
wakhawuleza wandinceda!

<span id="an_40:14">40:14</span> Mabadane babe neentloni kuphele
Abazungula umphefumlo wam ukuze bawuphephethe; Mababuye muva bahlazeke

<span id="an_40:15">40:15</span> Mabamangaliswe ngumvuzo wehlazo labo
Abathi kum, Tshotsho! Tshotsho!

<span id="an_40:16">40:16</span> Mababe nemihlali bavuye ngawe bonke
abakufunayo, Abaluthandayo usindiso lwakho bahlale besithi, Makenziwe
mkhulu uYehova.

<span id="an_40:17">40:17</span> Mna ke ndilusizana, ndilihlwempu;
INkosi iya kundikhumbulela. Umncedi wam nomsindisi wam nguwe; Thixo wam,
musa ukulibala.

<span id="an_41:1">41:1</span> Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide. Hayi, uyolo
lwalowo unyamekela ihlwempu! Ngomhla wobubi uYehova uya kumhlangula.

<span id="an_41:2">41:2</span> UYehova uya kumlondoloza amgcine, aphile.
Kuya kuthiwa unoyolo yena ehlabathini; Ungamnikeli elitheni leentshaba
zakhe.

<span id="an_41:3">41:3</span> UYehova uya kumxhasa elukhukweni
lobulwelwe; Uya kuluguqula ukhuko lwakhe lonke esifeni sakhe.

<span id="an_41:4">41:4</span> Ndithi mna, Yehova, tarhu; Philisa
umphefumlo wam, ngokuba ndonile kuwe.

<span id="an_41:5">41:5</span> Iintshaba zam zithetha kakubi ngam;
Zithi, Uya kufa nini na, lidake igama lakhe?

<span id="an_41:6">41:6</span> Nothe weza kundilunguza, uthetha into
ekhohlakeleyo; Intliziyo yakhe ibutha ubutshinga; Uphuma phandle,
abuthethe.

<span id="an_41:7">41:7</span> Basebezelana ngam bonke abandithiyayo;
Bacinga ububi ngam.

<span id="an_41:8">41:8</span> Bathi, Unanyekwe bubutshijolo, Engoleleyo
nje, akayi kubuya avuke.

<span id="an_41:9">41:9</span> Kwanendoda ebixolelene nam, ebe
ndikholose ngayo, Ebisidla isonka sam, indiphakamisele isithende sayo.

<span id="an_41:10">41:10</span> Wena Yehova, ndibabale, undiphakamise,
Ndibabuyekeze.

<span id="an_41:11">41:11</span> Ndazi ngale nto, ukuba undinonelele,
Yokokuba lungenakundidumela utshaba lwam.

<span id="an_41:12">41:12</span> Mna ekugqibeleleni kwam uyandixhasa,
Undimisa phambi kwakho ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_41:13">41:13</span> Makabongwe uYehova, uThixo kaSirayeli,
kususela kwaphakade kude kuse ephakadeni. Amen, amen.

<span id="an_42:1">42:1</span> Kumongameli: eyokuqiqa; eyoonyana
bakaKora. Njengexhama elitsalela emifuleni yamanzi, Wenjenjalo
ukutsalela kuwe, Thixo, umphefumlo wam.

<span id="an_42:2">42:2</span> Umphefumlo wam unxanela uThixo, uThixo
ophilileyo; Ndiya kufika nini na, ndibonakale ebusweni bukaThixo?

<span id="an_42:3">42:3</span> Iinyembezi zam zaba kukudla kwam imini
nobusuku, Bakuthi kum imihla yonke, Uphi na uThixo wakho?

<span id="an_42:4">42:4</span> Ndikhumbula oku, ndiwuphalazela kum
umphefumlo wam, Ukuhamba kwam nezihlwele ndisiya endlwini kaThixo,
Sinezwi lokumemelela nokubulela, siyingxokolo evuyayo.

<span id="an_42:5">42:5</span> Kungani na ukuba usibekeke, mphefumlo
wam; Kungani na ukuba ugule ngaphakathi kwam? Lindela kuThixo, ngokuba
ndisaya kubuya ndibulele kuye, Olusindiso lobuso bam, noThixo wam.

<span id="an_42:6">42:6</span> Thixo wam, umphefumlo wam usibekekile
kum; ngenxa yoko ndikhumbula wena Ezweni laseYordan, nakweleHermon,
entabeni yeMitsare.

<span id="an_42:7">42:7</span> Amanzi anzongonzongo abiza amanzi
anzongonzongo ngesandi seengxangxasi zakho; Onke amaza akho alwayo,
amaza akho agugumayo, adlule phezu kwam.

<span id="an_42:8">42:8</span> Emini uYehova uya kuyiwisela umthetho
inceba yakhe, Nasebusuku ukuvuma ngaye kunam, Ukuthandaza kuThixo wobomi
bam.

<span id="an_42:9">42:9</span> Ndithi ke kuThixo oyingxondorha yam,
Undilibele ngani na? Ndihambelani na ngezimnyama zokuzila ngokuxina
kotshaba?

<span id="an_42:10">42:10</span> Ngento ephehlayo emathanjeni am,
bayandingcikiva abandibandezelayo, Ngokuthi kwabo kum imihla yonke, Uphi
na uThixo wakho?

<span id="an_42:11">42:11</span> Kungani na ukuba usibekeke, mphefumlo
wam; Kungani na ukuba ugule ngaphakathi kwam? Lindela kuThixo, ngokuba
ndisaya kubuya ndibulele kuye, Olusindiso lobuso bam, noThixo wam.

<span id="an_43:1">43:1</span> Lithethe ityala lam, Thixo, ubambane
ngenxa yam nohlanga olungenanceba; Ndisindise endodeni ekhohlisayo,
enobugqwetha.

<span id="an_43:2">43:2</span> Ngokuba unguThixo oyinqaba yam;
undihlambelani na? Ndihambelani na ngezimnyama zokuzila, ngokuxina
kotshaba?

<span id="an_43:3">43:3</span> Thuma ukukhanya kwakho nenyaniso yakho,
zindikhaphe, Zindise entabeni yakho engcwele, Naseminqubeni yakho.

<span id="an_43:4">43:4</span> Ndoya ke esibingelelweni sikaThixo,
KuThixo wovuyo lwam olugcobayo, Ndibulele kuwe ngohadi, Thixo onguThixo
wam.

<span id="an_43:5">43:5</span> Kungani na ukuba usibekeke, mphefumlo
wam? Kungani na ukuba ugule ngaphakathi kwam? Lindela kuThixo, ngokuba
ndisaya kubuya ndibulele kuye, Olusindiso lobuso bam, noThixo wam.

<span id="an_44:1">44:1</span> Kumongameli: eyoonyana bakaKora:
eyokuqiqa. Thixo, sivile ngeendlebe zethu, oobawo basibalisela,
Ngomsebenzi owawenza ngemihla yabo, ngemihla yamandulo:

<span id="an_44:2">44:2</span> Okokuba isandla sakho sagqogqa iintlanga,
sabatyala bona; Saviva izizwe, sabanabisa bona.

<span id="an_44:3">44:3</span> Ngokuba abalihluthanga ilizwe ngekrele
labo, Abazisindisanga ngengalo yabo; Sisandla sakho sokunene, nengalo
yakho, nokukhanya kobuso bakho; Ngokuba wawunesisa kubo.

<span id="an_44:4">44:4</span> Wena unguKumkani wam, Thixo; Yitsho
lubekho usindiso kuYakobi.

<span id="an_44:5">44:5</span> Ngawe sobangqula abasibandezelayo;
Egameni lakho sobagqusha abasukela phezulu kuthi.

<span id="an_44:6">44:6</span> Ngokuba andikholose ngasaphetha sam;
Andisindiswa ngakrele lam.

<span id="an_44:7">44:7</span> Hayi! Nguwe osisindisayo
kwabasibandezelayo, Ubadanise abasithiyileyo.

<span id="an_44:8">44:8</span> NgoThixo sidumisa imihla yonke, Sibulele
kwigama lakho ngonaphakade. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_44:9">44:9</span> Noko ke usihlambile, usihlazile,
Akwaphuma nemikhosi yethu.

<span id="an_44:10">44:10</span> Usibuyise umva phambi kombandezeli;
Abasithiyileyo basiphangile okwabo.

<span id="an_44:11">44:11</span> Wasinikela njengeegusha ezidliwayo;
Wasichitha-chitha ezintlangeni;

<span id="an_44:12">44:12</span> Wathengisa ngabantu bakho, akwazuza,
