Akwalinyusa ixabiso labo.

<span id="an_44:13">44:13</span> Wasenza isingcikivo kubamelwane bethu,
Isigculelo nesicukucezo kwabasijikelezileyo.

<span id="an_44:14">44:14</span> Wasenza umzekelo ezintlangeni,
Abokuhlunguzelelwa intloko ezizweni.

<span id="an_44:15">44:15</span> Yonke imihla ihlazo lam liphambi kwam,
Nokudana kobuso bam kundigubungele,

<span id="an_44:16">44:16</span> Ngenxa yezwi lomngcikivi nomnyelisi,
Ngenxa yokukhangela kotshaba nomphindezeli.

<span id="an_44:17">44:17</span> Oko konke kusifikele, asikulibalanga
wena, Asixokanga emnqophisweni wakho;

<span id="an_44:18">44:18</span> Ayibuyanga umva intliziyo yethu,
Ukunyathela kwethu akuthanga gu bucala emendweni wakho;

<span id="an_44:19">44:19</span> Ukuba usityumze endaweni yeempungutye,
Usigubungele ngethunzi lokufa.

<span id="an_44:20">44:20</span> Ukuba besililibele igama loThixo wethu,
Sazolulela kuthixo wasemzini izandla zethu,

<span id="an_44:21">44:21</span> Ubengayi kuyigoca-goca na uThixo loo
nto, Ngokuba ezazi iindawo ezifihlakeleyo zentliziyo?

<span id="an_44:22">44:22</span> Hayi, Ngenxa yakho sibulawa imihla
yonke; Kuthiwa siziigusha zokuxhelwa.

<span id="an_44:23">44:23</span> Vuka, ulaleleni na, Nkosi yam? Qabuka,
ungasihlambi kuphele.

<span id="an_44:24">44:24</span> Ubusitheliselani na ubuso bakho,
Ukulibale ukucinezelwa kwethu, nokuxinwa kwethu?

<span id="an_44:25">44:25</span> Ngokuba usibekeke eluthulini umphefumlo
wethu, Sanamathela emhlabeni isisu sethu.

<span id="an_44:26">44:26</span> Khawusuk’ ume usincede, Usikhulule
ngenxa yenceba yakho.

<span id="an_45:1">45:1</span> Kumongameli: ngeyeenyibiba. Eyoonyana
bakaKora; eyokuqiqa. Ingoma yeentanda. Intliziyo yam iphuphuma ilizwi
elihle, Ndisithi, Into endiyenzayo isingise kukumkani; Ulwimi lwam
lusiba lombhali okhawulezayo.

<span id="an_45:2">45:2</span> Umhle wamhle ngaphezu koonyana babantu;
Kugalelwe ubumnandi emlonyeni wakho; Ngenxa yoko ukusikelele uThixo
wakho ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_45:3">45:3</span> Bhinqa ikrele lakho ethangeni, gorha,
Bhinqa indili yakho nobungangamela bakho.

<span id="an_45:4">45:4</span> Tyhudisa, ukhwele uhambe, unobungangamela
bakho, Ngenxa yenyaniso, nolulamo olunobulungisa. Sikuyale ngezinto
ezoyikekayo isandla sakho sokunene.

<span id="an_45:5">45:5</span> Iintolo zakho zitsolile; Kuya kuwa izizwe
phantsi kwakho; Zitsolile entliziyweni yeentshaba zokumkani.

<span id="an_45:6">45:6</span> Itrone yakho, itrone kaThixo,
ingunaphakade kanaphakade; Yintonga ethe tye intonga yobukumkani bakho.

<span id="an_45:7">45:7</span> Uthanda ubulungisa, uthiye okungendawo;
Ngenxa yoko ukuthambisile uThixo, uThixo wakho, Ngeoli yemihlali
ngaphezu kwabalingane bakho.

<span id="an_45:8">45:8</span> Ziyimore nehaloti nekasiya iingubo zakho
zonke; Emabhotweni eempondo zeendlovu uhadi lukuvuyisile.

<span id="an_45:9">45:9</span> Kukho iintombi zokumkani phakathi
kwabathandekayo bakho; Ukumkanikazi umi ngasekunene kwakho, Enxibe
igolide ecikizekileyo yakwaOfire.

<span id="an_45:10">45:10</span> Yiva, ntombi, ubone, uthobe indlebe
yakho, Ubalibale abantu bakowenu, nendlu kayihlo;

<span id="an_45:11">45:11</span> Akubunqwenela ubunzwakazi bakho
ukumkani, Woqubuda kuye, ngokuba eyinkosi yakho.

<span id="an_45:12">45:12</span> Intombi enguTire, izityebi zabantu,
Ziya kukuncekelela ngomnikelo.

<span id="an_45:13">45:13</span> Bubuyokoyoko bodwa intombi yokumkani
kweliphakathi igumbi. Isambatho sayo sesilukwe igolide.

<span id="an_45:14">45:14</span> Isiwa kukumkani ineengubo
ezimfakamfele; Ziyilandela iintombi ezingowayo, Zisiwa kuwe,

<span id="an_45:15">45:15</span> Zisiwa ngovuyo nangomgcobo, Zingene
ebhotweni lokumkani.

<span id="an_45:16">45:16</span> Endaweni yooyihlo iya kuba ngoonyana
bakho; Uya kubamisa babe ngabathetheli ehlabathini lonke.

<span id="an_45:17">45:17</span> Ndiya kulikhankanya igama lakho
kwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana zonke; Ngenxa yoko izizwe ziya kubulela
kuwe ngonaphakade kanaphakade.

<span id="an_46:1">46:1</span> Kumongameli: eyoonyana bakaKora;
ngeyeentombi. Ingoma. UThixo ulihlathi, uligwiba kuthi; Ezimbandezelweni
ufumaneke eluncedo kunene.

<span id="an_46:2">46:2</span> Ngenxa yoko asoyiki ekuphendukeni
kwehlabathi, Ekudilikeleni kweentaba esazulwini solwandle.

<span id="an_46:3">46:3</span> Makagqume alephuze amanzi alo, Iintaba
zinyikime ngokukratsha kwalo. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_46:4">46:4</span> Kukho umlambo ozibhaxa zivuyisa umzi
kaThixo, Ingcwele yeminquba yOsenyangweni.

<span id="an_46:5">46:5</span> UThixo uphakathi kwawo, awushukunyiswa;
UThixo uyawunceda kwasekuzeni kokusa.

<span id="an_46:6">46:6</span> Ziyaxokozela iintlanga, ziyashukuma
izikumkani: Ukhupha izwi lakhe, linyibilike ihlabathi.

<span id="an_46:7">46:7</span> UYehova wemikhosi unathi, Ingxonde yethu
nguThixo kaYakobi. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_46:8">46:8</span> Yizani nikhangele imisebenzi kaYehova:
Owenze iziphanziso ehlabathini;

<span id="an_46:9">46:9</span> Ulophelisa iimfazwe kude kuse eziphelweni
zehlabathi; Waphula isaphetha, angqumze umkhonto, Atshise iinqwelo
zokulwa ngomlilo.

<span id="an_46:10">46:10</span> Yekani, nazi ukuba ndinguThixo mna.
Ndiya kuphakanyiswa ezintlangeni, ndiya kuphakanyiswa ehlabathini.

<span id="an_46:11">46:11</span> UYehova wemikhosi unathi, Ingxonde
yethu nguThixo kaYakobi. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_47:1">47:1</span> Kumongameli; eyoonyana bakaKora. Umhobe.
Nonke zizwe, bethani izandla, Dumani kuThixo ngezwi lokumemelela.

<span id="an_47:2">47:2</span> Ngokuba uYehova Osenyangweni uyoyikeka;
Ngukumkani omkhulu ehlabathini lonke.

<span id="an_47:3">47:3</span> Uzikhandanisela phantsi kwethu izizwe,
Izizwe phantsi kweenyawo zethu.

<span id="an_47:4">47:4</span> Usinyulela ilifa lethu, Iqhayiya
likaYakobi awamthandayo. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_47:5">47:5</span> UThixo unyukile, kudunywa; Unyukile
uYehova, kuhlokoma isigodlo.

<span id="an_47:6">47:6</span> Mbetheleni uhadi uThixo, mbetheleni,
Mbetheleni uhadi uKumkani wethu, mbetheleni!

<span id="an_47:7">47:7</span> Ngokuba uKumkani wehlabathi lonke
nguThixo; Mbetheleni ngeyokuqiqa.

<span id="an_47:8">47:8</span> UThixo nguKumkani weentlanga; UThixo
uhleli etroneni yakhe engcwele.

<span id="an_47:9">47:9</span> Amanene ezizwe ahlanganisene, Abantu
boThixo ka-Abraham; Ngokuba iingweletshetshe zehlabathi zezikaThixo;
Unyusiwe kakhulu yena.

<span id="an_48:1">48:1</span> Ingoma. Umhobe. Eyoonyana babaKora.
Mkhulu uYehova, engowokudunyiswa kunene Emzini kaThixo wethu, entabeni
yakhe engcwele.

<span id="an_48:2">48:2</span> Intle ukuphakama kwayo, yimihlali yehla
bathi lonke Intaba yaseZiyon, intlomo yasentla, Umzi woKumkani omkhulu.

<span id="an_48:3">48:3</span> UThixo, ezingxandeni zawo ezinde, Wazelwa
ukuba yingxonde.

<span id="an_48:4">48:4</span> Kuba nabo ookumkani babenqophisene,
Bawela beza kunye;

<span id="an_48:5">48:5</span> Bakuthi ukubona, abakhuluma; Bakhwankqa,
babaleka buphuthuphuthu;

<span id="an_48:6">48:6</span> Babanjwa khona kukuthuthumela,
Kukuzibhijabhija njengozalayo.

<span id="an_48:7">48:7</span> Ngomoya wasempumalanga Uyazivitha
iinqanawa zaseTarshishe.

<span id="an_48:8">48:8</span> Njengoko sikuvileyo, sibone kunjalo
Emzini kaYehova wemikhosi, emzini kaThixo wethu: UThixo uyawuzinzisa
ngonaphakade. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_48:9">48:9</span> Sayikhumbula, Thixo, inceba yakho
Phakathi kwetempile yakho.

<span id="an_48:10">48:10</span> Njengoko linjalo igama lakho, Thixo,
Lunjalo udumiso lwakho, Kwesa eziphelweni zehlabathi; Isandla sakho
sokunene sizele bubulungisa.

<span id="an_48:11">48:11</span> Mayivuye intaba yaseZiyon, Agcobe
amagxamesi akwaYuda, Ngenxa yezigwebo zakho.

<span id="an_48:12">48:12</span> Yijikelezeni iZiyon, niyizunguleze;
Zibaleni iinqaba zayo ezinde.

<span id="an_48:13">48:13</span> Gqalani ungqameko lomsele wayo; Candani
ezingxandeni zayo ezinde; Ukuze nibalisele isizukulwana esizayo,

<span id="an_48:14">48:14</span> Ukuba lo Thixo nguThixo wethu
ngonaphakade kanaphakade, Yena uya kusikhapha kude kuse ekufeni.

<span id="an_49:1">49:1</span> Kumongameli: eyoonyana bakaKora. Umhobe.
Yivani oku, nina nonke zizwe; Bekani indlebe, nina nonke, bemi beli
phakade,

<span id="an_49:2">49:2</span> Nina nyana boluntu, nani nyana bamadoda,
Nina zityebi, nani mahlwempu kunye.

<span id="an_49:3">49:3</span> Umlomo wam uza kuthetha ubulumko;
Nokucamanga kwentliziyo yam kukuqonda.

<span id="an_49:4">49:4</span> Ndiya kuyithobela emzekelisweni indlebe
yam, Ndiya kuyivulela ngohadi intsonkotha yam.

<span id="an_49:5">49:5</span> Ndoyikelani na emihleni yobubi, Xa
ubugwenxa babandibambisayo bundijikelayo?

<span id="an_49:6">49:6</span> Abo bakholose ngemfuyo yabo, Baqhayisa
ngobuninzi bobutyebi babo.

<span id="an_49:7">49:7</span> Akukho bani unokukhulula umzalwana;
Akanakumnika uThixo isicamagusho ngaye

<span id="an_49:8">49:8</span> (Sinqabile isikhululo somphefumlo wabo,
Masincanywe ngonaphakade),

<span id="an_49:9">49:9</span> Sokuba ahlale esidla ubomi ngamaxesha
onke, Angasiboni isihogo.

<span id="an_49:10">49:10</span> Ngokuba ubona izilumko zibhubha, Bedaka
kunye abanyabileyo nezityhakala, Bayishiye nabanye imfuyo yabo.

<span id="an_49:11">49:11</span> Imbilini yabo ithi izindlu zabo
zingunaphakade. Iminquba yabo ikwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana; Bayithiya
imihlaba yabo ngamagama abo.

<span id="an_49:12">49:12</span> Ke umntu enobuhandiba akanakuhlala,
Ufana neenkomo ezi zitshabalalayo.

<span id="an_49:13">49:13</span> Yiyo le indlela yabanyabileyo, Neyabo
babalandelayo, bekholiswa ngumlomo wabo. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_49:14">49:14</span> Babuthe ngokweegusha kwelabafileyo;
Ukufa kuyabalusa; Abathe tye bayabanyathela kwakusa; Isithomo sabo abo
siyonakala kwelabafileyo, singabi nandawo yakuhlala.

<span id="an_49:15">49:15</span> Kodwa uThixo uya kuwukhulula umphefumlo
wam esandleni selabafileyo, Ngokuba eya kundithabatha. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_49:16">49:16</span> Musa ukoyika, yakuba sisityebi indoda,
Bakwanda ubuqaqawuli bendlu yayo:

<span id="an_49:17">49:17</span> Ngokuba ekufeni kwayo ayiyi kuthabatha
nento, Aluyi kuhla emva kwayo uzuko lwayo.

<span id="an_49:18">49:18</span> Nakuba umntu ekudleni kwakhe ubomi
ebewusikelela umphefumlo wakhe, Bekudumisa ngokuzichwayithisa kwakho,

<span id="an_49:19">49:19</span> Uya kuya noko esizukulwaneni sooyise;
Abayikukubona ukukhanya naphakade.

<span id="an_49:20">49:20</span> Ke umntu onobuhandiba, abe engaqondi,
Ufana neenkomo ezi zitshabalalayo.

<span id="an_50:1">50:1</span> Umhobe ka-Asafu. UThixo, uThixo uYehova
uyathetha; Uyalibiza ihlabathi, ethabathela ekuphumeni kwelanga esisa
ekutshoneni kwalo.

<span id="an_50:2">50:2</span> EZiyon, ukuphela kweenzwana, Uyakhazimla
uThixo.

<span id="an_50:3">50:3</span> Uyeza uThixo wethu, akayi kuthi cwaka.
Kudla umlilo phambi kwakhe, Ngeenxa zonke kuye sisaqhwithi esikhulu.

<span id="an_50:4">50:4</span> Ubiza izulu phezulu, Nehlabathi, ukuba
agwebe phakathi kwabantu bakhe.

<span id="an_50:5">50:5</span> Uthi, Bahlanganiseleni kum abam benceba,
Abenze umnqophiso nam ngombingelelo.

<span id="an_50:6">50:6</span> Izulu lixela ubulungisa bakhe, Ngokuba
uThixo eza kugweba yena. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_50:7">50:7</span> Yivani, bantu bam, ndithethe; Sirayeli,
ndiqononondise kuwe; NdinguThixo, uThixo wakho.

<span id="an_50:8">50:8</span> Andikohlwayi ngenxa yemibingelelo yakho,
Namadini akho anyukayo aphambi kwam amaxesha onke.

<span id="an_50:9">50:9</span> Andiyi kuthabatha zinkunzi zankomo
endlwini yakho, Nazinkunzi zabhokhwe esibayeni sakho.

<span id="an_50:10">50:10</span> Ngokuba zezam zonke iinyamakazi
zehlathi, Neenkomo ezisezintabeni eziliwaka.

<span id="an_50:11">50:11</span> Iintaka zonke zasezintabeni ndiyazazi,
Nento edakasa endle inam.

<span id="an_50:12">50:12</span> Ukuba bendilambile, ndibe ndingayi
kukuxelela; Ngokuba lelam elimiweyo nenzaliseko yalo.

<span id="an_50:13">50:13</span> Ndidle inyama yeenkunzi eziziimbalasane
na? Ndisele igazi leenkunzi zeebhokhwe na?

<span id="an_50:14">50:14</span> Bingelela kuYehova umbulelo, Uzizalise
kOsenyangweni izibhambathiso zakho;

<span id="an_50:15">50:15</span> Ubize mna ngemini yembandezelo,
Ndikuhlangule, undizukise.

<span id="an_50:16">50:16</span> Ke kongendawo uthi uThixo, Useke phi na
wena ukuxela ummiselo wam, Uwuphathe ngomlomo wakho umnqophiso wam,

<span id="an_50:17">50:17</span> Uyithiyile nje intethiso wena, Uwaphose
nje amazwi am emva kwakho?

<span id="an_50:18">50:18</span> Xa ubona isela, ukholana nalo, Wabelane
nabakrexezi.

<span id="an_50:19">50:19</span> Umlomo wakho uwuyekela ebubini; Ulwimi
lwakho luthungela inkohliso;

<span id="an_50:20">50:20</span> Uthi uhlale uthethe ngomzalwana wakho,
Uhlaze umntwana kanyoko.

<span id="an_50:21">50:21</span> Uzenzile ezo nto, ndathi tu, Waba
ndinjengawe. Ndiya kukohlwaya ndizicwangcise emehlweni akho.

<span id="an_50:22">50:22</span> Khaniqonde ke oko, nina bamlibalayo
uThixo, Hleze ndiqwenge, kungabikho uhlangulayo.

<span id="an_50:23">50:23</span> Obingelela umbulelo uyandizukisa,
Alungise indlela, Endombonisa kuyo usindiso lukaThixo.

<span id="an_51:1">51:1</span> Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide: ekuzeni
kukaNatan umprofeti kuye, emveni kokuba ebengene uBhatshebha. Tarhu,
Thixo, ngokwenceba yakho! Ngokobuninzi benceba yakho, cima ukreqo lwam!

<span id="an_51:2">51:2</span> Nd’ixovule kunene, busuke ubugwenxa bam,
Undihlambulule esonweni sam.

<span id="an_51:3">51:3</span> Ngokuba ndiyalwazi mna ukreqo lwam,
Nesono sam siphambi kwam ngamaxesha onke.

<span id="an_51:4">51:4</span> Ndonile kuwe, kuwe wedwa, Ndenza okubi
emehlweni akho; Ukuze ube lilungisa ekuthetheni kwakho, Ucace ekugwebeni
kwakho.

<span id="an_51:5">51:5</span> Uyabona, ndizalelwe ebugwenxeni,
Ndakhawulwa nguma esonweni.

<span id="an_51:6">51:6</span> Uyabona, ufuna inyaniso ezintsweni,
Esitheni undazisa ubulumko.

<span id="an_51:7">51:7</span> Ndihlambulule isono ngehisope,
ndihlambuluke; Ndixovule, ndibe mhlophe kunekhephu;

<span id="an_51:8">51:8</span> Ndivise imihlali nemivuyo, Agcobe
amathambo owacolileyo.

<span id="an_51:9">51:9</span> Sithelisa ubuso bakho ezonweni zam,
Ubucime bonke ubugwenxa bam.

<span id="an_51:10">51:10</span> Dala phakathi kwam, Thixo, intliziyo
ehlambulukileyo, Uhlaziye umoya oqinisekileyo phakathi kwam.

<span id="an_51:11">51:11</span> Musa ukundilahla ebusweni bakho, UMoya
wakho oyiNgcwele ungamsusi kum.

<span id="an_51:12">51:12</span> Buyisela kum imihlali yosindiso lwakho,
Undixhase ngomoya wentumekelelo.

<span id="an_51:13">51:13</span> Ndobafundisa abangendawo iindlela
zakho, Babuyele kuwe aboni.

<span id="an_51:14">51:14</span> Ndihlangule emagazini, Thixo, Thixo
ondisindisayo; Lomemelela ngobulungisa bakho ulwimi lwam.

<span id="an_51:15">51:15</span> Nkosi yam, vula imilebe yomlomo wam,
Uyixele indumiso yakho umlomo wam.

<span id="an_51:16">51:16</span> Ngokuba akunanze mibingelelo, bendiya
kukunika; Akalikholo kuwe amadini anyukayo.

<span id="an_51:17">51:17</span> Imibingelelo kaThixo ngumoya
owaphukileyo, Intliziyo eyaphukileyo, etyumkileyo, Thixo, akuyi
kuyidela.

<span id="an_51:18">51:18</span> Yenzele okulungileyo iZiyon
ngokukholekileyo kuwe; Yakha iindonga zeYerusalem.

<span id="an_51:19">51:19</span> Kuya kwandula ukuba mnandi kuwe
imibingelelo yobulungisa, amadini apheleleyo; Ziya kwandula ukunyuswa
iinkunzi ezintsha zeenkomo esibingelelweni sakho.

<span id="an_52:1">52:1</span> Kumongameli. Eyokuqiqa: ekaDavide: oko
uDowegi umEdom waya waxelela uSawule, wathi kuye, UDavide ungene
endlwini ka-Ahimeleki. Uqhayiselani na ngobubi, wena gorha? Inceba
kaThixo ikho imihla yonke.

<span id="an_52:2">52:2</span> Ulwimi lwakho lucinga ukweyelisela,
Njengesitshetshe sokuguya iindevu esiloliweyo, wena mkhohlisi.

<span id="an_52:3">52:3</span> Uthanda okubi kunokulungileyo; Ubuxoki,
kunokuthetha ubulungisa. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_52:4">52:4</span> Uthanda onke amazwi aginyayo,
Lulwimindini lukhohlisayo.

<span id="an_52:5">52:5</span> Naye uThixo uya kukudiliza kuphele; Uva
kukuxwila, akuncothule ententeni, Akudonyule ezweni labaphilileyo.
(Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_52:6">52:6</span> Obona amalungisa, oyike, Amhleke, athi,

<span id="an_52:7">52:7</span> Nanko umfo ongamenzanga igwiba lakhe
uThixo, Owakholosa ngobuninzi bobutyebi bakhe, Waba nengcwangu
ekweyeliseleni kwakhe.

<span id="an_52:8">52:8</span> Ke mna ndinjengomnquma oluhlaza endlwini
kaThixo; Ndikholose ngenceba kaThixo ngonaphakade kanaphakade.

<span id="an_52:9">52:9</span> Ndiya kubulela kuwe ngonaphakade, kuba
ukwenzile oku; Ndiya kuthemba igama lakho, ngokuba lilungile, phambi
kwabenceba bakho.

<span id="an_53:1">53:1</span> Kumongameli: ngeyokhuzo. Eyokuqiqa;
ekaDavide. Sithi isidenge entliziyweni yaso, Akukho Thixo. Bonakalisile,
balisikizi ngobugqwetha babo; Akukho wenza okulungileyo.

<span id="an_53:2">53:2</span> UThixo esemazulwini uqondele koonyana
babantu, Ukubona ukuba ukho na oqiqayo, Ofuna uThixo.

<span id="an_53:3">53:3</span> Bonke babuye umva, bayimbozisa bephelele;
Akukho wenza okulungileyo, Akukho nokuba abe mnye.

<span id="an_53:4">53:4</span> Abanakwazi na abasebenzi bobutshinga,
Abathi, bebadla abantu bam, bathi badla isonka, Bangamnquli uThixo?

<span id="an_53:5">53:5</span> Apho bankwantya benkwantyile, phofu
kungekho nto inkwantyisayo; Ngokuba uThixo wawathi saa amathambo
omngqingi wakho; Wabadanisa, ngokuba uThixo ebebacekisile.

<span id="an_53:6">53:6</span> Akwaba bekuvela eZiyon ukusindiswa
kwamaSirayeli! Ekubuyiseni kukaThixo abantu bakhe ekuthinjweni, Wogcoba
uYakobi, avuye uSirayeli.

<span id="an_54:1">54:1</span> Eyokubethelwa ngezinto ezineentambo.
Kumongameli. Eyokuqiqa. EkaDavide: ekufikeni kwabaseZifi, bathi
kuSawule, UDavide akazimele phakathi kwethu na? Thixo, ndisindise
ngegama lakho, Uligwebe ityala lam ngobugorha bakho.

<span id="an_54:2">54:2</span> Thixo, yiva umthandazo wam; Wabekele
indlebe amazwi omlomo wam.

<span id="an_54:3">54:3</span> Ngokuba abasemzini basukela phezulu kum,
Nabanobungqwangangqwili bafuna umphefumlo wam; Abammisi uThixo phambi
kwabo. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_54:4">54:4</span> Yabona, uThixo ngumncedi wam; INkosi yam
ikwabasekela umphefumlo wam.

<span id="an_54:5">54:5</span> Uya kubuyisela ububi kwabandilalelayo;
Ngenyaniso yakho babhangise.

<span id="an_54:6">54:6</span> Ndiya kubingelela kuwe ngokuqhutywa
yintliziyo; Ndiya kubulela kwigama lakho, Yehova, kuba lilungile.

<span id="an_54:7">54:7</span> Ngokuba lindihlangule embandezelweni
yonke; Iliso lam libonela iintshaba zam.

<span id="an_55:1">55:1</span> Kumongameli. Eyokubethelwa ngezinto
ezineentambo. Eyokuqiqa: ekaDavide. Wubekele indlebe umthandazo wam,
Thixo, Musa ukuzifihla esikhungweni sam.

<span id="an_55:2">55:2</span> Ndibazele indlebe undiphendule.
Ndiyaphaphatheka ekucamngceni kwam, ndincwine,

<span id="an_55:3">55:3</span> Ngenxa yelizwi lotshaba, Ngenxa
yokuxinzelelwa phantsi ngabangendawo; Ngokuba zindiqengqela ubutshinga,
Ziyandisukela ngomsindo.

<span id="an_55:4">55:4</span> Intliziyo yam iyazibhija-bhija phakathi
kwam; Izothuso zokufa zindiwele.

<span id="an_55:5">55:5</span> Ukoyika nokuthuthumela kundingene;
Ndigutyungelwe kukududuzela.

<span id="an_55:6">55:6</span> Ndathi, Andaba bendinamaphiko njengehobe!
Bendiya kubaleka ndiye ndihlale!

<span id="an_55:7">55:7</span> Nanko ndibalekela kude, Ndilalise
entlango. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_55:8">55:8</span> Bendiya kukhawuleza, ndisinde Emoyeni
ovuthuzayo naseluqhwitheleni.

<span id="an_55:9">55:9</span> Tshabalalisa, Nkosi yam, yahlula ulwimi
lwazo; Ngokuba ndibone ukugonyamela nokubambana phakathi komzi.

<span id="an_55:10">55:10</span> Imini nobusuku bajikeleza ezindongeni
zawo; Ubutshinga nokwaphula kuphakathi kwawo;

<span id="an_55:11">55:11</span> Ukweyelisela kuphakathi kwawo; Endaweni
yembutho yawo akusuki ukuxinezela nokukhohlisa.

<span id="an_55:12">55:12</span> Ngokuba asilutshaba olu
lundingcikivayo; Bendiya kukuthwala oko. Asingondithiyileyo lo
uzikhulisayo kum; Bendiya kusithela kuye.

<span id="an_55:13">55:13</span> Nguwe, mntu ubungumlingane wam,
Ikholwane lam endazana nalo,

<span id="an_55:14">55:14</span> Ebesicweya kamnandi, Siye endlwini
kaThixo silihlokondiba eligcobayo.

<span id="an_55:15">55:15</span> Ukufa makubaqubule, Mabehle baye
kwelabafileyo besaphilile; Ngokuba ububi busemizini yabo phakathi kwabo.

<span id="an_55:16">55:16</span> Mna ndinqula uThixo; UYehova uya
kundisindisa.

<span id="an_55:17">55:17</span> Ngokuhlwa, nakusasa, nasemini enkulu
ndiya kucamngca, ndincwine; Uya kuliva izwi lam.

<span id="an_55:18">55:18</span> Uwukhulula umphefumlo wam unoxolo,
ukuze bangasondeli kum, Ngokuba baninzi abandichasayo.

<span id="an_55:19">55:19</span> UThixo uya kuva, abaphendule,
Uselokwamandulo ehleli, (Phakamisani.) Abo bangenanguquko, Bangamoyikiyo
uThixo.

<span id="an_55:20">55:20</span> Babasa isandla abaxolelene nabo;
Bahlambela umnqophiso wabo;

<span id="an_55:21">55:21</span> Ubuthelezi njengamasi umlomo wabo, Ke
yimfazwe intliziyo yabo. Athambile amazwi abongaphezu kweoli, Kanti
aziintlangothi zekrele.

<span id="an_55:22">55:22</span> Umthwalo wakho wulahlele kuYehova; yena
wokuzimasa; Akayi kuliyekela ilungisa lishukunyiswe naphakade.

<span id="an_55:23">55:23</span> Wena ke, Thixo, uya kubahlisela
emngxunyeni wesihogo. Abantu bamagazi nenkohliso abayi kuyiqingathisa
imihla yabo; Ke mna ndikholose ngawe.

<span id="an_56:1">56:1</span> Kumongameli; ngeyehobe elithe cwaka
phakathi kwabakude. EkaDavide. Eliligugu. Ukubanjwa kwakhe ngamaFilisti
eGati. Ndibabale, Thixo, ngokuba abantu bendizonda; Bandixinile, besilwa
yonke imini;

<span id="an_56:2">56:2</span> Abandilalelayo bandizonda yonke imini,
Ngokuba baninzi abalwa nam beziphakamisile.

<span id="an_56:3">56:3</span> Mhlana ndinxunguphalayo mna, Ndokholosa
ngawe.

<span id="an_56:4">56:4</span> Ndiya kulidumisa ngoThixo ilizwi lakhe,
Ndikholose ngoThixo, ndingoyiki; Inokundenza ntoni na inyama?

<span id="an_56:5">56:5</span> Yonke imini bayawaphambanisa amazwi am;
Zingam zonke iingcinga zabo zobubi.

<span id="an_56:6">56:6</span> Baqukene, babonisele, Bona bagcine
izithende zam, Ngokokuba belinde umphefumlo wam.

<span id="an_56:7">56:7</span> Bengamatshinga nje, bosinda na? Zihlise
ngomsindo izizwe, Thixo.

<span id="an_56:8">56:8</span> Ukuphalaphala kwam ukubhalile wena; Yitha
iinyembezi zam entsubeni yakho; Azisencwadini yakho na?

<span id="an_56:9">56:9</span> Ziya kubuya umva ke iintshaba zam, mhlana
ndibizayo; Ndiyakwazi oku, ukuba uThixo unam.

<span id="an_56:10">56:10</span> Ndilidumisa ngoThixo ilizwi,
Ndilidumisa ngoYehova ilizwi.

<span id="an_56:11">56:11</span> Ndikholose ngoThixo, ndingoyiki;
Unokundenza ntoni na umntu?

<span id="an_56:12">56:12</span> Ziphezu kwam, Thixo, izibhambathiso
zakho; Ndiya kuyizalisa kuwe imibingelelo yombulelo.

<span id="an_56:13">56:13</span> Ngokuba uwuhlangule ekufeni umphefumlo
wam, Iinyawo zam ekukhubekeni, Ukuba ndihambe phambi koThixo Ekukhanyeni
kobomi.

<span id="an_57:1">57:1</span> Kumongameli; ngethi, Ungonakalisi.
EkaDavide. Eliligugu: ekumbalekeni kwakhe uSawule emqolombeni.
Ndibabale, Thixo, ndibabale; Ngokuba uzimela ngawe umphefumlo wam;
Ndizimela esithunzini samaphiko akho, Kude kudlule inkxwaleko.

<span id="an_57:2">57:2</span> Ndinqula uThixo Osenyangweni, UThixo
ondifezelayo.

<span id="an_57:3">57:3</span> Uya kuthuma esemazulwini andisindise,
Emngcikiva nje ondizondayo; (Phakamisani.) UThixo uya kuthuma inceba
yakhe nenyaniso yakhe.

<span id="an_57:4">57:4</span> Umphefumlo wam uphakathi kweengonyama;
Ndiya kulala phantsi nabafutha umlilo, Oonyana babantu abamazinyo
aziintshuntshe neentolo, Ulwimi lwabo lulikrele elibukhali.

<span id="an_57:5">57:5</span> Ziphakamisele ngaphezu kwamazulu, Thixo,
Lube phezu kwehlabathi lonke uzuko lwakho.

<span id="an_57:6">57:6</span> Isibatha basilungisele iinyawo zam;
Bawugobile umphefumlo wam; Bandimbela isihogo, Beyela kuso ngokwabo.
(Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_57:7">57:7</span> Izimasekile intliziyo yam, Thixo,
izimasekile intliziyo yam; Ndiya kuvuma, ndiya kubetha uhadi.

<span id="an_57:8">57:8</span> Vuka, luzuko lwam! Vukani, mrhubhe
nohadi! Ndiya kusiphangela isifingo.

<span id="an_57:9">57:9</span> Ndiya kubulela kuwe phakathi kwezizwe,
Nkosi yam; Ndiya kukubethela uhadi phakathi kwezizwe.

<span id="an_57:10">57:10</span> Ngokuba inkulu, yada yaya ezulwini,
inceba yakho; Yada yesa esibhakabhakeni inyaniso yakho.

<span id="an_57:11">57:11</span> Ziphakamisele ngaphezu kwezulu, Thixo,
Lube phezu kwehlabathi lonke uzuko lwakho.

<span id="an_58:1">58:1</span> Kumongameli; ngethi, Ungonakalisi.
EkaDavide. Eliligugu. Yinene na kodwa ukuba nithetha ubulungisa, nina
bothixo? Nigweba oonyana babantu ngokuthe tye?

<span id="an_58:2">58:2</span> Hayi, entliziyweni nenza ngobugqwetha;
Ezweni nilinganisela ukugonyamela kwezandla zenu.

<span id="an_58:3">58:3</span> Abangendawo baphambukile kwasesizalweni;
Bandwendwile kwasesiswini abathethi bamanga.

<span id="an_58:4">58:4</span> Banobuhlungu obunjengobuhlungu benyoka,
Njengephimpi elizenza isithulu, elivingca indlebe yalo;

<span id="an_58:5">58:5</span> Ukuze lingaliva izwi labanyangi,
Lababopha ngomabophe, beziingcibi.

<span id="an_58:6">58:6</span> Thixo, yaphula amazinyo abo emlonyeni
wabo; Amabamba eengonyama ezintsha wavithe, Yehova.

<span id="an_58:7">58:7</span> Mabaphalale njengamanzi equkuqela;
Akuxuna iintolo zakhe, mazinge zicutshiwe.

<span id="an_58:8">58:8</span> Mababe njengenkumba ehamba inyibilika,
Njengemva-mbilini yomfazi, engalibonanga ilanga.

<span id="an_58:9">58:9</span> Zingekaziva iintsasa iimbiza zenu, Nokuba
ikrwada inyama, nokuba iza kuvuthwa, uyayiqweqwedisa.

<span id="an_58:10">58:10</span> Liya kuvuya ilungisa, lakuyibona
impindezelo; Liya kuzihlamba iinyawo zalo egazini longendawo,

<span id="an_58:11">58:11</span> Athi umntu, Inene, ilungisa
linesiqhamo; Inene, ukho uThixo ogwebayo ehlabathini.

<span id="an_59:1">59:1</span> Kumongameli; ngethi, Ungonakalisi.
EkaDavide. Eliligugu: ekuthumeleni kukaSawule, bayilinda indlu ukuba
bambulale. Ndihlangule ezintshabeni zam, Thixo wam, Ndise engxondeni
kwabasukela phezulu kum.

<span id="an_59:2">59:2</span> Ndihlangule kubasebenzi bobutshinga;
Ndisindise ebantwini abanamagazi.

<span id="an_59:3">59:3</span> Ngokuba nabo bewulalela umphefumlo wam;
Baqukana ngam abanamandla, Kungekho lukreqo kum, kungekho sono kum,
Yehova.

<span id="an_59:4">59:4</span> Ndingenabugwenxa nje, bagidime baxhoba.
Vuka, undikhawulele, ubone.

<span id="an_59:5">59:5</span> Wena Yehova, Thixo wemikhosi, Thixo
kaSirayeli, Phapha, uzivelele zonke iintlanga; Musa ukubayeka bonke
abanginizayo bengabagqithi. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_59:6">59:6</span> Bayabuya ngokuhlwa, bayavungama
njengezinja, Bawuhamba-hambe umzi.

<span id="an_59:7">59:7</span> Nabo belephuza amagwebu ngomlomo;
Ngamakrele emlonyeni wabo; Ngokuba bathi, Kuva bani na?

<span id="an_59:8">59:8</span> Wena, Yehova, uyabahleka, Uyazigculela
zonke iintlanga.

<span id="an_59:9">59:9</span> Mandla am, ndiva kulindela kuwe; Ngokuba
uThixo uyingxonde yam.

<span id="an_59:10">59:10</span> UThixo wam uya kundikhawulela ngenceba
yakhe; UThixo uya kundibonisa abandilaleleyo.

<span id="an_59:11">59:11</span> Musa ukubabulala, hleze balibale abantu
bakowethu; Babhadulise ngamandla akho, ubawise, Ngweletshetshe yethu,
Nkosi yethu.

<span id="an_59:12">59:12</span> Isono somlomo wabo lilizwi lemilebe
yomlomo wabo; Mababanjiswe likratshi labo, Nangenxa yokushwabula
nokuhanahanisa abakuthethayo.

<span id="an_59:13">59:13</span> Bagqibe ngobushushu; gqiba, bangabi
sabakho; Baqonde ukuba uThixo ngumlawuli kwaYakobi, Wesa eziphelweni
zehlabathi. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_59:14">59:14</span> Bayabuya ngokuhlwa, bayavungama
njengezinja, Bawuhamba-hambe umzi.

<span id="an_59:15">59:15</span> Bona babhadulela ukudla; Ukuba bathe
abahlutha, balala apho.

<span id="an_59:16">59:16</span> Ke mna, ndiya kuvuma ngamandla akho,
Ndimemelele kwakusasa ngenceba yakho, Kuba ubuyingxonde kum, Nendawo
endisabela kuyo ngemini yokubandezelwa kwam.

<span id="an_59:17">59:17</span> Mandla am, ndiya kukubethela uhadi;
Ngokuba uThixo yingxonde yam, nguThixo wam onenceba.

<span id="an_60:1">60:1</span> Kumongameli; ngeyenyibiba yesingqino.
Eliligugu. EkaDavide. Eyokufundisa: ekulweni kwakhe nama-Aram phakathi
kweMilambo nama-Aram aseTsobha; wabuya uYowabhi, wawabulala amaEdom
emfuleni wetyuwa, amawaka alishumi elinamabini. Thixo, usihlambile,
wasichitha, Waqumba; ngamana wasibuyisa.

<span id="an_60:2">60:2</span> Ulinyikimisile ilizwe, ulikrazule;
Philisa iintanda zalo ngokuba lishukuma.

<span id="an_60:3">60:3</span> Ubabonisile abantu bakho into elukhuni,
Usiseze iwayini ehexisayo.

<span id="an_60:4">60:4</span> Ubanike ibhanile abakoyikayo, Ukuba
bayiphakamise ngenxa yenyaniso. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_60:5">60:5</span> Ukuze zihlangulwe iintanda zakho, Sindisa
ngesandla sakho sokunene, undiphendule.

<span id="an_60:6">60:6</span> UThixo uthethe engcwele: mandivuyelele,
Ndimabe uShekem, ndiyilinganisele intili yaseSukoti.

<span id="an_60:7">60:7</span> Ngowam uGiliyadi, ngowam uManase,
UEfrayim sisigcina-ntloko sam, UYuda yintonga yam yommiselo;

<span id="an_60:8">60:8</span> UMowabhi sisitya sam sokuhlambela,
Ndiyiphosa kuEdom imbadada yam; Filisti, nkqangaza wena ngam.

<span id="an_60:9">60:9</span> Ngubani na owondisa emzini wamandla?
Ngubani na owondikhaphela kwaEdom?

<span id="an_60:10">60:10</span> Asinguwe na, kwawena Thixo,
osihlambileyo? Akwaphuma, Thixo, nemikhosi yethu.

<span id="an_60:11">60:11</span> Sincede kumbandezeli wethu; Alunto
yanto usindiso lomntu.

<span id="an_60:12">60:12</span> NgoThixo siya kweyisa, Wobagqusha yena
ababandezeli bethu.

<span id="an_61:1">61:1</span> Kumongameli; eyokubethelwa ngezinto
ezineentambo. EkaDavide. Kuve, Thixo, ukuhlahlamba kwam; Wubazele
indlebe umthandazo wam.

<span id="an_61:2">61:2</span> Ndidanduluka kuwe ndisesiphelweni
sehlabathi, ekutyhafeni kwentliziyo yam; Ndikhaphele eweni
elisemalengalengeni kum.

<span id="an_61:3">61:3</span> Ngokuba ulihlathi lam, Uyinqaba ende
eliqele phambi kotshaba.

<span id="an_61:4">61:4</span> Ndiya kuphambukela ententeni yakho
ngonaphakade, Ndiya kuzimela ngesithe lamaphiko akho. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_61:5">61:5</span> Ngokuba wena, Thixo, uzivile
izibhambathiso zam; Ubanike ilifa abaloyikayo igama lakho.

<span id="an_61:6">61:6</span> Uya kongeza imihla emihleni yokumkani;
Iminyaka yakhe iya kuba njengezizukulwana ngezizukulwana;

<span id="an_61:7">61:7</span> Uya kuhlala ngonaphakade phambi koThixo;
Mmisele inceba nenyaniso, ukuba zimlondoloze.

<span id="an_61:8">61:8</span> Kukhona ndiya kulibethela uhadi igama
lakho ngonaphakade, Ndizizalise izibhambathiso zam imihla ngemihla.

<span id="an_62:1">62:1</span> Kumongameli. KuYedutun. Umhobe kaDavide.
Uthozamele kuThixo kwaphela umphefumlo wam; Kuvela kuye ukusindiswa
kwam.

<span id="an_62:2">62:2</span> Nguye kwaphela iliwa lam, umsindisi wam,
Ingxonde yam; andiyi kushukunyiswa kakhulu.

<span id="an_62:3">62:3</span> Kunini na nisuka indulumbane emntwini?
Kunini na nimncinitha nonke niphela, enjengodonga oluzimkayo,
enjengothango oluwayo?

<span id="an_62:4">62:4</span> Bagqibe kwelokuba bamtyhale bamsuse
ekuphakameni kwakhe kuphele; Bakholene namanga; Basikelela elowo
ngomlomo, embilinini yabo bayatshabhisa. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_62:5">62:5</span> Thozamela kuThixo yedwa, mphefumlo wam,
Ngokuba livela kuye ithemba lam.

<span id="an_62:6">62:6</span> Nguye kwaphela iliwa lam, umsindisi wam,
Ingxonde yam; andiyi kushukunyiswa.

<span id="an_62:7">62:7</span> KunoThixo ukusindiswa kwam nozuko lwam;
Iliwa lokunqaba kwam nehlathi lam likuThixo.

<span id="an_62:8">62:8</span> Kholosani ngaye ngamaxesha onke, nina
bantu; Phalazani intliziyo yenu phambi kwakhe. UThixo ulihlathi kuthi.
(Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_62:9">62:9</span> Bangumphunga kwaphela onyana boluntu,
ngamanga oonyana bamadoda; Esikalini bangenyuka, Bangumphunga bephelele.

<span id="an_62:10">62:10</span> Musani ukukholosa ngokudla abantu,
Ningazenzi into engeyanto ngento exhakamfuliweyo. Yakwanda imfuyo,
musani ukuyinyamekela.

<span id="an_62:11">62:11</span> Uthethe nto-nye uThixo, Ezi zinto
zimbini ndizivile: Ukuba amandla ngakaThixo,

<span id="an_62:12">62:12</span> Nenceba yeyakho, Nkosi yam; Ngokuba
uyababuyekeza, elowo ngokwezenzo zakhe.

<span id="an_63:1">63:1</span> Umhobe kaDavide: oko ebesentlango
yakwaYuda. Thixo, unguThixo wam, ndiya kukuquqela kwakusasa, Umphefumlo
wam unxanele wena; inyama yam iyakulangazelela Ezweni elingumqwebedu,
elibharhileyo, eligenamanzi.

<span id="an_63:2">63:2</span> Ndenjenjalo ukukhangela kuwe engcweleni,
Ukuba ndibone amandla akho nobuqaqawuli bakho.

<span id="an_63:3">63:3</span> Ngokuba inceba yakho ilungile ngaphezu
kobomi, Umlomo wam uya kukuncoma.

<span id="an_63:4">63:4</span> Ndiya kwenjenjalo ukukubonga lo gama
ndihleliyo, Ndiphakamise izandla zam egameni lakho.

<span id="an_63:5">63:5</span> Umphefumlo wam uhluthi umongo namanqatha;
Ngemilebe yomlomo wam omemelelayo uya kukudumisa umlomo wam,

<span id="an_63:6">63:6</span> Ndakukukhumbula emandlalweni wam,
Emilindweni yobusuku ndicamanga ngawe.

<span id="an_63:7">63:7</span> Ngokuba uluncedo kum, Ndinokumemelela
esithunzini samaphiko akho.

<span id="an_63:8">63:8</span> Umphefumlo wam uthene mbende nawe;
Isandla sakho sokunene sindibambile.

<span id="an_63:9">63:9</span> Ke bona bafuna umphefumlo wam ukuze
batshabalale, Baya kutshona kwezisezantsi iindawo zehlabathi.

<span id="an_63:10">63:10</span> Baphalazelwa emandleni ekrele; Baba
sisabelo seempungutye.

<span id="an_63:11">63:11</span> Ke yena ukumkani uya kuvuya ngoThixo;
Baya kuqhayisa abo bonke bafunga yena; Ngokuba uya kuvingcwa umlomo
wabathetha ubuxoki.

<span id="an_64:1">64:1</span> Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide. Live,
Thixo, izwi lam ekukhalazeni kwam; Ekunkwantyiseni kotshaba bulondoloze
ubomi bam.

<span id="an_64:2">64:2</span> Ndisithelise egquguleni labanobubi,
Ehlokondibeni labasebenzi bobutshinga;

<span id="an_64:3">64:3</span> Abalulola njengekrele ulwimi lwabo,
Abaxuna iintolo zabo, amazwi akrakra,

<span id="an_64:4">64:4</span> Bamtole ogqibeleleyo besentsithelweni;
Bamtola ngesiquphe, bangoyiki.

<span id="an_64:5">64:5</span> Bazomelezela ilizwi elibi, Bagqiba
kwelokuba bafihle izirhintyelo, Bathi, Singabonwa ngubani na?

<span id="an_64:6">64:6</span> Baceba ubugqwetha; Baligqibile icebo
abalicebileyo; Imbilini yendoda nentliziyo yayo yinzulu.

<span id="an_64:7">64:7</span> Ke uThixo uyabatola ngotolo; Amanxeba abo
abakho ngesiquphe.

<span id="an_64:8">64:8</span> Baya kukhutyekiswa, lufikele kwabona
ulwimi lwabo; Bayahlunguzela intloko bonke abababonayo.

<span id="an_64:9">64:9</span> Basuka boyike bonke abantu, Bawuxele
umsebenzi kaThixo, Basiqiqe isenzo sakhe.

<span id="an_64:10">64:10</span> Liya kuvuya ilungisa ngoYehova,
lizimele ngaye, Baqhayise bonke abantliziyo zithe tye.

<span id="an_65:1">65:1</span> Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide. Ingoma.
Ukuthozama kuyindumiso kuwe, Thixo, eZiyon; Sizaliswa kuwe
isibhambathiso.

<span id="an_65:2">65:2</span> Wena mphulaphuli wemithandazo, Iza kuwe
inyama yonke.

<span id="an_65:3">65:3</span> Zindoyisile nje iindawo zobugwenxa,
Ukreqo lwethu uyaluxolela wena ngocamagushelo.

<span id="an_65:4">65:4</span> Hayi, uyolo lomnyulayo, umsondeze Ukuba
ahlale ezintendelezweni zakho! Siya kuzihluthisa ngokulunga kwendlu
yakho, Kwetempile yakho engcwele.

<span id="an_65:5">65:5</span> Usiphendula ngezenzo ezoyikekayo
zobulungisa, Thixo osisindisayo; Nkoloseko yeziphelo zonke zehlabathi,
neyolwandle olukude;

<span id="an_65:6">65:6</span> Ulozinzisa iintaba ngamandla akhe,
Ebhinqe ubugorha;

<span id="an_65:7">65:7</span> Ulodambisa ukugquma kweelwandle, ukugquma
kwamaza azo, Nokuxokozela kwezizwe.

<span id="an_65:8">65:8</span> Bayayoyika imiqondiso yakho abemi
beziphelo zehlabathi. Umemelelisa ukuvela kokusa nokuhlwa.

<span id="an_65:9">65:9</span> Uwuvelele umhlaba, wawunyela, Wawutyebisa
kakhulu. Umjelo kaThixo uzele ngamanzi: Walungisa ingqolowa yabo,
ngokuba uwenjenje ukuwulungisa.

<span id="an_65:10">65:10</span> Useza ihluthe imisele yawo; Unyakamisa
imiqela yawo. Uthambisa ngeziphango; Usikelela izilimo zawo.

<span id="an_65:11">65:11</span> Uwuthwesile umnyaka wokulunga kwakho,
Imikhondo yakho itsitsa ukutyeba.

<span id="an_65:12">65:12</span> Ayatsitsa amakriwa entlango, Iinduli
zizibhinqise umgcobo.

<span id="an_65:13">65:13</span> Amadlelo anxibe imihlambi yeenkomo;
Iintili zambethe ingqolowa. Yonke into iyaduma, yonke into iyavuma.

<span id="an_66:1">66:1</span> Kumongameli. Ingoma. Umhobe. Dumani
kuThixo, nonke hlabathi,

<span id="an_66:2">66:2</span> Lubetheleni uhadi uzuko lwegama lakhe,
Mzukiseni, mdumiseni.

<span id="an_66:3">66:3</span> Yithini kuThixo, Hayi, ukoyikeka
kwemisebenzi yakho! Ngenxa yobuninzi bamandla akho ziya kuhanahanisa
kuwe iintshaba zakho.

<span id="an_66:4">66:4</span> Lonke ihlabathi liya kukunqula,
Bakubethele uhadi; Balibethele uhadi igama lakho. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_66:5">66:5</span> Yizani, nibone imisebenzi emikhulu
kaThixo, Engowoyikekayo ekwenzeni kwakhe koonyana babantu.

<span id="an_66:6">66:6</span> Waluguqula ulwandle lwayinto eyomileyo;
Bawuwela umlambo ngeenyawo; Apho savuya ngaye.

<span id="an_66:7">66:7</span> Ulolawula ngobugorha bakhe ngonaphakade;
Amehlo akhe ayabonisela ezintlangeni; Abaziinjubaqa mabangaziphakamisi.
(Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_66:8">66:8</span> Mbongeni, zizwe, uThixo wethu, Nivakalise
ilizwi lendumiso yakhe.

<span id="an_66:9">66:9</span> Ulomisa umphefumlo wethu ebomini,
Akalunikela unyawo lwethu ekutyibilikeni.

<span id="an_66:10">66:10</span> Ngokuba usicikidile, Thixo;
Usinyibilikisile njengokunyibilikiswa kwesilivere;

<span id="an_66:11">66:11</span> Usingenise emboniselweni; Ubeke
uxinzelelo esinqeni sethu;

<span id="an_66:12">66:12</span> Ukhwelise abantu entlokweni yethu;
Singene emlilweni nasemanzini; Waza wasikhuphela endaweni enendyebo.

<span id="an_66:13">66:13</span> Ndiya kungena endlwini yakho
ndinamadini anyukayo; Ndiya kuzizalisa kuwe izibhambathiso zam,

<span id="an_66:14">66:14</span> Eyazivulelayo imilebe yomlomo wam,
Owazithethayo umlomo wam ekubandezelweni kwam.

<span id="an_66:15">66:15</span> Ndiya kunyusela kuwe amadini anyukayo
eemvana ezityebileyo, Ndawonye nesiqhumiso seenkunzi zeegusha; Ndiya
kwenza aweenkomo ndawonye naweenkunzi zeebhokhwe. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_66:16">66:16</span> Yizani, nive, ndinixelele, nonke nina
bamoyikayo uThixo, Oko akwenzele umphefumlo wam.

<span id="an_66:17">66:17</span> Ndadanduluka kuye ngomlomo wam; Kwaye
ukubonga kuphantsi kolwimi lwam.

<span id="an_66:18">66:18</span> Ukuba bendisekeleze ubutshinga
ngentliziyo yam, INkosi yam ibingayi kuphulaphula.

<span id="an_66:19">66:19</span> Hayi ke, uThixo uphulaphule, Ulibazele
indlebe ilizwi lomthandazo wam.

<span id="an_66:20">66:20</span> Makabongwe uThixo, Yena ungawugxothanga
umthandazo wam, Nobubele bakhe kum.

<span id="an_67:1">67:1</span> Kumongameli; eyokubethelwa ngezinto
ezineentambo. Umhobe. Ingoma. Ngamana uThixo wasibabala, wasisikelela,
Wabukhanyisa ubuso bakhe kuthi; (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_67:2">67:2</span> Ukuze yaziwe ehlabathini indlela yakho,
Usindiso lwakho ezintlangeni zonke.

<span id="an_67:3">67:3</span> Ngamana zabulela izizwe kuwe, Thixo,
Zabulela izizwe kuwe zonke ziphela;

<span id="an_67:4">67:4</span> Zavuya zamemelela izizwe: Ngokuba uya
kugweba phakathi kwezizwe ngokuthe tye, Uzikhaphe izizwe ehlabathini.
(Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_67:5">67:5</span> Ngamana zabulela izizwe kuwe, Thixo,
Zabulela izizwe kuwe zonke ziphela.

<span id="an_67:6">67:6</span> Umhlaba uyivelisile indyebo yawo; Uya
kusisikelela uThixo, uThixo wethu;

<span id="an_67:7">67:7</span> Uya kusisikelela uThixo, Zimoyike zonke
iziphelo zehlabathi.

<span id="an_68:1">68:1</span> Kumongameli; ekaDavide. Umhobe. Ingoma.
Makasuk’ eme uThixo, zibe ziintsali iintshaba zakhe, Basabe ebusweni
bakhe abamthiyayo.

<span id="an_68:2">68:2</span> Njengokuphetshethwa komsi, baphephethe;
Njengokunyibilika komthwebeba phambi komlilo, Mabadake ngokunjalo
abangendawo ebusweni bukaThixo.

<span id="an_68:3">68:3</span> Ke wona amalungisa makavuye, adlamke
phambi koThixo, Abe nemihlali, enemivuyo.

<span id="an_68:4">68:4</span> Vumani kuThixo, libetheleni uhadi igama
lakhe; Menzeleni umendo ophakamileyo, ulokhwela ecanda ezinkqantosini,
Ogama lakhe linguYehova; nidlamke phambi kwakhe.

<span id="an_68:5">68:5</span> Uyise weenkedama, umthetheleli
wabahlolokazi, NguThixo ekhayeni lakhe elingcwele.

<span id="an_68:6">68:6</span> UThixo nguhlalisa endlwini ababebodwa,
Ngukhuphela enywebeni ababanjiweyo; Ngabaziinjubaqa bodwa abahlala
kwelibalelelweyo.

<span id="an_68:7">68:7</span> Thixo, ekuphumeni kwakho uphambi kwabantu
bakho, Ekunyatheleni kwakho enkangala, (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_68:8">68:8</span> Lanyikima ihlabathi, Lavuza izulu
ebusweni bukaThixo, ISinayi leya ebusweni bukaThixo, uThixo kaSirayeli.

<span id="an_68:9">68:9</span> Walitshiza ngemvula eninzi yesisa sakho,
Thixo, ilifa lakho; Lakubharha, walizimasa wena.

<span id="an_68:10">68:10</span> Wahlala khona umhlambi wakho,
Wamlungisela olusizana ngokulunga kwakho, Thixo.

<span id="an_68:11">68:11</span> INkosi iya kukhupha izwi elinamandla,
Ube mkhulu umkhosi weentokazi ezishumayela iindaba ezilungileyo.

<span id="an_68:12">68:12</span> Ookumkani bemikhosi baya kusaba
besabile; Intokazi esele ekhaya iya kuwaba amaxhoba.

<span id="an_68:13">68:13</span> Nakulala phantsi phakathi kweentlanti,
Noxelisa amaphiko evukuthu alekwe ngesilivere, Neentsiba zalo ezalekwe
ngegolide ebengezelayo.

<span id="an_68:14">68:14</span> Ekubadubadubeni kukaSomandla ookumkani
kulo, Koba mhlophe ngowekhephu eTsalimon.

<span id="an_68:15">68:15</span> Yintaba kaThixo intaba yaseBhashan,
Yintaba encopho zininzi intaba yaseBhashan.

<span id="an_68:16">68:16</span> Niyigxeleshelani na, zintaba zincopho
zininzi, Intaba ayinqweneleyo uThixo ukuba ahlale kuyo? Ewe, uYehova uya
kuhlala kuyo ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_68:17">68:17</span> Iinqwelo zokulwa zikaThixo zizigidi,
ngamawaka-waka; INkosi ikuzo; yiSinayi ebungcweleni,

<span id="an_68:18">68:18</span> Unyuke waya phezulu, uthimbe
abathinjwa, Uthabathe izipho phakathi kwabantu, Naphakathi
kwabaziinjubaqa, ukuba ahlale uYehova uThixo khona.

<span id="an_68:19">68:19</span> Mayibongwe iNkosi; Ithwala imithwalo
yethu imihla ngemihla; NguThixo umsindisi wethu. (Phakamisani.

<span id="an_68:20">68:20</span> Yena uThixo kuthi nguThixo wosindiso,
KokukaYehova, iNkosi yethu, ukukhupha ekufeni.

<span id="an_68:21">68:21</span> Kodwa uThixo uya kuyiphalusa intloko
yeentshaba zakhe, Nentloko enesihlwitha yohambayo kwizigqitho zakhe.

<span id="an_68:22">68:22</span> Yathi iNkosi, Ndiya kuzibuyisa
eBhashan, Ndiya kuzibuyisa iintshaba zakho ezinzulwini zolwandle;

<span id="an_68:23">68:23</span> Ukuze uziphaluse, unyawo lwakho
lusegazini, Nolwimi lwezinja zakho lube nesabelo salo ezintshabeni.

<span id="an_68:24">68:24</span> Bakubona ukunyathela kwakho, Thixo,
Ukunyathela koThixo wam, koKumkani wam, esebungcweleni.

<span id="an_68:25">68:25</span> Phambili ziimvumi, ngasemva ngababethi
bohadi, Emacaleni ziintombi ezibetha iingqongqo.

<span id="an_68:26">68:26</span> Emabandleni bongani uThixo, INkosi,
nina basemthonjeni wakwaSirayeli.

<span id="an_68:27">68:27</span> Balapho ooBhenjamin, inci yabo,
umphathi wabo, Abathetheli bakwaYuda, ihlokondiba labo; Abathetheli
bakwaZebhulon, abathetheli bakwaNafetali.

<span id="an_68:28">68:28</span> UThixo wakho wakuwisela umthetho wokuba
uqine; Kuqinise, Thixo, oko usenzeleyo.

<span id="an_68:29">68:29</span> Bevela etempileni yakho eyongamele
iYerusalem, Ookumkani mabeze nezithabathaba kuwe.

<span id="an_68:30">68:30</span> Khalimela amarhamncwa asengcongolweni,
Umhlambi weenkunzi eziziimbalasane, kunye namathole ezizwe, Ukuze
baziwise benezijungqe zesilivere. Wazibhangisa izizwe eziyithandayo
imfazwe.

<span id="an_68:31">68:31</span> Kovela amanono eYiputa; UKushi
wozolulela msinya izandla zakhe kuThixo.

<span id="an_68:32">68:32</span> Zikumkani zehlabathi, vumani kuThixo,
Niyibethele uhadi iNkosi; (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_68:33">68:33</span> Ekhwela ecanda emazulwini awo amazulu
amandulo; Nanko elikhupha ilizwi lakhe, ilizwi elinamandla.

<span id="an_68:34">68:34</span> Mnikeni amandla uThixo; Buphezu
koSirayeli ubungangamsha bakhe; Asesibhakabhakeni amandla akhe.

<span id="an_68:35">68:35</span> UloThixo woyikekayo ezingcweleni zakho.
UloThixo kaSirayeli, ubanikayo amandla nokomelela abantu. Makabongwe
uThixo.

<span id="an_69:1">69:1</span> Kumongameli; ngeyeenyibiba. EkaDavide.
Ndisindise, Thixo; Ngokuba amanzi andifikele, ada eza emphefumlweni.

<span id="an_69:2">69:2</span> Nditshonile eludakeni olunzulu, akukho
kuma; Ndingene emmbithini onamanzi, umsinga uyandintywilisela.

<span id="an_69:3">69:3</span> Ndidiniwe kukudanduluka; womile umqala
wam; Aphelile amehlo am; mna ndilindele kuThixo.

<span id="an_69:4">69:4</span> Abandithiyayo ngelize baninzi ngaphezu
kweenwele zentloko yam; Baninzi abandibangisayo, abaziintshaba zam
bexoka; Into endingayiphanganga bathi mandiyibuyise.

<span id="an_69:5">69:5</span> Thixo, wena uyakwazi ukumatha kwam;
Namatyala am akanakugushwa kuwe.

<span id="an_69:6">69:6</span> Mabangadani ngam abakuthembayo, Nkosi
yam, Yehova wemikhosi; Mabangangcikivwa ngam abakufunayo, Thixo
kaSirayeli.

<span id="an_69:7">69:7</span> Ngokuba ndithwele ingcikivo ngenxa yakho;
Ihlazo libugqubuthele ubuso bam;

<span id="an_69:8">69:8</span> Ndingowasemzini kubazalwana bam;
Ndingowolunye uhlanga kubantwana bakama:

<span id="an_69:9">69:9</span> Ngokuba lindidlile ikhwele ngenxa yendlu
yakho: Iingcikivo zabakungcikivayo ziwe phezu kwam.

<span id="an_69:10">69:10</span> Mna, umphefumlo wam walila, uzila
ukudla; Oko kwaba yingcikivo kum.

<span id="an_69:11">69:11</span> Iingubo zam zaba zezirhwexayo, Ndaba
yinto yokuzekelisa kubo.

<span id="an_69:12">69:12</span> Bathetha ngam abahleli esangweni;
Ndiyingoma yamanxila.

<span id="an_69:13">69:13</span> Ke mna ndithandaza kuwe, Yehova,
ngexesha elikholekileyo: Thixo, ngobuninzi benceba yakho, Ndiphendule
ngenyaniso yosindiso lwakho.

<span id="an_69:14">69:14</span> Ndihlangule eludakeni, ndingatshoni;
Mandihlangulwe kwabandithiyayo nasemimbithini enamanzi.

<span id="an_69:15">69:15</span> Mawungandintywiliseli umsinga wamanzi;
Ingandiginyi inzulu; Iqula malingandivingceli ngomlomo walo

<span id="an_69:16">69:16</span> Ndiphendule, Yehova, ngokuba ilungile
inceba yakho, Ngangobuninzi bemfesane yakho ndibheke.

<span id="an_69:17">69:17</span> Musa ukubusithelisa ubuso bakho
kumkhonzi wakho, Ngokuba ndibandezelekile; khawuleza undiphendule.

<span id="an_69:18">69:18</span> Sondela emphefumlweni wam, uwukhulule;
Ngenxa yeentshaba zam ndikhulule.

<span id="an_69:19">69:19</span> Wena uyakwazi ukungcikivwa kwam,
nokudaniswa kwam, nokuhlazwa kwam; Baphambi kwakho bonke
abandibandezelayo.

<span id="an_69:20">69:20</span> Ingcikivo yaphula intliziyo yam,
ndaphantsa ukufa; Ndathemba ukukhuzwa, akwabakho; Nokuthuthuzelwa,
andakufumana.

<span id="an_69:21">69:21</span> Ukudla bandinika inyongo; Ekunxanweni
kwam bandiseza iviniga.

<span id="an_69:22">69:22</span> Isithebe sabo phambi kwabo masibe
ngumgibe; Sibe sisirhintyelo kwabanemasi.

<span id="an_69:23">69:23</span> Makabe mnyama amehlo abo, bangaboni,
Usigxadazelise isinqe sabo amaxesha onke.

<span id="an_69:24">69:24</span> Baphalazele ngobhavumo lwakho,
Kubafikele ukuvutha komsindo wakho.

<span id="an_69:25">69:25</span> Ingqili yabo mayibe senkangala,
Ezintenteni zabo kungahlali mntu;

<span id="an_69:26">69:26</span> Ngokuba bayamsukela obethwe nguwe,
Bancokole ngomvandedwa wobahlabileyo wena.

<span id="an_69:27">69:27</span> Yongeza ubugwenxa ebugwenxeni babo,
Bangangeni ebulungi senibakho.

<span id="an_69:28">69:28</span> Mabacinywe encwadini yobomi,
Bangabhalwa namalungisa.

<span id="an_69:29">69:29</span> Ke mna ndilusizana, ndinomvandedwa;
Usindiso lwakho, Thixo, malundise engxondeni.

<span id="an_69:30">69:30</span> Ndiya kulidumisa igama likaThixo
ngokuvuma, Ndilenze likhulu ngokubulela.

<span id="an_69:31">69:31</span> Oko kuya kukholeka kuYehova ngaphezu
kweenkunzi ezintsha, Ezineempondo neempuphu.

<span id="an_69:32">69:32</span> Bebona abalulamileyo, bovuya; Nina
bamquqelayo uThixo, intliziyo yenu mayiphile.

<span id="an_69:33">69:33</span> Ngokuba uYehova uyaweva amahlwempu,
Akabadeli ababanjiweyo bakhe.

<span id="an_69:34">69:34</span> Malimdumise izulu nomhlaba, Ulwandle
nento yonke enambuzelayo kulo.

<span id="an_69:35">69:35</span> Ngokuba uThixo uya kuyisindisa iZiyon,
ayakhe imizi yakwaYuda, Bahlale khona, bayime;

<span id="an_69:36">69:36</span> Ilidle ilifa imbewu yabakhonzi bakhe;
Bahlale kuyo abalithandayo igama lakhe.

<span id="an_70:1">70:1</span> Kumongameli; ekaDavide; eyokukhumbuza.
Thixo, khawuleza undihlangule; Yehova, khawuleza undincede.

<span id="an_70:2">70:2</span> Mabadane babe neentloni abawufunayo
umphefumlo wam; Mababuye umva bahlazeke abananze ukuba ndihlelwe bububi;

<span id="an_70:3">70:3</span> Mababuye ngenxa yomvuzo wedano labo
Abathi, Tshotsho! Tshotsho!

<span id="an_70:4">70:4</span> Mababe nemihlali bavuye ngawe bonke
abakuquqelayo; Abaluthandayo usindiso lwakho Mabahlale besithi,
Makenziwe mkhulu uThixo.

<span id="an_70:5">70:5</span> Ke mna ndilusizana, ndilihlwempu; Thixo,
khawuleza uze kum. Umncedi wam nomsindisi wam nguwe; Yehova, musa
ukulibala.

<span id="an_71:1">71:1</span> Ndizimela ngawe, Yehova, Mandingaze
ndidane naphakade:

<span id="an_71:2">71:2</span> Ngobulungisa bakho ndihlangule, ndisize;
Ndithobele indlebe yakho, undisindise.

<span id="an_71:3">71:3</span> Yiba liliwa elilikhaya kum, ndize kulo
ngamaxesha onke. Uwise umthetho wokuba ndisindiswe, Ngokuba ingxondorha
yam nemboniselo yam nguwe.

<span id="an_71:4">71:4</span> Thixo wam, ndisize esandleni songendawo,
Esandleni sogqwethayo nosisibhovubhovu.

<span id="an_71:5">71:5</span> Ngokuba ulithemba lam, Nkosi yam, Yehova,
Inkoloseko yam kwasebuncinaneni bam.

<span id="an_71:6">71:6</span> Ndixhaswe nguwe kwasesizalweni; Nguwe
owandityhobozisayo ezibilinini zikama. Indumiso yam ingawe ngamaxesha
onke.

<span id="an_71:7">71:7</span> Ndinjengesimanga kwabaninzi; Ke wena
ulihlathi lam elinqabileyo.

<span id="an_71:8">71:8</span> Umlomo wam uya kuzala yindumiso yakho,
Sisihombo sakho imini yonke.

<span id="an_71:9">71:9</span> Musa ukundilahla ngexesha lobuxhego; Musa
ukundishiya akuphela amandla am.

<span id="an_71:10">71:10</span> Ngokuba zithetha ngam iintshaba zam;
Abawulindayo umphefumlo wam bayacebisana,

<span id="an_71:11">71:11</span> Besithi, UThixo umlahlile; Msukeleni
nimbambe, ngokuba akukho mhlanguli.

<span id="an_71:12">71:12</span> Thixo, musa ukuba kude kum; Thixo wam,
khawuleza undincede.

<span id="an_71:13">71:13</span> Mabadane, bagqitywe, abawuchasayo
umphefumlo wam, Bathiwe wambu yingcikivo nehlazo abafuna ukuba ndihlelwe
bububi.

<span id="an_71:14">71:14</span> Ke mna ndiya kuhlala ndilindile,
Ndongeze endumisweni yakho yonke.

<span id="an_71:15">71:15</span> Umlomo wam uya kubalisa ngemisebenzi
yobulungisa bakho, Neyosindiso lwakho imini yonke, ngokuba ndingawazi
amanani ayo.

<span id="an_71:16">71:16</span> Ndiya kuza nemisebenzi yobugorha
beNkosi uYehova; Ndiya kukhankanya ubulungisa bakho, bakho wedwa.

<span id="an_71:17">71:17</span> Thixo, undifundisile kwasebuncinaneni
bam; Unangoku ndiyayixela imisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo.

<span id="an_71:18">71:18</span> Thixo, musa ukundishiya kude kuye
ebuxhegweni nasezimvini; Ndide ndiyixele ingalo yakho kwisizukulwana
esitsha, Nobugorha bakho kubo bonke abaya kuza.

<span id="an_71:19">71:19</span> Thixo, ubulungisa bakho buye bafika
phezulu; Wena uzenzayo izinto ezinkulu, Thixo, ngubani na onjengawe?

<span id="an_71:20">71:20</span> Wena, usibonisileyo iimbandezelo
ezininzi ezinobubi, Uya kubuya usiphilise, Ubuye usirhole
ezinzonzobileni zamanzi ehlabathi;

<span id="an_71:21">71:21</span> Uya kubandisa ubukhulu bam, Ubuye wena
undithuthuzele.

<span id="an_71:22">71:22</span> Ndiya kuyibulela nokuyibulela kuwe
ngomrhubhe Inyaniso yakho, Thixo wam; Ndiya kukubethela uhadi, Ngcwele
kaSirayeli.

<span id="an_71:23">71:23</span> Uya kumemelela umlomo wam,
ndakukubethela uhadi, Nomphefumlo wam owukhululeyo;

<span id="an_71:24">71:24</span> Nolwimi lwam luya kuxela ubulungisa
bakho imini yonke, Ngokuba bedanile beneentloni abafuna ukuba ndihlelwe
bububi.

<span id="an_72:1">72:1</span> EkaSolomon. Thixo, mnike ukumkani
imigwebo yakho, Mnike unyana wokumkani ubulungisa bakho.

<span id="an_72:2">72:2</span> Makagwebe ebantwini bakho ngobulungisa,
Nakwabaziintsizana zakho ngokwesiko.

<span id="an_72:3">72:3</span> Iintaba mazibathwalele uxolo abantu,
Kwaneenduli zibathwalele ebulungiseni.

<span id="an_72:4">72:4</span> Makagwebe ityala labaziintsizana
ebantwini, Asindise oonyana bamahlwempu, Abatyumze abacudisi.

<span id="an_72:5">72:5</span> Mabakoyike, ukuhlala elihleliyo ilanga
Kwanenyanga, izizukulwana ngezizukulwana.

<span id="an_72:6">72:6</span> Makehle njengemvula ehla phezu kotyani
obusikwayo, Njengeziphango, njengemvula emathontsi makhulu, emhlabeni.

<span id="an_72:7">72:7</span> Malityatyambe ngemihla yakhe ilungisa,
Nobuninzi boxolo, ide ingabi sabakho inyanga.

<span id="an_72:8">72:8</span> Makaphathe ubukhosi ethabathela elwandle
ase elwandle, Ethabathela kuwo uMlambo ase eziphelweni zehlabathi.

<span id="an_72:9">72:9</span> Baya kuguqa phambi kwakhe abemi
bomqwebedu, Zikhothe uthuli iintshaba zakhe.

<span id="an_72:10">72:10</span> Ookumkani baseTarshishe nabeziqithi
baya kunika iminikelo; Ookumkani bakwaShebha nabakwaSebha baya kusondeza
isithabathaba;

<span id="an_72:11">72:11</span> Baqubude kuye bonke ookumkani,
Zimkhonze sonke iintlanga.

<span id="an_72:12">72:12</span> Ngokuba uya kulihlangula ihlwempu
elizibikayo, Nabaziintsizana abangenaluncedo;

<span id="an_72:13">72:13</span> Abenzele inceba abasweleyo
nabangamahlwempu; Asindise imiphefumlo yamahlwempu;

<span id="an_72:14">72:14</span> Akhulule imiphefumlo yawo
ekuxinezelweni nasekugonyamelweni; Linqabile emehlweni akhe igazi lawo.

<span id="an_72:15">72:15</span> Uya kuphila anikwe igolide yakwaShebha,
Bahlale bemthandazela, Bamsikelele imini yonke.

<span id="an_72:16">72:16</span> Makubekho intabalala yengqolowa ezweni,
ise encotsheni yeentaba; Ukuqhama kwayo makurhashaze njengeLebhanon;
Mabatyatyambe emizini yabo njengemifuno yomhlaba.

<span id="an_72:17">72:17</span> Malibe ngunaphakade igama lakhe;
Malivelise amagatya igama lakhe phambi kwelanga, Bazisikelele ngaye;
Mazithi zonke iintlanga ungonoyolo.

<span id="an_72:18">72:18</span> Makabongwe uYehova uThixo, uThixo
kaSirayeli. Ulomenzi wemisebenzi ebalulekileyo yena yedwa.

<span id="an_72:19">72:19</span> Malisikelelwe igama lakhe elizukileyo
ngonaphakade, Lizale lonke ihlabathi luzuko lwakhe. Amen, amen.

<span id="an_72:20">72:20</span> Iphelile imithandazo kaDavide unyana
kaYese.

<span id="an_73:1">73:1</span> Umhobe ka-Asafu. Ulungile kwaphela uThixo
kuSirayeli, Kwabantliziyo zinyulu.

<span id="an_73:2">73:2</span> Ke mna, beziphantse ukumka iinyawo zam;
Gcwizi ukutyibilika ukunyathela kwam;

<span id="an_73:3">73:3</span> Ngokuba bendibamonela abaqhayisayo,
Ndakukubona ukuphumelela kwabangendawo.

<span id="an_73:4">73:4</span> Ngokuba abanazintlungu ekufeni kwabo;
Baphilile, batyebile umzimba wabo;

<span id="an_73:5">73:5</span> Ebubini babantu abakho bona; Abakhathazwa
njengabanye abantu.

<span id="an_73:6">73:6</span> Ngako oko intamo yabo inxitywe ikratshi;
Ukugonyamela kubathe wambu ngokwengubo.

<span id="an_73:7">73:7</span> Amehlo abo avelile kukutyeba; Amabhongo
eentliziyo zabo aphumela phandle.

<span id="an_73:8">73:8</span> Bahlalela ngentlamba, bathetha
ngokubandezela, benobubi; Bathetha iindumbisa zamazwi.

<span id="an_73:9">73:9</span> Bawubeka ezulwini umlomo wabo, Ulwimi
lwabo luhamba emhlabeni wonke.

<span id="an_73:10">73:10</span> Ngako oko abantu babo babuyela apha;
Bafinca amanzi amaninzi.

<span id="an_73:11">73:11</span> Bathi, Unokuthini na ukwazi uThixo?
Kukho ukwazi na kOsenyangweni?

<span id="an_73:12">73:12</span> Yabona abangendawo abaya
Banokuchulumacha ngonaphakade, bandile ngokutyeba.

<span id="an_73:13">73:13</span> Sifumane sayiqaqambisa intliziyo yethu
kanti, Sazihlamba izandla zethu ngokuba msulwa;

<span id="an_73:14">73:14</span> Ndakhathazeka imini yonke, Ukohlwaywa
kwethu kwaba kokwemiso yonke.

<span id="an_73:15">73:15</span> Ukuba bendithe, Ndiya kwenjenjalo
ukuthetha, Yabona, ngendinginizile kwisizukulwana soonyana bakho.

<span id="an_73:16">73:16</span> Ndathi ke ndakucinga ukuba ndikwazi
oko, Kwayinkohla emehlweni am;

<span id="an_73:17">73:17</span> Ndada ndaya kungena ezingcweleni
zikaThixo, Ndakugqala ke ukuphela kwabo.

<span id="an_73:18">73:18</span> Inene, ubamise ezindaweni ezibuthelezi,
Wabawisa baba yintshabalala.

<span id="an_73:19">73:19</span> Hayi, ukuphanziswa kwabo ngephanyazo;
Baphelile, bagqityiwe kukukhwankqa.

<span id="an_73:20">73:20</span> Njengephupha ekuqabukeni komntu,
Ekuvukeni kwakho, Nkosi, wowudela umfanekiso wabo.

<span id="an_73:21">73:21</span> Ukuba ndithe ndabindeka intliziyo,
Ndahlabeka ezintsweni,

<span id="an_73:22">73:22</span> Ndoba ke ndisisityhakala,
ndingenakwazi; Ndoba ke ndisisilo kuwe.

<span id="an_73:23">73:23</span> Mna ke ndihlala ndinawe; Undibambile
ngesandla sam sokunene;

<span id="an_73:24">73:24</span> Uya kundikhapha ngecebo lakho.
Undithabathe emveni koku, ndibe nozuko.

<span id="an_73:25">73:25</span> Ndinabani na emazulwini? Ukuba wena
ungowam, andilinanze nganto ihlabathi.

<span id="an_73:26">73:26</span> Ingaphela inyama yam nentliziyo yam:
Iliwa lentliziyo yam, nesabelo sam, nguThixo ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_73:27">73:27</span> Ngokuba, yabona, abanyawukileyo kuwe
baya kudaka; Uyababhangisa bonke abahenyuzayo, bemke kuwe.

<span id="an_73:28">73:28</span> Mna ke, ukusondela kuThixo kulungile
kum, Ndiyenza ihlathi lam iNkosi uYehova, Ukuze ndiyibalise yonke
imisebenzi yakhe.

<span id="an_74:1">74:1</span> Eyokuqiqa; eka-Asafu. Yini na Thixo,
ukuba uhlale usihlambile, Uqhume umsindo wakho kwizimvu zedlelo lakho?

<span id="an_74:2">74:2</span> Likhumbule ibandla lakho olithengileyo
kwakudala, Olikhululeyo, laba sisizwe selifa lakho; Intaba yaseZiyon,
ohleli kuyo.

<span id="an_74:3">74:3</span> Phakamisa ukunyathela kwakho, ukuya
kumanxuwa ahlala ehleli: Utshaba luvive into yonke engcweleni.

<span id="an_74:4">74:4</span> Babharhula ababandezeli bakho endaweni
yokuhlangana phakathi; Bamisa eyabo imiqondiso, yaba yiyo eyimiqondiso.

<span id="an_74:5">74:5</span> Kwanga kungenelwe Intshinyela yemithi
ngezixengxe.

<span id="an_74:6">74:6</span> Kungoku, uqoqo lwayo lonke Balucanda
ngamazembe neengxobonga.

<span id="an_74:7">74:7</span> Bayifaka umlilo ingcwele yakho;
Bawuhlambela ngokuwuwisela emhlabeni umnquba wegama lakho.

<span id="an_74:8">74:8</span> Bathi ezintliziyweni zabo, Siya
kubanyanzelela phantsi kuphele; Bazitshisile zonke iindawo zikaThixo
zokuhlangana ezweni apha.

<span id="an_74:9">74:9</span> Imiqondiso yethu asiyiboni, Akusekho
mprofeti; Kuthi akukho waziyo ukuba koda kuse phi na kunjalo.

<span id="an_74:10">74:10</span> Kunini na, Thixo, umbandezeli
engcikiva? Utshaba luhleli luligiba igama lakho?

<span id="an_74:11">74:11</span> Usifinyezeleni na isandla sakho,
nesokunene sakho? Sirhole esifubeni sakho, ulugqibe.

<span id="an_74:12">74:12</span> Ke uThixo nguKumkani wam kwakumandulo,
Ulosebenza usindiso phakathi kwehlabathi lonke.

<span id="an_74:13">74:13</span> Nguwe owahlula ulwandle ngamandla akho,
Owaphula iintloko zeengwenya emanzini.

<span id="an_74:14">74:14</span> Nguwe owaxhaxha iintloko zeleviyatan,
Wazinika zakukudla kubantu, kubemi bomqwebedu.

<span id="an_74:15">74:15</span> Nguwe owagqobhoza yayimithombo,
yayimilanjana; Nguwe owomisa imilambo engomiyo.

<span id="an_74:16">74:16</span> Yeyakho imini, bobakho nobusuku; Nguwe
owalungisa ukukhanya nelanga.

<span id="an_74:17">74:17</span> Nguwe owamisa yonke imida yehlabathi;
Ihlobo, nobusika, nguwe owazibumbayo ezo zinto.

<span id="an_74:18">74:18</span> Khumbula oku; utshaba lungcikiva
uYehova, Abantu abanobudenge baligibile igama lakho.

<span id="an_74:19">74:19</span> Musa ukuwunikela erhamncweni umphefumlo
wehobe lakho; Ungahlali uwulibele umhlambi wakho oziintsizana.

<span id="an_74:20">74:20</span> Bheka emnqophisweni, Ngokuba iindawo
ezimnyama zelizwe zizele zizindlu zogonyamelo.

<span id="an_74:21">74:21</span> Makangabuyi otyumkileyo ehlazisiwe;
Makalidumise igama lakho olusizana nolihlwempu.

<span id="an_74:22">74:22</span> Khawusuk’ ume, Thixo, ubambane
nababambene nawe; Khumbula ukukungcikiva kwesidenge yonke imini.

<span id="an_74:23">74:23</span> Musa ukulilibala izwi lababandezeli
bakho, Ukungxola kwabasukela phezulu kuwe, okuhlala kunyuka.

<span id="an_75:1">75:1</span> Kumongameli; ngethi, Ungonakalisi. Umhobe
ka-Asafu. Ingoma. Siyabulela kuwe, Thixo, siyabulela; Lisondele igama
lakho; Babalisa imisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo.

<span id="an_75:2">75:2</span> Ngokuba uthi, Ndiya kwenza ngexesha
elimisiweyo, Mna ndiya kugweba ngokuthe tye.

<span id="an_75:3">75:3</span> Liyetha amandla ihlabathi, nabemi balo;
Ke mna, ndizizinzisile iintsika zalo. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_75:4">75:4</span> Ndithi kubaqhayisi, Musani ukuqhayisa;
Nakwabangendawo, Musani ukuphakamisa uphondo;

<span id="an_75:5">75:5</span> Musani ukuluphakamisela phezulu uphondo
lwenu, Ningathethi ngokusa, nolule intamo.

<span id="an_75:6">75:6</span> Ngokuba ugwebo aluveli empumalanga
nasentshonalanga, Nasentlango yeentaba.

<span id="an_75:7">75:7</span> Hayi, nguThixo ogwebayo; Uyamthoba lo,
amphakamise lowa.

<span id="an_75:8">75:8</span> Ngokuba indebe isesandleni sikaYehova,
Iphuphuma igwebu lewayini, izele yephithikeziweyo. Uthulula kuyo; ewe,
iintlenga zayo Ziya kuselwa zifincwe ngabangendawo bonke behlabathi.

<span id="an_75:9">75:9</span> Ke mna ndiya kushumayela ngonaphakade,
Ndiya kuvuma kuThixo kaYakobi;

<span id="an_75:10">75:10</span> Zonke iimpondo zabangendawo ndiya
kuzixakaxa, Iimpondo zelungisa ziya kuphakanyiswa.

<span id="an_76:1">76:1</span> Kumongameli; eyokubethelwa ngezinto
ezineentambo. Umhobe ka-Asafu. Ingoma. Waziwa kwaYuda uThixo, Likhulu
kwaSirayeli igama lakhe.

<span id="an_76:2">76:2</span> Umnquba wakhe waba seSalem, Nekhaya lakhe
eZiyon.

<span id="an_76:3">76:3</span> Wayaphula apho imibane yesaphetha,
Ingweletshetshe, nekrele, nezixhobo zemfazwe. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_76:4">76:4</span> Ukhanyile, uyingangamsha ngaphezu
kweentaba zokuqwenga.

<span id="an_76:5">76:5</span> Babhunyulwe abantliziyo iyimbalasane,
Balala umlala kanye, Akazifumana izandla zawo onke amakroti.

<span id="an_76:6">76:6</span> Ekukhalimeni kwakho, Thixo kaYakobi,
Kwasindwa bubuthongo iinqwelo zokulwa namahashe.

<span id="an_76:7">76:7</span> Unguwena wena woyikekayo; Ngubani na
onokuma phambi kwakho, wakuba nomsindo?

<span id="an_76:8">76:8</span> Emazulwini usivakalisile isigwebo; Loyika
ihlabathi, lazola,

<span id="an_76:9">76:9</span> Ekusukeni kukaThixo ukuba agwebe,
Abasindise bonke abalulamileyo behlabathi. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_76:10">76:10</span> Ngokuba ubushushu bomntu buya kuba
ngumbulelo kuwe; Uya kuwabhinqa amasalela obushushu.

<span id="an_76:11">76:11</span> Bhambathisani, nisizalise
isibhambathiso kuYehova uThixo wenu; Bonke abamngqongileyo mabeze
nezithabathaba kofanele kukoyikwa.

<span id="an_76:12">76:12</span> Uya kunqumla ukufutha kweenganga,
Uyoyikeka kookumkani behlabathi.

<span id="an_77:1">77:1</span> Kumongameli. KuYedutun. Eka-Asafu.
Umhobe. Izwi lam lisingisa kuThixo, ndikhala; Izwi lam lisingisa
kuThixo, ukuba andibekele indlebe.

<span id="an_77:2">77:2</span> Ngemini yokubandezelwa kwam ndiquqela
eNkosini yam; Isandla sam solukile ebusuku, asaqoba; Awavuma
ukuthuthuzeleka umphefumlo wam.

<span id="an_77:3">77:3</span> Ndikhumbula uThixo, ndincwine;
Ndithelekelele, utyhafe umoya wam. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_77:4">77:4</span> Uzibambile iinkophe zamehlo am,
Ndikhandiwe, andaba nakuthetha.

<span id="an_77:5">77:5</span> Ndicinga ngemihla yamandulo, Iminyaka
yasephakadeni;

<span id="an_77:6">77:6</span> Ndiya kukhumbula ebusuku ukubetha kwam
uhadi; Ndithetha nentliziyo yam, uphengulula umoya wam.

<span id="an_77:7">77:7</span> Ndithi, Iya kundihlamba ngonaphakade na
iNkosi yam, Ingabi saphinda iphathe ngetarhu na?

<span id="an_77:8">77:8</span> Iphele yaphela na inceba yayo? Sigqibele
na isithembiso sayo kwisizukulwana ngesizukulwana?

<span id="an_77:9">77:9</span> UThixo ukulibele na ukubabala?
Uyivingcele ngomsindo kusini na imfesane yakhe? (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_77:10">77:10</span> Ndide ndithi ke, Sisifo sam esi;
Yiminyaka yesandla sokunene sOsenyangweni.

<span id="an_77:11">77:11</span> Ndikhankanya izenzo ezincamisayo
zikaYehova; Ngokuba ndikhumbula imisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo
yamandulo.

<span id="an_77:12">77:12</span> Ndicamanga ngako konke ukusebenza
kwakho, Ndithelekelele ngezenzo zakho zonke ezincamisayo.

<span id="an_77:13">77:13</span> Thixo, isebungcweleni indlela yakho;
Ngubani na onguthixo omkhulu njengoThixo wethu?

<span id="an_77:14">77:14</span> UnguloThixo, wenza ngokubalulekileyo;
Wawazisa amandla akho ezizweni,

<span id="an_77:15">77:15</span> Wabakhulula ngengalo abantu bakho,
Oonyana bakaYakobi noYosefu. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_77:16">77:16</span> Akubona amanzi, Thixo, Akubona amanzi,
azibhija-bhija, Ewe, agungqa amanzi enzonzobila;

<span id="an_77:17">77:17</span> Amafu engqingqwa aphalaza amanzi,
Isibhakabhaka savakalisa isandi; Ewe, iintolo zakho zahamba-hamba.

<span id="an_77:18">77:18</span> Izwi lendudumo yakho laba
sesaqhwithini, Imibane yalikhanyisa elimiweyo, Lagungqa lanyikima
ihlabathi.

<span id="an_77:19">77:19</span> Yaba selwandle indlela yakho, Nomendo
wakho waba semanzini amaninzi; Awaziwa umkhondo wakho.

<span id="an_77:20">77:20</span> Wabakhokela njengezimvu abantu bakho,
Ngesandla sooMoses noAron.

<span id="an_78:1">78:1</span> Eyokuqiqa ka-Asafu. Wubekeleni indlebe
umyalelo wam, bantu bakowethu, Wathobeleni indlebe amazwi omlomo wam.

<span id="an_78:2">78:2</span> Ndiya kuwuvula umlomo wam ngomzekeliso;
Ndiya kumpompozisa iintsonkotha zamandulo;

<span id="an_78:3">78:3</span> Esakuvayo sakwazi, Abasibaliselayo
oobawo.

<span id="an_78:4">78:4</span> Asiyi kukugusha koonyana babo; Sobalisela
isizukulwana esizayo iindumiso zikaYehova, Namandla akhe, nemisebenzi
yakhe ebalulekileyo awayenzayo.

<span id="an_78:5">78:5</span> Wamisa isingqiniso kwaYakobi, Wabeka
umyalelo kwaSirayeli, Awawumisela oobawo, Ukuba bawazise oonyana babo;

<span id="an_78:6">78:6</span> Ukuze siwazi isizukulwana esizayo,
oonyana abaza kuzalwa, Basuke babalisele ababo oonyana;

<span id="an_78:7">78:7</span> Bayame ngoThixo, Bangazilibali izenzo
ezincamisayo zikaThixo, Bayilondoloze imithetho yakhe:

<span id="an_78:8">78:8</span> Bangabi njengooyise, Isizukulwana
esiyinjubaqa, esineenkani, Isizukulwana esingayilungisanga intliziyo
yaso, Esimoya unganyanisanga kuThixo.

<span id="an_78:9">78:9</span> Oonyana bakaEfrayim, bexhobile,
beziintoli ezinezaphetha, Bajika ngemini yemfazwe.

<span id="an_78:10">78:10</span> Abawugcinanga umnqophiso kaThixo,
Abavumanga ukuhamba ngomyalelo wakhe;

<span id="an_78:11">78:11</span> Bazilibala izenzo zakhe ezincamisayo,
Nezibalulekileyo zakhe awababonisayo.

<span id="an_78:12">78:12</span> Phambi kooyise wenza ngokubalulekileyo
Ezweni lamaYiputa, emhlabeni waseTsohan.

<span id="an_78:13">78:13</span> Waludabula ulwandle, wabaweza, Wawamisa
amanzi njengemfumba.

<span id="an_78:14">78:14</span> Wabakhapha ngelifu emini, Ngokukhanya
komlilo ubusuku bonke,

<span id="an_78:15">78:15</span> Walicanda iliwa entlango, Wabaseza
amanzi anzongonzongo kakhulu;

<span id="an_78:16">78:16</span> Wavelisa imiqukuqela yamanzi
engxondorheni, Wahlisa amanzi njengemilambo.

<span id="an_78:17">78:17</span> Baqokela noko ukona kuye, Nokumphikisa
Osenyangweni emqwebedwini.

<span id="an_78:18">78:18</span> Bamlinga uThixo ngentliziyo yabo,
Ngokuwubizela umphefumlo wabo ukudla.

<span id="an_78:19">78:19</span> Bathetha ngoThixo, bathi, Unako na
uThixo ukulungisa isithebe entlango?

<span id="an_78:20">78:20</span> Yabona, walibetha iliwa, abaleka
amanzi, Yakhukula nemilanjana; Woba nako na nokubanika ukutya,
Nokubalungiselela inyama abantu bakhe?

<span id="an_78:21">78:21</span> Weva ke uThixo, waphuphuma umsindo
wakhe, Watsha umlilo kwaYakobi, Kwenyuka kwaya umsindo kwaSirayeli;

<span id="an_78:22">78:22</span> Ngokuba bengakholwanga kuThixo,
Bengakholosanga ngosindiso lwakhe.

<span id="an_78:23">78:23</span> Waziwisela ke umthetho iingqimba zamafu
ngaphezulu, Wazivula iingcango zezulu;

<span id="an_78:24">78:24</span> Wabanisela ngemana ukuze badle,
Wabanika ingqolowa yasezulwini.

<span id="an_78:25">78:25</span> Umntu wadla isonka sOnamandla;
Wabathumela umphako bada badikwa.

<span id="an_78:26">78:26</span> Wandulula umoya wasempumalanga
ezulwini, Wawuqhuba ngamandla akhe umoya wasezantsi;

<span id="an_78:27">78:27</span> Wabanisela inyama njengothuli, Neentaka
ezinamaphiko njengentlabathi yolwandle;

<span id="an_78:28">78:28</span> Yawa phakathi kweminquba yabo, Ngeenxa
zonke emakhayeni abo.

<span id="an_78:29">78:29</span> Badla, bahlutha kakhulu, Wabazisela ke
inkanuko yabo.

<span id="an_78:30">78:30</span> Bengekashenxi enkanukweni yabo, Kusekho
ukudla kwabo emlonyeni wabo:

<span id="an_78:31">78:31</span> Kwenyuka umsindo kaThixo waya kubo,
Wabulala phakathi kwabatyebileyo babo, Wawawisa amadodana akwaSirayeli.

<span id="an_78:32">78:32</span> Kuyo yonke loo nto bahambisa ngokona,
Abakholwa yimisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo.

<span id="an_78:33">78:33</span> Wayiphelisa ke imihla yabo
njengomphunga, Neminyaka yabo ngokukhwankqisa.

<span id="an_78:34">78:34</span> Xa wathi wababulala, bamquqela; Babuya
bamquqela uThixo ngenyameko,

<span id="an_78:35">78:35</span> Bakhumbula ukuba uThixo uliliwa labo,
UThixo Osenyangweni ungumkhululi wabo.

<span id="an_78:36">78:36</span> Ke bamthomalalisa ngomlomo wabo,
Bamxokisa ngolwimi lwabo;

<span id="an_78:37">78:37</span> Intliziyo yabo ayaqina kuye,
Abanyaniseka emnqophisweni wakhe.

<span id="an_78:38">78:38</span> Ke yena unemfesane, Uxolela ubugwenxa
ngocamagushelo, akonakalisi; Wawubuyisa futhi umsindo wakhe, Akabuxhoxha
bonke ubushushu bakhe.

<span id="an_78:39">78:39</span> Wakhumbula ukuba bayinyama, Bangumoya
omkayo, ongabuyiyo.

<span id="an_78:40">78:40</span> Kukangaphi bemphikisa entlango, Bemenza
buhlungu enkangala!

<span id="an_78:41">78:41</span> Babuya bamlinga uThixo, Bamenzakalisa
oyiNgcwele wakwaSirayeli.

<span id="an_78:42">78:42</span> Abasikhumbula isandla sakhe, Imini
awabakhulula ngayo embandezelweni;

<span id="an_78:43">78:43</span> Awamisa ngayo imiqondiso yakhe eYiputa,
Nezimanga zakhe emhlabeni waseTsohan.

<span id="an_78:44">78:44</span> Wayiguqula imijelo yabo, yaba ligazi,
Ababa nakuyisela imiqukuqela yabo yamanzi.

<span id="an_78:45">78:45</span> Wathumela kubo iingcongconi, zabadla;
Namasele, abatshabalalisa.

<span id="an_78:46">78:46</span> Izilimo zabo wazinika iinkumbi
ezinqunquthayo, Ukuxelenga kwabo wakunika iinkumbi ezandayo.

<span id="an_78:47">78:47</span> Wawubulala ngesichotho umdiliya wabo,
Nemithombe yabo ngomkhenkce.

<span id="an_78:48">78:48</span> Wayinikela kwisichotho imfuyo yabo,
Nemihlambi yabo ngemibane.

<span id="an_78:49">78:49</span> Wathumela kubo ukuvutha komsindo wakhe,
Ukuphuphuma kwawo, nokubhavuma, nembandezelo, Ibutho lezithunywa zobubi.

<span id="an_78:50">78:50</span> Wawulungelelanisela umendo umsindo
wakhe, Akawunqanda ekufeni umphefumlo wabo, Wabunikela ubomi babo
kwindyikitya yokufa.

<span id="an_78:51">78:51</span> Wababulala bonke abamazibulo eYiputa,
Iintlahlela zamandla obudoda ezintenteni zakwaHam.

<span id="an_78:52">78:52</span> Abantu bakhe wabafudusa njengezimvu,
Wabaqhuba njengomhlambi entlango;

<span id="an_78:53">78:53</span> Wabakhapha bekholosile, bengankwantyi;
Ke zona iintshaba zabo lwazigubungela ulwandle

<span id="an_78:54">78:54</span> Wabazisa emdeni wakhe ongcwele, Kule
ntaba sayizuzayo isandla sakhe sokunene.

<span id="an_78:55">78:55</span> Wagxotha iintlanga ebusweni babo,
Wazenzela amaqashiso zalilifa elicandiweyo; Izizwe zakwaSirayeli
wazihlalisa ezintenteni zazo.

<span id="an_78:56">78:56</span> Kodwa bamlinga, bamphikisa uThixo
Osenyangweni, Abazigcina izingqiniso zakhe,

<span id="an_78:57">78:57</span> Babuya unuva, banginiza njengooyise.
Bajika njengesaphetha esikhohlisayo.

<span id="an_78:58">78:58</span> Bamqumbisa ngeziganga zabo,
Bamkhweletisa ngemifanekiso yabo eqingqiweyo.

<span id="an_78:59">78:59</span> Weva uThixo, waphuphuma umsindo,
Wawacekisa kakhulu amaSirayeli;

<span id="an_78:60">78:60</span> Wawulahla umnquba waseShilo, Intente
abeyimise esintwini;

<span id="an_78:61">78:61</span> Wawanikela ekuthinjweni amandla akhe,
Isihombo sakhe esandleni sombandezeli.

<span id="an_78:62">78:62</span> Wabanikela abantu bakhe kwikrele,
Umsindo wakhe waphuphumela ilifa lakhe.

<span id="an_78:63">78:63</span> Amadodana abo adliwa ngumlilo, Iintombi
zabo azagcotyelwa.

<span id="an_78:64">78:64</span> Ababingeleli babo bawa likrele,
Abahlolokazi babo abalila.

<span id="an_78:65">78:65</span> Yaza yavuka njengobelele iNkosi,
Njengegorha elimemeleliswa yiwayini.

<span id="an_78:66">78:66</span> Yababetha ngasemva ababandezeli bayo,
Yabenza ingcikivo engunaphakade.

<span id="an_78:67">78:67</span> Yayicekisa intente yakwaYosefu,
Ayasinyula isizwe sakwaEfrayim.

<span id="an_78:68">78:68</span> Yanyula isizwe sakwaYuda, Intaba
yaseZiyon eyayithandayo.

<span id="an_78:69">78:69</span> Yayakha njengokuphakama kwezulu
ingcwele yakhe, Njengomhlaba lo awusekileyo ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_78:70">78:70</span> Yanyula uDavide umkhonzi wayo,
Yamthabatha ezibayeni zezimvu;

<span id="an_78:71">78:71</span> Yamthabatha elandela izimvu ezanyisayo,
Yamzisa ukuba aluse kwaYakobi abantu bayo, KwaSirayeli ilifa layo.

<span id="an_78:72">78:72</span> Wabalusa ke ngengqibelelo yentliziyo
yakhe, Wabakhapha ngokwazi kwezandla zakhe.

<span id="an_79:1">79:1</span> Umhobe ka-Asafu. Thixo, iintlanga zingene
elifeni lakho, Ziyenze inqambi itempile yakho engcwele; Ziyenze
yayimiwewe iYerusalem.

<span id="an_79:2">79:2</span> Izidumbu zabakhonzi bakho zizinike
iintaka zezulu ukuba zizidle, Nenyama yabakho benceba ziyinike
amarhamncwa elizwe.

<span id="an_79:3">79:3</span> Ziliphalazile igazi labo njengamanzi
ngeenxa zonke eYerusalem; Akwabakho mngcwabi.

<span id="an_79:4">79:4</span> Senziwe ingcikivo kubamelwane bethu,
Isigculelo nesicukucezo kwabasingqongileyo.

<span id="an_79:5">79:5</span> Kunini na, Yehova, uhleli uqumbile? Liya
kuvutha njengomlilo na ikhwele lakho?

<span id="an_79:6">79:6</span> Phalaza ubushushu bakho ezintlangeni
ezingakwaziyo, Ezikumkanini ezingalinquliyo igama lakho.

<span id="an_79:7">79:7</span> Ngokuba zimdlile uYakobi, Zalenza inxuwa
ikhaya lakhe.

<span id="an_79:8">79:8</span> Musa ukubukhumbula kuthi ubugwenxa
bamanyange ethu, Mayingxame isikhawulele imfesane yakho: Ngokuba siswele
kakhulu.

<span id="an_79:9">79:9</span> Sincede, Thixo ongumsindisi wethu, ngenxa
yozuko lwegama lakho, Usihlangule, uzixolele ngocamagushelo izono zethu
ngenxa yegama lakho.

<span id="an_79:10">79:10</span> Yini na ukuba iintlanga zithi kuthi,
Uphi na uThixo wabo? Makwazeke ezintlangeni, emehlweni ethu,
Ukuphindezelwa kwegazi labakhonzi bakho eliphalaziweyo.

<span id="an_79:11">79:11</span> Makuze phambi kwakho ukugcuma
kwamakhonkxwa; Ngokobukhulu bengalo yakho basalise oonyana bokufa.

<span id="an_79:12">79:12</span> Yibuyisele kubamelwane bethu kasixhenxe
esondweni lengubo yabo Ingcikivo yabo, abakungcikive ngayo, Nkosi.

<span id="an_79:13">79:13</span> Ke thina bantu bakho, zimvu zaluswa
nguwe, Siya kubulela kuwe ngonaphakade, Sibalise ngendumiso yakho
kwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana.

<span id="an_80:1">80:1</span> Kumongameli; ngeyeenyibiba ezingqinisayo.
Ka-Asafu. Umhobe. Ulomalusi kaSirayeli, beka indlebe! Uloqhuba uYosefu
njengezimvu, Ulohlala ezikerubhini, bengezela!

<span id="an_80:2">80:2</span> Phambi koEfrayim noBhenjamin noManase,
Vusa ubugorha bakho, Uze kusisindisa.

<span id="an_80:3">80:3</span> Thixo, sibuyise, Ukhanyise ubuso bakho,
sisindiswe.

<span id="an_80:4">80:4</span> Yehova, Thixo wemikhosi, Kunini na uqhuma
umsindo wakho ekuthandazeni kwabantu bakho?

<span id="an_80:5">80:5</span> Ubadlisa isonka seenyembezi, Wabaseza
iinyembezi ngemilinganiso.

<span id="an_80:6">80:6</span> Usenze into abaxabana ngayo abamelwane
bethu; Iintshaba zethu ziyasigculela.

<span id="an_80:7">80:7</span> Thixo wemikhosi, sibuyise, Ukhanyise
ubuso bakho, sisindiswe.

<span id="an_80:8">80:8</span> Wanyothula umdiliya eYiputa, Wagxotha
iintlanga, wawutyala;

<span id="an_80:9">80:9</span> Wahlahla phambi kwawo, Wendelisa
iingcambu, wazalisa ilizwe.

<span id="an_80:10">80:10</span> Zagutyungelwa iintaba ngumthunzi wawo,
Nemisedare kaThixo ngamasebe awo.

<span id="an_80:11">80:11</span> Wasa amasebe awo elwandle, Namagatya
awo kuwo uMlambo.

<span id="an_80:12">80:12</span> Uzityhobozeleni na iintango zawo, Ukuze
bawukhe bonke abadlula ngendlela?

<span id="an_80:13">80:13</span> Ingulube yasehlathini iyawubhuqa, Nento
edakasa endle iyawudla.

<span id="an_80:14">80:14</span> Thixo wemikhosi, khawubuye, Uqondele
usemazulwini, ubone, Uwuvelele lo mdiliya.

<span id="an_80:15">80:15</span> Yikhusele into esiyityeleyo isandla
sakho sokunene, Unyana lo uzizimaseleyo ngokwakho.

<span id="an_80:16">80:16</span> Utshisiwe ngumlilo, uhlahliwe; Bayadaka
ngokusongela kobuso bakho.

<span id="an_80:17">80:17</span> Isandla sakho masibe phezu komfo
wesandla sakho sokunene, Phezu koonyana babantu, ozizimaseleyo
ngokwakho.

<span id="an_80:18">80:18</span> Asiyi kumka kuwe; Siphilise, silinqule
igama lakho.

<span id="an_80:19">80:19</span> Yehova, Thixo wemikhosi, sibuyise,
Ukhanyise ubuso bakho, sisindiswe.

<span id="an_81:1">81:1</span> Kumongameli; ngolwaseGati. Ka-Asafu.
Memelelani kuThixo, igwiba lethu, Dumani kuThixo kaYakobi.

<span id="an_81:2">81:2</span> Hlabani ingoma, nibethe ingqongqo, Uhadi
olumnandi, kunye nomrhubhe.

<span id="an_81:3">81:3</span> Vuthelani isigodlo ukuthwasa kwenyanga,
Nokuhlangana kwenyanga, ngemini yomthendeleko wethu.

<span id="an_81:4">81:4</span> Ngokuba ngummiselo lowo kuSirayeli,
Lisiko likaThixo kaYakobi.

<span id="an_81:5">81:5</span> Sisingqiniso awasimisayo kwaYosefu,
Ekucandeni kwakhe ezweni laseYiputa; Ndeva intetho endingayaziyo.

<span id="an_81:6">81:6</span> Ndawususa umthwalo egxalabeni lakhe;
Izandla zakhe zasuka ezingobozini zokuthwala.

<span id="an_81:7">81:7</span> Embandezelweni wadanduluka wena,
ndakuhlangula; Ndakuphendula esitheni leendudumo, Ndakuvavanya emanzini
aseMeribha. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_81:8">81:8</span> Ndathi, Yivani, bantu bam, ndiqononondise
kuni; Sirayeli, ukuba unokuphulaphula kum!

<span id="an_81:9">81:9</span> Makungabikho thixo wasemzini kuwe;
Unganquli thixo wolunye uhlanga.

<span id="an_81:10">81:10</span> Ndim uYehova uThixo wakho, Okunyusileyo
elizweni laseYiputa. Yakhamisa, ndiwuzalise umlomo wakho.

<span id="an_81:11">81:11</span> Ke abantu bam abaliva izwi lam,
USirayeli akandivumanga.

<span id="an_81:12">81:12</span> Ndabanikela ebungqoleni beentliziyo
zabo; Bahamba ngawabo amaqhinga.

<span id="an_81:13">81:13</span> Akwaba abantu bam bebendiva, Akwaba
uSirayeli ubehamba ngendlela yam!

<span id="an_81:14">81:14</span> Bendiya kuzithoba kamsinya iintshaba
zabo, Ndisibuyisele phezu kwababandezeli babo isandla sam.

<span id="an_81:15">81:15</span> Abamthiyayo uYehova bebeya kuhanahanisa
