kuye, Libe ngunaphakade ixesha labo.

<span id="an_81:16">81:16</span> Bendiya kubadlisa ingqolowa etyebileyo,
Ndibahluthise ngobusi etsilini.

<span id="an_82:1">82:1</span> Umhobe ka-Asafu. UThixo umi ebandleni
likaThixo, Ugweba phakathi koothixo; uthi,

<span id="an_82:2">82:2</span> Kunini na nigweba ngobugqwetha,
Nibanonelela abangendawo? (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_82:3">82:3</span> Thethani ityala losweleyo nelenkedama,
Gwebelani olusizana nolihlwempu.

<span id="an_82:4">82:4</span> Sizani osweleyo nolihlwempu, Bahlanguleni
esandleni sabangendawo.

<span id="an_82:5">82:5</span> Abazi, abaqondi, Bahamba-hamba emnyameni;
Ziyashukuma zonke iziseko zehlabathi.

<span id="an_82:6">82:6</span> Ndithe mna, Ningoothixo, Ningoonyana
bOsenyangweni nonke niphela.

<span id="an_82:7">82:7</span> Noko niya kufa njengomntu, Niwe
njengomnye kubathetheli.

<span id="an_82:8">82:8</span> Khawusuk’ ume, Thixo, gweba ehlabathini;
Ngokuba uya kuzidla ilifa wena zonke iintlanga.

<span id="an_83:1">83:1</span> Ingoma. Umhobe ka-Asafu. Thixo, musa
ukuthi cwaka, Musa ukuthi tu, musa ukuzola, Thixo.

<span id="an_83:2">83:2</span> Ngokuba nanzo iintshaba zakho zixokozela;
Abakuthiyayo baphakamisa intloko.

<span id="an_83:3">83:3</span> Bagqugula igqugula elinobuqhophololo
ngabantu bakho, Bacebisane ngabagushiweyo nguwe.

<span id="an_83:4">83:4</span> Bathi, Yizani sibethe bee shwaka, bangabi
luhlanga, Lingabi sakhunjulwa igama likaSirayeli.

<span id="an_83:5">83:5</span> Ngokuba bacebisana ngantliziyo-nye, Benza
umnqophiso ngawe:

<span id="an_83:6">83:6</span> Iintente zakwaEdom nezakwaIshmayeli,
AmaMowabhi namaHagari,

<span id="an_83:7">83:7</span> AmaGebhali nama-Amon nama-Amaleki,
AmaFilisti kunye nabemi baseTire;

<span id="an_83:8">83:8</span> Nama-Asiriya athelele kubo, Baba yingalo
koonyana bakaLote. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_83:9">83:9</span> Yenza kubo njengoko wenza ngako
kumaMidiyan, NakuSisera, nakuYabhin esihlanjeni seKishon.

<span id="an_83:10">83:10</span> Batshabalala e-Endore, Baba ngumgquba
wokugalelwa emhlabeni.

<span id="an_83:11">83:11</span> Benze bona, amanene abo ke, babe
njengo-Orebhe nanjengoZebhe; Zonke iinkosi zabo zibe njengoZebha
nanjengoTsalimuna;

<span id="an_83:12">83:12</span> Bona bathi, Masiwahluthe abe ngawethu
amakhaya kaThixo.

<span id="an_83:13">83:13</span> Thixo wam, benze babe njengesaqhwithi,
Njengomququ phambi komoya.

<span id="an_83:14">83:14</span> Njengomlilo odla ihlathi,
Njengedangatye lilenya intaba,

<span id="an_83:15">83:15</span> Yenjenjalo ukubasukela ngoqhwithela
lwakho, Ubakhwankqise ngomoya wakho ovuthuzayo.

<span id="an_83:16">83:16</span> Buzalise ubuso babo ngehlazo, Balifune
igama lakho, Yehova.

<span id="an_83:17">83:17</span> Mabadane bakhwankqiswe ngonaphakade,
Babe neentloni, badake;

<span id="an_83:18">83:18</span> Bazi ukuba wena, ugama linguYehova,
unguwe wedwa Osenyangweni phezu kwehlabathi lonke.

<span id="an_84:1">84:1</span> Kumongameli; ngolwaseGati. Eyoonyana
bakaKora. Umhobe. Hayi, ukuthandeka kweminquba yakho, Yehova wemikhosi!

<span id="an_84:2">84:2</span> Umphefumlo wam ulangazelela, uyaphela
kukuzilangazelela, iintendelezo zikaYehova; Intliziyo yam nenyama yam
imemelela kuThixo ophilileyo.

<span id="an_84:3">84:3</span> Intakana le ifumene ikhaya; Inkonjane
izifumanele indlu, Apho izalela khona amathole ayo: Izibingelelo zakho,
Yehova wemikhosi, Kumkani wam, Thixo wam.

<span id="an_84:4">84:4</span> Hayi, uyolo lwabahlala endlwini yakho!
Basaya kukudumisa. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_84:5">84:5</span> Hayi, uyolo lwabantu abamandla akuwe,
Abakhumbula umendo oya eZiyon!

<span id="an_84:6">84:6</span> Bephumela entilini yemithi yeBhaka,
Bayenza ibe nemithombo; Ewe, imvula iyithi wambu ngentsikelelo.

<span id="an_84:7">84:7</span> Baya besomelela ngokomelela; Babonakala
phambi koThixo eZiyon, bathi,

<span id="an_84:8">84:8</span> Yehova, Thixo wemikhosi, Wuve umthandazo
wam, Wubekele indlebe, Thixo kaYakobi. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_84:9">84:9</span> Khangela, Thixo, ngweletshetshe yethu,
Ubukhangele ubuso bomthanjiswa wakho.

<span id="an_84:10">84:10</span> Ngokuba imini enye ezintendelezweni
zakho ilungile kunewaka; Ndinyule ukuba semnyango endlwini kaThixo wam,
Kunokuhlala ngaphakathi kweentente zokungendawo.

<span id="an_84:11">84:11</span> Ngokuba ulilanga, uyingweletshetshe
uYehova uThixo, UYehova uyababala azukise; Abahamba ngokugqibeleleyo
akabavimbi nto ilungileyo.

<span id="an_84:12">84:12</span> Yehova wemikhosi, Hayi, uyolo lomntu
okholose ngawe!

<span id="an_85:1">85:1</span> Kumongameli; eyoonyana bakaKora. Umhobe.
Yehova, wabe unetarhu kwilizwe lakho. Ububabuyisa abathinjwa bakaYakobi;

<span id="an_85:2">85:2</span> Ububuxolela ubugwenxa babantu bakho,
Ubuziselela zonke izono zabo. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_85:3">85:3</span> Ubuwufinyeza umsindo wakho ophuphumayo,
Ububuya ekuvutheni komsindo wakho.

<span id="an_85:4">85:4</span> Sibuyise, Thixo ongumsindisi wethu,
Uyisuse ingqumbo yakho kuthi.

<span id="an_85:5">85:5</span> Uya kusiqumbela ngonaphakade na? Umsindo
wakho uya kuwolulela kwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana na?

<span id="an_85:6">85:6</span> Akuyi kubuya usiphilise na, Abantu bakho
bavuye ngawe?

<span id="an_85:7">85:7</span> Sibonise inceba yakho, Yehova, Siphe
usindiso lwakho.

<span id="an_85:8">85:8</span> Mandive oko aya kukuthetha uThixo,
uYehova; Hayi, uthetha uxolo kubantu bakhe nakwabakhe benceba;
Mabangabuyeli ke ekunyabeni kwabo.

<span id="an_85:9">85:9</span> Inene, usindiso lwakhe lusondele
kwabamoyikayo, Ukuze luhlale uzuko ezweni lakowethu.

<span id="an_85:10">85:10</span> Kuya kuqubisana inceba nenyaniso, Kuya
kwangana ubulungisa noxolo.

<span id="an_85:11">85:11</span> Inyaniso iya kuntshula emhlabeni,
Ubulungisa buqondele busemazulwini.

<span id="an_85:12">85:12</span> Kananjalo uYehova uya kusinika
okulungileyo, Ilizwe lethu lisinike indyebo yalo.

<span id="an_85:13">85:13</span> Ubulungisa buya kuhamba phambi kwakhe,
Buyigqale ngentliziyo indlela yokunyathela kwakhe.

<span id="an_86:1">86:1</span> Umthandazo kaDavide. Thoba indlebe yakho,
Yehova, ndiphendule, Ngokuba ndilusizana, ndilihlwempu.

<span id="an_86:2">86:2</span> Wugcine umphefumlo wam, ngokuba
ndingowenceba; Msindise, wena Thixo wam, umkhonzi wakho, Lo ukholose
ngawe.

<span id="an_86:3">86:3</span> Ndibabale, Nkosi yam, Ngokuba
ndidanduluka kuwe yonke imini.

<span id="an_86:4">86:4</span> Wuvuyise umphefumlo womkhonzi wakho,
Ngokuba umphefumlo wam ndiwuphakamisela kuwe, Nkosi yam;

<span id="an_86:5">86:5</span> Ngokuba ulungile wena, Nkosi yam,
uxolela; Umkhulu ngenceba kubo bonke abakunqulayo.

<span id="an_86:6">86:6</span> Wubekele indlebe umthandazo wam, Yehova,
Ulibazele indlebe izwi lokutarhuzisa kwam.

<span id="an_86:7">86:7</span> Ngemini yokubandezelwa kwam ndinqula
wena, Ngokuba uya kundiphendula.

<span id="an_86:8">86:8</span> Akukho unjengawe, Nkosi yam, phakathi
koothixo; Akukho zenzo zinjengezakho.

<span id="an_86:9">86:9</span> Zonke iintlanga owazenzayo ziya kuza
ziqubude phambi kwakho, Nkosi yam, Zizukise igama lakho.

<span id="an_86:10">86:10</span> Ngokuba umkhulu, wenza imisebenzi
ebalulekileyo, UnguThixo wena wedwa.

<span id="an_86:11">86:11</span> Ndiyalele, Yehova, indlela yakho,
Ndihambe ngenyaniso yakho; Yibandakanye intliziyo yam ukuba ndiloyike
igama lakho.

<span id="an_86:12">86:12</span> Ndiya kubulela kuwe, Nkosi yam, Thixo
wam, ngentliziyo yonke, Ndilizukise igama lakho ngonaphakade:

<span id="an_86:13">86:13</span> Ngokuba inceba yakho ibe inkulu kum;
Wawuhlangula umphefumlo wam kwelingaphantsi labafileyo.

<span id="an_86:14">86:14</span> Thixo, abakhukhumali basukele phezulu
kum; Ibandla labanobungqwangangqwili lifuna umphefumlo wam; Abakumisi
wena phambi kwabo.

<span id="an_86:15">86:15</span> Ke wena, Nkosi yam, unguThixo
onemfesane, onobabalo, Ozeka kade umsindo, omkhulu ngenceba nenyaniso.

<span id="an_86:16">86:16</span> Ndibheke, undibabale; Mphe amandla akho
umkhonzi wakho, Umsindise unyana womkhonzazana wakho.

<span id="an_86:17">86:17</span> Ndenzele umqondiso wokulungileyo,
Bawubone abandithiyayo, badane, Kuba wena, Yehova, undincedile,
wandithuthuzela.

<span id="an_87:1">87:1</span> Eyoonyana bakaKora. Umhobe. Ingoma. Useko
alusekileyo lusezintabeni ezingcwele;

<span id="an_87:2">87:2</span> Amasango eZiyon uYehova uwathanda
Ngaphezu kweminquba yonke kaYakobi.

<span id="an_87:3">87:3</span> Kuthethwa iinto ezizukileyo ngawe, Mzi
kaThixo. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_87:4">87:4</span> ORahabhi noBhabheli ndiya kubakhankanyela
kwabandaziyo; Nalo elamaFilisti nelaseTire, kunye nelakwaKushi, Aba
bazalelwe khona.

<span id="an_87:5">87:5</span> Ngokusingisele kwiZiyon, kuya kuthiwa,
Lo, nalo, uzalelwe kuyo, Abe yena Osenyangweni eyizinzisa.

<span id="an_87:6">87:6</span> UYehova uya kubala, ekuzibhaleni izizwi,
athi, Abaya bazalelwe khona: (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_87:7">87:7</span> Baze, bevuma beqamba, bathi, Yonke
imithombo yam ikuwe.

<span id="an_88:1">88:1</span> Ingoma; umhobe woonyana bakaKora;
kumongameli; ngosizi, ngelidambileyo. Owokuqiqa kaHeman umEzra. Yehova,
Thixo ongumsindisi wam, Mhlenikweni ndikhalayo ebusuku phambi kwakho,

<span id="an_88:2">88:2</span> Mawuze phambi kwakho umthandazo wam;
Thoba indlebe yakho ekuhlahlambeni kwam.

<span id="an_88:3">88:3</span> Ngokuba umphefumlo wam uhluthi zizinto
ezimbi, Ubomi bam bufike kwelabafileyo.

<span id="an_88:4">88:4</span> Ndibalelwe kwabahla baye emhadini,
Ndisuke ndanjengomfo ongenamandla

<span id="an_88:5">88:5</span> Ndingumkhululwa phakathi kwabafileyo,
Njengababuleweyo, belele engcwabeni, Ongasabakhumbuliyo; Bona
banqunyulweyo esandleni sakho.

<span id="an_88:6">88:6</span> Undibeke emhadini ongaphantsi, Ezindaweni
ezimnyama, ezinzulwini.

<span id="an_88:7">88:7</span> Ubushushu bakho bundishicilele,
Undithobele onke amaza akho alwayo. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_88:8">88:8</span> Ubashenxisele kude kum abo ndazana nabo,
Undenze isikizi kubo; Ndivalelwe, andinakuphuma.

<span id="an_88:9">88:9</span> Iliso lam liyaphela yingcinezelo.
Ndidanduluka kuwe, Yehova, yonke imini, Ndizolulela kuwe izandla zam.

<span id="an_88:10">88:10</span> Uya kuyenzela abafileyo na imisebenzi
ebalulekileyo? Kuya kuvuka abangasekhoyo, kusini na, babulele kuwe?
(Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_88:11">88:11</span> Ibaliswa engcwabeni na inceba yakho?
Enzonzobileni na, ukunyanisa kwakho?

<span id="an_88:12">88:12</span> Yaziswa emnyameni na imisebenzi yakho
ebalulekileyo? Baziswa ezweni lokulibala na ubulungisa bakho?

<span id="an_88:13">88:13</span> Ke mna, Yehova, ndizibika kuwe,
Kwakusasa umthandazo wam wokuhlangabeza.

<span id="an_88:14">88:14</span> Uwuhlambelani na, Yehova, umphefumlo
wam? Ubusitheliselani na ubuso bakho kum?

<span id="an_88:15">88:15</span> Ndilusizana, ndiyinto efayo
kwasebuncinaneni bam, Ndithwele izothuso zakho, lindikhohlile.

<span id="an_88:16">88:16</span> Kugqithe phezu kwamukuvutha kwakho,
Izidandathekiso zakho zindibhangisile;

<span id="an_88:17">88:17</span> Zindijikelezile njengamanzi imini
yonke, Zindizungulezile kwaphela.

<span id="an_88:18">88:18</span> Umsusile kum ondithandayo nonguwethu;
Abo ndazana nabo babubumnyama.

<span id="an_89:1">89:1</span> Eyokuqiqa kaEtan, umEzra. Iinceba
zikaYehova ndiya kuvuma ngazo ngonaphakade, Kwizizukulwana
ngezizukulwana ndiya kwazisa ukuthembeka kwakho ngomlomo wam.

<span id="an_89:2">89:2</span> Ngokuba ndithi, Yakheka ngonaphakade
inceba; Amazulu, uya kukuzinzisa kuwo ukuthembeka kwakho.

<span id="an_89:3">89:3</span> Wathi, Ndenze umnqophiso nomnyulwa wam,
Ndifungile kuDavide umkhonzi wam:

<span id="an_89:4">89:4</span> Ndiya kuyizimasa ngonaphakade imbewu
yakho, Ndiyakhe itrone yakho kwisizukulwana ngesizukulwana.
(Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_89:5">89:5</span> Amazulu abulela imisebenzi yakho
ebalulekileyo, Yehova, Nokuthembeka kwakho ebandleni labangcwele.

<span id="an_89:6">89:6</span> Ngokuba ngubani na esibhakabhakeni
olingana noYehova? Ngubani na ofana noYehova phakathi koonyana
bakaThixo.

<span id="an_89:7">89:7</span> UThixo ongowokungcangcazelelwa ebhungeni
elikhulu labangcwele, Ongofanelwe kukoyikwa ngaphezu kwabo bonke
abamngqongileyo?

<span id="an_89:8">89:8</span> Yehova, Thixo wemikhosi, Ngubani na
onjengawe, oluqilima, Yehova? Ukuthembeka kwakho kukungqongile.

<span id="an_89:9">89:9</span> Nguwena mlawuli wekratshi lolwandle;
Ekuphakameni kwamaza alo uyawadambisa.

<span id="an_89:10">89:10</span> Nguwena mtyumzi kaRahabhi
njengongxwelerhiweyo, Wazithi saa iintshaba zakho ngengalo yakho
eqinileyo.

<span id="an_89:11">89:11</span> Lelakho izulu, likwalelakho ihlabathi;
Elimiweyo nenzaliseko yalo lasekwa nguwe.

<span id="an_89:12">89:12</span> Umntla nomzantsi wadalwa nguwe;
ITabhore neHermon zimemelela ngegama lakho.

<span id="an_89:13">89:13</span> Yeyakho ingalo enobugorha; Sithe nkqi
isandla sakho, siphakamile esokunene sakho.

<span id="an_89:14">89:14</span> Ummiso wetrone yakho bubulungisa
nokusesikweni; Inceba nenyaniso ilungiselela phambi kwakho.

<span id="an_89:15">89:15</span> Hayi, uyolo lwabantu abakwaziyo
ukuduma! Baya kuhamba ekukhanyeni kobuso bakho, Yehova.

<span id="an_89:16">89:16</span> Baya kugcoba egameni lakho imini yonke,
Baphakame ngobulungisa bakho.

<span id="an_89:17">89:17</span> Ngokuba isihombo samandla abo nguwe;
Ekuthandeni kwakho, uphondo lwethu luphakamile.

<span id="an_89:18">89:18</span> Ngokuba ikuYehova ingweletshetshe
yethu, UkoyiNgcwele kaSirayeli ukumkani wethu.

<span id="an_89:19">89:19</span> Wakha wathetha ngombono kowenceba
wakho, wathi, Ndibeke uncedo egorheni, Ndiphakamise indodana ebantwini.

<span id="an_89:20">89:20</span> Ndifumene uDavide umkhonzi wam;
Ndimthambisile ngeoli yam engcwele,

<span id="an_89:21">89:21</span> Esiya kuqinisela kuye isandla sam,
Nengalo yam imkhaliphise.

<span id="an_89:22">89:22</span> Utshaba aluyi kumqubula; Nonyana
wobugqwetha akayi kumcinezela.

<span id="an_89:23">89:23</span> Ndiya kubaqoba phambi kwakhe
ababandezeli bakhe, Ndibaxabele abamthiyayo.

<span id="an_89:24">89:24</span> Inyaniso yam nenceba yam inaye; Luya
kuphakama uphondo lwakhe egameni lam.

<span id="an_89:25">89:25</span> Ndiya kusisa elwandle isandla sakhe,
EMilanjeni esokunene sakhe.

<span id="an_89:26">89:26</span> Yena ukundibiza wothi, UnguBawo,
UnguThixo wam, neliwa lokundisindisa.

<span id="an_89:27">89:27</span> Kananjalo mna ndiya kumenza
owamazibulo, Osenyangweni kookumkani behlabathi.

<span id="an_89:28">89:28</span> Ndiya kumgcinela inceba yam
ngonaphakade, Umnqophiso wam unyanise kuye;

<span id="an_89:29">89:29</span> Ndiyimise ngonaphakade imbewu yakhe,
Netrone yakhe ibe njengemihla yamazulu.

<span id="an_89:30">89:30</span> Ukuba bathe oonyana bakhe bawulahla
umyalelo wam, Abahamba ngamasiko am;

<span id="an_89:31">89:31</span> Ukuba bathe bayihlambela imimiselo yam,
Abayigcina imithetho yam:

<span id="an_89:32">89:32</span> Ndoluvelela ukreqo lwabo ngentonga,
Nobugwenxa babo ngemivumbo.

<span id="an_89:33">89:33</span> Ke yona inceba yam andiyi kuyaphula
kuye, Ndingaxoki ekuthembekeni kwam.

<span id="an_89:34">89:34</span> Andiyi kuwuhlambela umnqophiso wam,
Ndiyijike into ephume emlonyeni wam.

<span id="an_89:35">89:35</span> Ndibufunge kwakanye ubungcwele bam,
ndathi, Inene, andiyi kumxokisa uDavide;

<span id="an_89:36">89:36</span> Imbewu yakhe iya kubakho ngonaphakade,
Netrone yakhe njengelanga phambi kwam.

<span id="an_89:37">89:37</span> Iya kuqiniseka njengenyanga
ngonaphakade; Ingqina lasesibhakabhakeni lithembekile. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_89:38">89:38</span> Kwawena umhlambile, umcekisile,
Umphuphumele ngomsindo umthanjiswa wakho;

<span id="an_89:39">89:39</span> Uthe nethe ngumnqophiso womkhonzi
wakho; Usidyobhile emhlabeni isithsaba sakhe.

<span id="an_89:40">89:40</span> Uzityhobozile zonke iintango zakhe,
Uzenze inxuwa iinqaba zakhe.

<span id="an_89:41">89:41</span> Bayamphanga bonke abadlula ngendlela,
Waba yingcikivo kubamelwane bakhe.

<span id="an_89:42">89:42</span> Usiphakamisile isandla sokunene
sabambandezelayo, Uzivuyisile zonke iintshaba zakhe.

<span id="an_89:43">89:43</span> Wabuyisa nokubuyisa uhlangothi lwekrele
lakhe, Akwammisa emfazweni.

<span id="an_89:44">89:44</span> Umsusile enkazimlweni yakhe,
Uyikhahlele emhlabeni itrone yakhe,

<span id="an_89:45">89:45</span> Uyinqumle imihla yobutsha bakhe, Wamthi
wambu ngokudana. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_89:46">89:46</span> Kunini na, Yehova, uhleli
uzisithelisile, Busitsha njengomlilo ubushushu bakho?

<span id="an_89:47">89:47</span> Khumbula ukunqamka kwam, into okuyiyo!
Ubadaleleni na, baba yinto engento bonke oonyana babantu?

<span id="an_89:48">89:48</span> Yiyiphi na indoda ehleliyo, engayi
kukubona ukufa, Enokuwusindisa umphefumlo wayo esandleni selabafileyo?
(Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_89:49">89:49</span> Ziphi na iinceba zakho zangaphambili,
Nkosi yam, Owamfungela zona uDavide ngokuthembeka kwakho?

<span id="an_89:50">89:50</span> Khumbula, Nkosi yam, ukungcikiveka
kwabakhonzi bakho; Ndithwele esifubeni sam zonke izizwe ezininzi,

<span id="an_89:51">89:51</span> Ezingcikivayo, ziziintshaba zakho,
Yehova; Ezingcikiva amanyathela omthanjiswa wakho.

<span id="an_89:52">89:52</span> Makabongwe uYehova ngonaphakade. Amen,
amen.

<span id="an_90:1">90:1</span> Umthandazo kaMoses, umfo wakwaThixo.
Nkosi yam, ulikhaya wena kuthi, Isizukulwana ngesizukulwana.

<span id="an_90:2">90:2</span> Kungekazalwa zintaba, Ungekavelisi
mhlaba, nazwe limiweyo, Kususela kwaphakade kude kuse ephakadeni, wena
unguThixo.

<span id="an_90:3">90:3</span> Umbuyisela umntu eluthulini, Uthi,
Buyani, nyana babantu.

<span id="an_90:4">90:4</span> Ngokuba iwaka leminyaka emehlweni akho
Linjengemini yezolo, xa idluleyo, Linjengomlindo wasebusuku.

<span id="an_90:5">90:5</span> Uyabakhukulisa, balale; Ngengomso babuya
bahlume njengotyani.

<span id="an_90:6">90:6</span> Ngomso butyatyamba, bubuye buhlume;
Ngokuhlwa buyasikwa bome.

<span id="an_90:7">90:7</span> Ngokuba siyaphela ngumsindo wakho,
Sikhwankqiswe bubushushu bakho.

<span id="an_90:8">90:8</span> Ububeke ubugwenxa bethu phambi kwakho,
Nesibufihlileyo ububeka ekukhanyiseleni kobuso bakho.

<span id="an_90:9">90:9</span> Ngokuba yonke imihla yethu isangene
ngokuphuphuma komsindo wakho, Siyiphelisile iminyaka yethu
njengentsebezo.

<span id="an_90:10">90:10</span> Imihla yeminyaka yethu iseminyakeni
engamashumi asixhenxe; Ukuba ithe yaba mininzi kakhulu, iba yiminyaka
emashumi asibhozo, Libe ke iqhayiya layo likukwaphuka nokungabi nto
yanto, Ngokuba ithe phe yakhawuleza, saphaphazela semka.

<span id="an_90:11">90:11</span> Ngubani na owaziyo amandla omsindo
wakho, Nokuphuphuma kwawo, ngoko ufanele ukoyikwa ngako?

<span id="an_90:12">90:12</span> Sazise kanye ukuyibala imihla yethu,
Ukuze sizuze intliziyo elumkileyo.

<span id="an_90:13">90:13</span> Buya, Yehova, kunini na? Uzohlwaye
ngenxa yabakhonzi bakho.

<span id="an_90:14">90:14</span> Sihluthise kwakusasa ngenceba yakho,
Simemelele, sivuye yonke imihla yethu.

<span id="an_90:15">90:15</span> Sivuyise ngangemihla owasicinezela
ngayo. Ngangeminyaka esabona ububi ngayo.

<span id="an_90:16">90:16</span> Mayibonakale kubakhonzi bakho
imisebenzi yakho, Nobungangamela bakho koonyana babo.

<span id="an_90:17">90:17</span> Ubumnandi bukaYehova mabube phezu
kwethu. Zimasa isenzo sezandla zethu phezu kwethu, Isenzo sezandla zethu
usizimase sona.

<span id="an_91:1">91:1</span> Ohleli esitheni lOsenyangweni, Azilalise
emthunzini kaSomandla,

<span id="an_91:2">91:2</span> Uthi kuYehova, Hlathi lam, Mboniselo yam,
Thixo wam, endikholose ngaye!

<span id="an_91:3">91:3</span> Ngokuba ngokwakhe uya kukuhlangula
emgibeni womthiyeli, Endyikityeni yokufa eyeyelisayo.

<span id="an_91:4">91:4</span> Wokugubungela ngeentsiba zakhe, Uzimele
phantsi kwamaphiko akhe. Likhaka, yingweletshetshe inyaniso yakhe.

<span id="an_91:5">91:5</span> Akuyi koyikiswa zizothuso ebusuku,
Nalutolo lubaleka emini;

<span id="an_91:6">91:6</span> Nandyikitya yakufa ihamba
esithokothokweni, Nasifo sibhubhisayo, sibhuqa emini enkulu.

<span id="an_91:7">91:7</span> Kungawa iwaka ecaleni kwakho, Isigidi
ngasekunene kwakho, Kodwa kungasondeli nto kuwe.

<span id="an_91:8">91:8</span> Wokhangela ngamehlo akho odwa, Ukubonele
ukubuyekezwa kwabangendawo.

<span id="an_91:9">91:9</span> Ngokuba nguwe, Yehova, ihlathi lam.
Umenze Osenyangweni ikhaya lakho.

<span id="an_91:10">91:10</span> Akuyi kuqubisana bubi nawe. Kungafiki
sibetho ententeni yakho.

<span id="an_91:11">91:11</span> Ngokuba izithunywa zakhe uziwisele
umthetho ngawe, Ukuba zikugcine ezindleleni zakho zonke.

<span id="an_91:12">91:12</span> Zokuthwala wena ngezandla zozibini,
Hleze ubetheke ngonyawo lwakho etyeni.

<span id="an_91:13">91:13</span> Wonyathela phezu kwengonyama nephimpi,
Uyinyashe ingonyama entsha nenamba ngeenyawo.

<span id="an_91:14">91:14</span> Ngokuba enamathele kum, ndomsiza;
Ndimse engxondeni, ngokuba elazi igama lam.

<span id="an_91:15">91:15</span> Wondibiza, ndiphendule, Ndoba naye
embandezelweni; Ndomhlangula, ndimzukise;

<span id="an_91:16">91:16</span> Ndimanelise ngemihla emide, Ndimbonise
ukusindisa kwam.

<span id="an_92:1">92:1</span> Umhobe; ingoma, ngemini yesabatha.
Kulungile ukubulela kuYehova, Nokulibethela uhadi igama lakho, Wena
usenyangweni;

<span id="an_92:2">92:2</span> Ukuyixela kwakusasa inceba yakho,
Nokunyanisa kwakho ebusuku,

<span id="an_92:3">92:3</span> Ngoweentambo ezilishumi nangomrhubhe,
Ngokulubetha uhadi ngofefe.

<span id="an_92:4">92:4</span> Ngokuba uyandivuyisa, Yehova, ngomsebenzi
wakho, Ngezenzo zezandla zakho ndinokumemelela.

<span id="an_92:5">92:5</span> Azizikhulu izenzo zakho, Yehova! Zinzulu
kakhulu iingcinga zakho.

<span id="an_92:6">92:6</span> Isityhakala asinakwazi; Isinyabi
asikuqondi oko.

<span id="an_92:7">92:7</span> Ekudubuleni kongendawo njengomfuno,
Ekutyatyambeni kwabasebenzi bonke bobutshinga, Kukuze batshabalale
ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_92:8">92:8</span> Ke wena, Yehova, ungophezulu
ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_92:9">92:9</span> Ngokuba uyabona, iintshaba zakho, Yehova,
Ngokuba uyabona, iintshaba zakho ziva kutshabalala; Baya
kuchithwa-chithwa bonke abasebenzi bobutshinga.

<span id="an_92:10">92:10</span> Uyaluphakamisa uphondo lwam
njengolwenqu; Ndigalelwe ioli entsha.

<span id="an_92:11">92:11</span> Iliso lam liyababonela abandilalelayo,
Indlebe yam iyabeva abasukela phezulu kum benobubi.

<span id="an_92:12">92:12</span> Amalungisa aya kudubula njengesundu,
Aya kukhula njengomsedare weLebhanon.

<span id="an_92:13">92:13</span> Etyelwe nje endlwini kaYehova, Aya
kutyatyamba ezintendelezweni zoThixo wethu.

<span id="an_92:14">92:14</span> Aya kuhluma eselenezimvi, Aya kuba
etyebile, eluhlaza;

<span id="an_92:15">92:15</span> Ukuze axele ukuba uthe tye uYehova,
Uliwa lam, kungekho bugqwetha kuye.

<span id="an_93:1">93:1</span> UYehova ungukumkani, uzambathise
ubungangamsha; UYehova uzambathise, ubhinqe, amandla; Lizinzile ke
elimiweyo, alinakushukunyiswa.

<span id="an_93:2">93:2</span> Kususela koko, izinzile itrone yakho;
Kususela kwaphakade, ukho wena.

<span id="an_93:3">93:3</span> Imilambo iphakamisile, Yehova, Imilambo
iphakamise isandi sayo, Imilambo iphakamise ingxolo yayo.

<span id="an_93:4">93:4</span> Ngaphezu kwezandi zamanzi amaninzi
Angangamsha, ngaphezu kwamaza alwayo olwandle, Unobungangamsha phezulu
uYehova.

<span id="an_93:5">93:5</span> Izingqiniso zakho zinyanise kunene,
Ubungcwele buyifanele indlu yakho, Yehova, imihla emide.

<span id="an_94:1">94:1</span> Thixo wempindezelo, Yehova, Thixo
wempindezelo, bengezela!

<span id="an_94:2">94:2</span> Phakama, Mgwebi wehlabathi! Babuyisele
impatho yabo abanekratshi.

<span id="an_94:3">94:3</span> Kunini na abangendawo, Yehova, Kunini na
abangendawo bevuyelela?

<span id="an_94:4">94:4</span> Balephuza amagwebu, bathetha ngokusa,
Bayandolosa bonke abasebenzi bobutshinga.

<span id="an_94:5">94:5</span> Batyumza abantu bakho, Yehova, Bacinezela
ilifa lakho.

<span id="an_94:6">94:6</span> Babulala umhlolokazi nowasemzini,
Bancinitha inkedama.

<span id="an_94:7">94:7</span> Bathi ke, Akaboni uYehova, Akagqali
uThixo kaYakobi.

<span id="an_94:8">94:8</span> Qondani, nina bazizityhakala ebantwini;
Nina zinyabi, niya kuqiqa nini na?

<span id="an_94:9">94:9</span> Omilisele indlebe, akayi kuva na? Obumbe
iliso, akayi kukhangela na?

<span id="an_94:10">94:10</span> Umthethisi weentlanga akayi kohlwaya
na, Ulofundisa abantu ukwazi?

<span id="an_94:11">94:11</span> UYehova ngumazi weengcinga zabantu,
Ukuba zingumphunga.

<span id="an_94:12">94:12</span> Hayi, uyolo lwendoda oyithethisayo,
Yehova, Oyifundisayo ngomyalelo wakho;

<span id="an_94:13">94:13</span> Ukuba uyizolise eziminini zobubi, Ade
ambelwe isihogo ongendawo.

<span id="an_94:14">94:14</span> Ngokuba uYehova akabalahli abantu
bakhe, Akalishiyi ilifa lakhe.

<span id="an_94:15">94:15</span> Ngokuba isiko liya kubuyela
ebulungiseni, Balilandele bonke abantliziyo zithe tye.

<span id="an_94:16">94:16</span> Ngubani na oya kusukela phezulu kubo
abanobubi, ngenxa yam? Ngubani na oya kumelana nabasebenzi bobutshinga,
ngenxa yam?

<span id="an_94:17">94:17</span> Koko uYehova abe luncedo lwam,
Umphefumlo wam unge uhle msinya, waya apho kuthiwa cwaka khona.

<span id="an_94:18">94:18</span> Ukuba ndithi, Lwatyibilika unyawo lwam,
Isuka inceba yakho, Yehova, indixhase.

<span id="an_94:19">94:19</span> Ebuninzini beengcinga-ngcinga zam
ngaphakathi kwam, Iintuthuzelo zakho ziyawuyolisa umphefumlo wam.

<span id="an_94:20">94:20</span> Ingaqhelana nawe na itrone
yolweyeliselo, Ebumba ububi ngommiselo?

<span id="an_94:21">94:21</span> Bahlanganyela umphefumlo welungisa,
Baligwebe igazi elimsulwa.

<span id="an_94:22">94:22</span> Kanti ke uYehova uyingxonde kum, UThixo
wam liliwa endizimela ngalo.

<span id="an_94:23">94:23</span> Ububuyisela phezu kwabo ubutshinga
babo, Uba bhangisa ngobubi babo; Uya kubabhangisa uYehova, uThixo wethu.

<span id="an_95:1">95:1</span> Yizani simemelele kuYehova, Sidume
kwiliwa lokusindiswa kwethu.

<span id="an_95:2">95:2</span> Masize phambi kobuso bakhe sinombulelo,
Masidume kuye ngeengoma.

<span id="an_95:3">95:3</span> Ngokuba uThixo omkhulu nguYehova,
NguKumkani omkhulu ngaphezu koothixo bonke.

<span id="an_95:4">95:4</span> Uzisesandleni sakhe iingontsingontsi
zehlabathi, Neencopho zeentaba zezakhe.

<span id="an_95:5">95:5</span> Ulolwakhe ulwandle, nguyena walwenzayo;
Nomhlaba owomileyo zawubumba izandla zakhe.

<span id="an_95:6">95:6</span> Yizani, masiqubude, siguqe, Sithobe
phambi koYehova umenzi wethu.

<span id="an_95:7">95:7</span> Ngokuba nguThixo wethu yena, Thina ke
singabantu bokwaluswa nguye, nezimvu zesandla sakhe. Namhla, ukuba
ninokuliva izwi lakhe,

<span id="an_95:8">95:8</span> Musani ukuyenza lukhuni intliziyo yenu,
njengaseMeribha, Njengemini yaseMasa entlango;

<span id="an_95:9">95:9</span> Oko bandilingayo ooyihlo. Bandicikida,
bewubona umsebenzi wam.

<span id="an_95:10">95:10</span> Iminyaka yaba ngamashumi amane
ndikruqukile sesi sizukulwana, Ndathi, Ngabantu abantliziyo
zindwendwayo, Abazazi iindlela zam bona;

<span id="an_95:11">95:11</span> Endada ndafunga ndinomsindo, ukuthi,
Inene, abasayi kungena ekuphumleni kwam.

<span id="an_96:1">96:1</span> Vumani kuYehova ingoma entsha, Vumani
kuYehova, nonke hlabathi.

<span id="an_96:2">96:2</span> Vumani kuYehova, bongani igama lakhe,
Shumayelani iimini ngeemini iindaba ezilungileyo zosindiso lwakhe.

<span id="an_96:3">96:3</span> Balisani ezintlangeni uzuko lwakhe,
Balisani ezizweni zonke imisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo;

<span id="an_96:4">96:4</span> Ngokuba mkhulu uYehova, engowokudunyiswa
kunene; Uyoyikeka yena ngaphezu koothixo bonke.

<span id="an_96:5">96:5</span> Ngokuba bonke oothixo bezizwe abanto
zanto; UYehova yena wenza amazulu.

<span id="an_96:6">96:6</span> Yindili nobungangamela phambi kwakhe,
Ngamandla nokuhomba engcweleni yakhe.

<span id="an_96:7">96:7</span> Mnikeni uYehova, nina mizalwane yezizwe,
Mnikeni uYehova uzuko namandla;

<span id="an_96:8">96:8</span> Mnikeni uYehova uzuko lwegama lakhe;
Thwalani umnikelo, nize ezintendelezweni zakhe.

<span id="an_96:9">96:9</span> Mnquleni uYehova, nivethe ezingcwele,
Thuthumelani phambi kwakhe, nonke hlabathi.

<span id="an_96:10">96:10</span> Yithini ezintlangeni, UYehova
ngukumkani, Liya kuzinza ngoko elimiweyo, lingashukumi, Uya kugweba
phakathi kwezizwe ngokuthe tye.

<span id="an_96:11">96:11</span> Liya kuvuya izulu, Ligcobe ihlabathi;
Luya kugquma ulwandle, nenzaliseko yalo.

<span id="an_96:12">96:12</span> Liya kudlamka ilizwe, nento yonke
ekulo, Ize imemelele yonke imithi yehlathi

<span id="an_96:13">96:13</span> Phambi koYehova, ngokuba esiza, Ngokuba
esiza kugweba ihlabathi. Uya kuligweba elimiweyo ngobulungisa, Nezizwe
ngokunyanisa kwakhe.

<span id="an_97:1">97:1</span> UYehova ngukumkani; liyagcoba ihlabathi,
Ziyavuya iziqithi ezininzi.

<span id="an_97:2">97:2</span> Ngamafu nesithokothoko ngeenxa zonke
kuye, Bubulungisa nokusesikweni ummiso wetrone yakhe.

<span id="an_97:3">97:3</span> Kuhamba umlilo phambi kwakhe; Ulenya
ababandezeli bakhe ngeenxa zonke.

<span id="an_97:4">97:4</span> Ikhanyisa elimiweyo imibane yakhe;
Uyabona umhlaba, uzibhija-bhije.

<span id="an_97:5">97:5</span> Iintaba zinyibilika njengomthwebeba
phambi koYehova, Phambi kweNkosi yehlabathi lonke.

<span id="an_97:6">97:6</span> Izulu lixela ubulungisa bakhe, Zilubone
uzuko lwakhe zonke izizwe.

<span id="an_97:7">97:7</span> Badanile bonke abakhonza umfanekiso
oqingqiweyo, Abaqhayisa ngeento ezingento; Bayamnqula bonke oothixo.

<span id="an_97:8">97:8</span> Iyeva, iyavuya iZiyon, Ziyagcoba iintombi
zakwaYuda, Ngenxa yemigwebo yakho, Yehova.

<span id="an_97:9">97:9</span> Ngokuba nguwe, Yehova, Osenyangweni phezu
kwehlabathi lonke; Unyukile kunene ngaphezu koothixo bonke.

<span id="an_97:10">97:10</span> Bathandi bakaYehova, kuthiyeni okubi.
Umgcini wemiphefumlo yabenceba bakhe Uya kubahlangula esandleni
sabangendawo.

<span id="an_97:11">97:11</span> Ukukhanya likuhlwayelelwe ilungisa,
Novuyo baluhlwayelelwe abantliziyo zithe tye.

<span id="an_97:12">97:12</span> Vuyani ngoYehova, malungisa, Nibulele
isikhumbuzo sakhe esingcwele.

<span id="an_98:1">98:1</span> Umhobe. Vumani kuYehova ingoma entsha,
Ngokuba wenze imisebenzi ebalulekileyo; Simzuzele uloyiso isandla sakhe
sokunene, nengalo yakhe engcwele.

<span id="an_98:2">98:2</span> Ulwazisile uYehova usindiso lwakhe,
Ubutyhilile emehlweni eentlanga ubulungisa bakhe.

<span id="an_98:3">98:3</span> Ukhumbule inceba yakhe nokunyanisa kwakhe
kwindlu kaSirayeli; Zilubonile zonke iziphelo zehlabathi usindiso
loThixo wethu.

<span id="an_98:4">98:4</span> Dumani kuYehova, nonke hlabathi,
Gqobhokelani ekumemeleleni, nibethe uhadi.

<span id="an_98:5">98:5</span> Mbetheleni uhadi uYehova, Uhadi nelizwi
lengoma;

<span id="an_98:6">98:6</span> Ngamaxilongo nezwi lesigodlo Dumani
phambi koKumkani uYehova.

<span id="an_98:7">98:7</span> Malugqume ulwandle nenzaliseko yalo,
Elimiweyo nabemi balo.

<span id="an_98:8">98:8</span> Imilambo mayibethe izandla, Zimemelele
kunye iintaba

<span id="an_98:9">98:9</span> Phambi koYehova, ngokuba esiza kugweba
ihlabathi. Uya kuligweba elimiweyo ngobulungisa, Izizwe ngokuthe tye.

<span id="an_99:1">99:1</span> UYehova nguKumkani, ziyagungqa izizwe;
Ulohlala ekerubhini, liyashukuma ihlabathi.

<span id="an_99:2">99:2</span> UYehova mkhulu eZiyon; Uphakamile
ngaphezu kwezizwe zonke.

<span id="an_99:3">99:3</span> Baya kulibulela igama lakho elikhulu
eloyikekayo; Ngokuba ungcwele yena.

<span id="an_99:4">99:4</span> Amandla okumkani athanda okusesikweni;
Uwazimasile wena ngokuthe tye; Wenze okusesikweni nobulungisa kwaYakobi
wena.

<span id="an_99:5">99:5</span> Mphakamiseni uYehova, uThixo wethu,
Niqubude esitulweni seenyawo zakhe; Ngokuba ungcwele yena.

<span id="an_99:6">99:6</span> OoMoses noAron phakathi kwababingeleli
bakhe, NoSamuweli phakathi kwabalinqulayo igama lakhe, Baye bebiza
kuYehova, wabaphendula yena.

<span id="an_99:7">99:7</span> Wathetha kubo esemqulwini welifu;
Bazigcina izingqino zakhe, Nommiselo awabanika wona.

<span id="an_99:8">99:8</span> Yehova, Thixo wethu, wabaphendula wena,
Waba nguThixo oxolelayo kubo, Ongoziphindezelayo iintlondi zabo.

<span id="an_99:9">99:9</span> Mphakamiseni uYehova, uThixo wethu,
Niqubude entabeni yakhe engcwele; Ngokuba ungcwele uYehova uThixo wethu.

<span id="an_100:1">100:1</span> Umhobe wombingelelo wokubulela. Dumani
kuYehova, nonke hlabathi.

<span id="an_100:2">100:2</span> Mkhonzeni uYehova nivuya; Yizani phambi
kwakhe nimemelela.

<span id="an_100:3">100:3</span> Yazini ukuba uYehova nguThixo yena;
Wasenza yena, asisithi; Singabantu bakhe nezimvu ezaluswa nguye.

<span id="an_100:4">100:4</span> Ngenani emasangweni akhe nibulela,
Ezintendelezweni zakhe nidumisa; Bulelani kuye, bongani igama lakhe.

<span id="an_100:5">100:5</span> Ngokuba uYehova ulungile, Inceba yakhe
ingunaphakade, Ukunyaniseka kwakhe kukwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana.

<span id="an_101:1">101:1</span> EkaDavide. Umhobe. Ndiya kuvuma
ngenceba nangomgwebo; Ndiya kukubethela uhadi, Yehova.

<span id="an_101:2">101:2</span> Ndiya kuqiqa indlela yengqibelelo; Uya
kuza nini na kum? Ndiya kuhamba ngengqibelelo yentliziyo yam Phakathi
kwendlu yam.

<span id="an_101:3">101:3</span> Andiyi kubeka phambi kwamehlo am Nto
inobutshijolo. Ukwenza ngokunxaxha ndikuthiyile, Akuyi kunamathela kum.

<span id="an_101:4">101:4</span> Intliziyo ejibilizayo iya kukhwelela
kude kum; Into embi andiyi kuyazi.

<span id="an_101:5">101:5</span> Omhlebayo ummelwane wakhe ngasese, Lowo
ndiya kumbhangisa. Omehlo aqwayingileyo, ontliziyo igungubeleyo, Lowo
andinakumthwala.

<span id="an_101:6">101:6</span> Amehlo am akwabanyanisayo ezweni, Ukuba
bandiphahle; Ohamba ngendlela yengqibelelo, Lowo makandilungiselele.

<span id="an_101:7">101:7</span> Akayi kuhlala phakathi kwendlu yam
Owenza inkohliso; Othetha ubuxoki akayi kuqina Phambi kwamehlo am.

<span id="an_101:8">101:8</span> Imiso ngemiso, ndiya kubabhangisa Bonke
abangendawo belizwe, Ukuze ndibanqumle emzini kaYehova Bonke abasebenzi
bobutshinga.

<span id="an_102:1">102:1</span> Umthandazo wolusizana xa atyhafileyo,
ephalaza iinkalazo zakhe phambi koYehova. Yehova, wuve umthandazo wam,
Kufike kuwe ukuzibika kwam.

<span id="an_102:2">102:2</span> Musa ukubusithelisa ubuso bakho kum
ngemini yokubandezelwa kwam, Ndithobele indlebe yakho; Ngemini
endidanduluka ngayo khawuleza undiphendule.

<span id="an_102:3">102:3</span> Ngokuba iyaphela imihla yam njengomsi;
Amathambo am avutha njengeziko.

<span id="an_102:4">102:4</span> Ibethwe yoma njengomfuno intliziyo yam,
Ngokuba ndilibele nokudla ukudla kwam.

<span id="an_102:5">102:5</span> Ngenxa yezwi lokugcuma kwam Amathambo
am atshele enyameni yam.

<span id="an_102:6">102:6</span> Ndifana nengcwangube yentlango,
Ndinjengesikhova sasemanxoweni.

<span id="an_102:7">102:7</span> Andilali; Ndinjengentaka eyodwa phezu
kwendlu.

<span id="an_102:8">102:8</span> Imini yonke ziyandingcikiva iintshaba
zam, Abandigezelayo bathuka ngam.

<span id="an_102:9">102:9</span> Ngokuba ndidle uthuthu njengesonka,
Into endiyiselayo ndiyiphithikeze nezililo,

<span id="an_102:10">102:10</span> Ngenxa yokubhabhama kwakho
noburhalarhume bakho; Ngokuba undifunqule wandilahla.

<span id="an_102:11">102:11</span> Imihla yam injengokoluka kwamathunzi;
Mna ndomile njengomfuno.

<span id="an_102:12">102:12</span> Ke wena, Yehova, uhleli ngonaphakade,
Inkumbuzo yakho ikwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana.

<span id="an_102:13">102:13</span> Uya kusuk’ ume, uyiphathe iZiyon
ngemfesane; Ngokuba lixesha lokuyibabala eli, ngokuba lifikile ixesha
elimisiweyo.

<span id="an_102:14">102:14</span> Ngokuba abakhonzi bakho bakholiswe
ngamatye ayo, Uthuli lwayo banofefe ngalo.

<span id="an_102:15">102:15</span> Ziya kuloyika iintlanga igama
likaYehova, Nookumkani bonke behlabathi ubuqaqawuli bakho;

<span id="an_102:16">102:16</span> Ngokuba eyakhile iZiyon uYehova,
Wabonakala ebuqaqawulini bakhe.

<span id="an_102:17">102:17</span> Uwubhekile umthandazo
wabachushuluzayo, Akawudela umthandazo wabo.

<span id="an_102:18">102:18</span> Oko kuya kubhalelwa isizukulwana
esizayo, Abantu abaza kudalwa badumise uYehova.

<span id="an_102:19">102:19</span> Ngokuba uqondele, esendaweni yakhe
ephezulu engcwele; Wondela ehlabathini esemazulwini uYehova,

<span id="an_102:20">102:20</span> Ukuba akuve ukugcuma
kwabakhonkxiweyo, Abakhulule oonyana bokufa;

<span id="an_102:21">102:21</span> Bancokole eZiyon ngegama likaYehova,
Ngendumiso yakhe eYerusalem;

<span id="an_102:22">102:22</span> Ekubuthelaneni kwezizwe ndawonye,
Nezikumkani, ukuba zikhonze uYehova.

<span id="an_102:23">102:23</span> Uwathobile endleleni amandla am,
Uyinqamle imihla yam.

<span id="an_102:24">102:24</span> Ndithi, Thixo wam, musa ukundisusa
phakathi kwemihla yam. Ikwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana iminyaka yakho.

<span id="an_102:25">102:25</span> Waliseka kudala ihlabathi; Lisisenzo
sezandla zakho izulu.

<span id="an_102:26">102:26</span> Ezo zinto ziya kudaka, wena ke ume;
Zona zonke ziya konakala njengengubo, Wozigugisa njengesambatho, ziguge;

<span id="an_102:27">102:27</span> Ke wena uhleli unguwe, Iminyaka yakho
ayinakuphela.

<span id="an_102:28">102:28</span> Oonyana babakhonzi bakho baya
kuhlala, Imbewu yabo izimaseke phambi kwakho.

<span id="an_103:1">103:1</span> EkaDavide. Mbonge uYehova, mphefumlo
wam, Ilibonge igama lakhe elingcwele into yonke engaphakathi kwam.

<span id="an_103:2">103:2</span> Mbonge uYehova, mphefumlo wam,
Ungayilibali yonke impatho yakhe entle:

<span id="an_103:3">103:3</span> Uloxolela bonke ubugwenxa bakho;
Ulophilisa zonke izifo zakho;

<span id="an_103:4">103:4</span> Ulokhulula ubomi bakho esihogweni,
Akuthi jize ngenceba nemfesane;

<span id="an_103:5">103:5</span> Lo uwuzalisayo umlomo wakho ngento
elungileyo, Buhlaziyeke ubutsha bakho njengobokhozi.

<span id="an_103:6">103:6</span> NguYehova umenzi wemisebenzi
yobulungisa, Nezigwebo ngenxa yabacudisiweyo bonke;

<span id="an_103:7">103:7</span> Umazisi weendlela zakhe kuMoses,
Wezenzo zakhe ezincamisayo koonyana bakaSirayeli.

<span id="an_103:8">103:8</span> Unemfesane enobabalo uYehova, Uzeka
kade umsindo, mkhulu ngenceba.

<span id="an_103:9">103:9</span> Akaphiki kuphele, Akawugcini umsindo
ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_103:10">103:10</span> Akenzi kuthi ngokwezono zethu,
Akasiphathi ngokobugwenxa bethu;

<span id="an_103:11">103:11</span> Ngokuba injengokuphakama kwezulu
phezu komhlaba, Ukuba namandla, inceba yakhe kwabamoyikayo;

<span id="an_103:12">103:12</span> Kunjengokuba kude kwempumalanga
entshonalanga, Ukulukhwelelisa kwakhe kuthi ukreqo lwethu;

<span id="an_103:13">103:13</span> Kunjengokusikwa yimfesane koyise
kubantwana, Ukusikwa yimfesane kukaYehova kwabamoyikayo.

<span id="an_103:14">103:14</span> Ngokuba uyakwazi yena ukubunjwa
kwethu, Ekhumbula ukuba siluthuli.

<span id="an_103:15">103:15</span> Hayi, umntu! Injengotyani imihla
yakhe; Njengentyantyambo yasendle, kunjalo ukutyatyamba kwakhe.

<span id="an_103:16">103:16</span> Xa uthe umoya wadlula kuyo, ayibikho,
Ingabi sazana nayo indawo yayo.

<span id="an_103:17">103:17</span> Ke yona inceba kaYehova
ikwabamoyikayo, kususela kwaphakade kude kuse ephakadeni, Nobulungisa
bakhe bukoonyana boonyana;

<span id="an_103:18">103:18</span> Kwabawugcinileyo umnqophiso wakhe,
Kwabazikhumbulayo iziyalezo zakhe ukuba bazenze.

<span id="an_103:19">103:19</span> UYehova uyizinzisile emazulwini
itrone yakhe, Ubukumkani bakhe bulawula into yonke.

<span id="an_103:20">103:20</span> Mbongeni uYehova, nina zithunywa
zakhe, Magorha omeleleyo, alenzayo ilizwi lakhe, Ephulaphula isandi
selizwi lakhe.

<span id="an_103:21">103:21</span> Mbongeni uYehova, nonke mikhosi
yakhe, Balungiseleli bakhe, benzi bokuthanda kwakhe.

<span id="an_103:22">103:22</span> Mbongeni uYehova, nonke zenzo zakhe,
Ezindaweni zonke zobukumkani bakhe. Mbonge uYehova, mphefumlo wam.

<span id="an_104:1">104:1</span> Mbonge uYehova, mphefumlo wam. Yehova,
Thixo wam, umkhulu kakhulu; Wambethe indili nobungangamela.

<span id="an_104:2">104:2</span> Ulothi wambu ukukhanya njengengubo.
Ulolaneka izulu njengelengalenga lentente;

<span id="an_104:3">104:3</span> Ulohlanganisa emanzini imiqadi
yamagumbi akhe aphezulu; Ulowenza amafu inqwelo yakhe, Ulohamba
ngamaphiko omoya;

<span id="an_104:4">104:4</span> Ulowenza izithunywa zakhe imimoya,
Abalungiseleli bakhe umlilo olenyayo.

<span id="an_104:5">104:5</span> Waliseka ihlabathi phezu kwemimiso
yalo, Ukuba lingashukunyiswa naphakade kanaphakade.

<span id="an_104:6">104:6</span> Waligubungela ngamanzi anzongonzongo
njengesambatho, Ema amanzi phezu kweentaba.

<span id="an_104:7">104:7</span> Ekukhalimeni kwakho asaba, Ezwini
lendudumo yakho abaleka buphuthuphuthu;

<span id="an_104:8">104:8</span> Kwenyuka iintaba, kwehla izihlambo, Aya
kuloo ndawo ubuwasekele yona.

<span id="an_104:9">104:9</span> Wamisa umda ukuba angegqithi, Angabuye
awugubungele umhlaba.

<span id="an_104:10">104:10</span> Ulothuma imithombo iye ezihlanjeni;
Ihamba phakathi kweentaba;

<span id="an_104:11">104:11</span> Iseza zonke iinyamakazi zasendle;
Amaesile asendle aqabula inxano lawo.

<span id="an_104:12">104:12</span> Kuhlala phezu kwayo iintaka zezulu,
Zitsholoza phakathi kwamasebe;

<span id="an_104:13">104:13</span> Uloseza iintaba kumagumbi akhe
aphezulu; Uyahlutha umhlaba ziziqhamo zezenzo zakho.

<span id="an_104:14">104:14</span> Ulontshulisela iinkomo utyani,
Nomfuno wokunceda umntu; Ukuze kuphume isonka emhlabeni.

<span id="an_104:15">104:15</span> Iwayini iyivuyise intliziyo yomntu;
Bukhazimle ubuso ngeoli, Isonka siyixhase intliziyo yomntu.

<span id="an_104:16">104:16</span> Iyahlutha imithi kaYehova, Imisedare
yaseLebhanon awayityalayo,

<span id="an_104:17">104:17</span> Apho zakhela khona iintaka; Ingwamza,
isemisipresini indlu yayo.

<span id="an_104:18">104:18</span> Iintaba zona ezo ziphakamileyo
zezamagogo, Amawa azimela iimbila.

<span id="an_104:19">104:19</span> Inyanga wayenzela amaxesha ayo,
Ilanga liyakwazi ukutshona kwalo.

<span id="an_104:20">104:20</span> Wenza ubumnyama wena, kube sebusuku,
Ashukume ngabo onke amarhamncwa ehlathi.

<span id="an_104:21">104:21</span> Iingonyama ezintsha zigqumela
ukuqwenga, Zifuna ukudla kwazo kuThixo.

<span id="an_104:22">104:22</span> Lakuthi chapha ilanga,
ziyahlanganisana, Zibuthume ezikhundleni zazo.

<span id="an_104:23">104:23</span> Uyaphuma umntu aye emsebenzini wakhe
Nasenkonzweni yakhe, ahlwise.

<span id="an_104:24">104:24</span> Hayi, ukuba zininzi izenzo zakho,
Yehova! Zonke ziphela uzenze ngobululumko; Uzele umhlaba zizidalwa
zakho.

<span id="an_104:25">104:25</span> Nalo ulwandle lulukhulu, lubanzi
ngeenxa zombini; Kulapho kuzinambuzane zingenakubalwa, Ezincinane
kwanezikhulu izinto eziphilileyo.

<span id="an_104:26">104:26</span> Kulapho kuhamba iinqanawa; Nango
umnenga owawubumbela ukudlala kulo.

<span id="an_104:27">104:27</span> Zonke ezo nto ziphela zikhangele
kuwe, Ukuba uzinike ukudla kwazo ngexesha elililo.

<span id="an_104:28">104:28</span> Uyazinika, ziyachola; Uyasivula
isandla sakho, ziyahlutha kokulungileyo.

<span id="an_104:29">104:29</span> Uyabusithelisa ubuso bakho,
ziyakhwankqiswa; Uyawuhlanganisa umoya wazo, ziphume umphefumlo,
Zibuyele eluthulini lwazo.

<span id="an_104:30">104:30</span> Uthuma umoya wakho, ziyadalwa,
Ubuhlaziye ubuso bomhlaba.

<span id="an_104:31">104:31</span> Ubuqaqawuli bukaYehova mabube
ngunaphakade; UYehova makavuye ngezenzo zakhe;

<span id="an_104:32">104:32</span> Ulobheka emhlabeni, uzamazame;
Uchukumisa iintaba, ziqhume.

<span id="an_104:33">104:33</span> Ndiya kuvuma kuYehova lo gama ndidla
ubomi, Ndiya kumbethela uhadi uThixo wam ekubeni ndingokhoyo.

<span id="an_104:34">104:34</span> Makube nencasa kuye ukucamngca kwam;
Mna ndiya kuvuya ngoYehova.

<span id="an_104:35">104:35</span> Mabagqitywe ehlabathini aboni,
Bangabi sabakho abangendawo. Mbonge uYehova, mphefumlo wam, Haleluya!

<span id="an_105:1">105:1</span> Bulelani kuYehova, nqulani igama lakhe;
Yazisani ezizweni izenzo zakhe ezincamisileyo.

<span id="an_105:2">105:2</span> Vumani kuye, mbetheleni uhadi; Xoxani
ngemisebenzi yakhe yonke ebalulekileyo.

<span id="an_105:3">105:3</span> Qhayisani ngegama lakhe elingcwele;
Mayivuye intliziyo yabamquqelayo uYehova.

<span id="an_105:4">105:4</span> Ngxamelani uYehova namandla akhe;
Funani ubuso bakhe ngamaxesha onke.

<span id="an_105:5">105:5</span> Khumbulani imisebenzi yakhe
ebalulekileyo awayenzayo, Izimanga zakhe, nezigwebo zomlomo wakhe,

<span id="an_105:6">105:6</span> Mbewu ka-Abraham, yomkhonzi wakhe,
Nyana bakaYakobi, banyulwa bakhe.

<span id="an_105:7">105:7</span> NguYehova uThixo wethu yena;
Zisehlabathini lonke izigwebo zakhe.

<span id="an_105:8">105:8</span> Uwukhumbula ngonaphakade umnqophiso
wakhe, Ilizwi awalimisela iwaka lezizukulwana;

<span id="an_105:9">105:9</span> Awanqophisana ngalo noAbraham,
Awalifungela uIsake;

<span id="an_105:10">105:10</span> Awalimisayo ukuba libe ngummiselo
kuYakobi, Libe ngumnqophiso ongunaphakade kuSirayeli;

<span id="an_105:11">105:11</span> Esithi, Ndikunika ilizwe lakwaKanan,
Libe licandelo lelifa lenu;

<span id="an_105:12">105:12</span> Besengamadoda ambalwa, Bebancinane,
bengabaphambukeli kulo.

<span id="an_105:13">105:13</span> Babehamba besuka kolunye uhlanga,
baye kolunye uhlanga, Besuka kobunye ubukumkani, baye kwabanye abantu.

<span id="an_105:14">105:14</span> Akavumelanga mntu ukuba abacudise,
Wohlwaya ookumkani ngenxa yabo;

<span id="an_105:15">105:15</span> Esithi, Musani ukubachukumisa
abathanjiswa bam, Musani ukubaphatha kakubi abaprofeti bam.

<span id="an_105:16">105:16</span> Wabiza indlala, yeza phezu kwelizwe,
Wawaphula wonke umsimelelo osisonka.

<span id="an_105:17">105:17</span> Wathuma indoda phambi kwabo;
Kwathengiswa ngoYosefu, waba likhoboka.

<span id="an_105:18">105:18</span> Bazicinezela iinyawo zakhe
ngamakhamandela, Wafika umphefumlo wakhe esinyithini;

<span id="an_105:19">105:19</span> Kwada kwalixesha lokufika kwelizwi
lakhe, Intetho kaYehova yamnyibilikisa.

<span id="an_105:20">105:20</span> Ukumkani wathuma, wamkhulula,
Umlawuli wezizwe wamvulela;

<span id="an_105:21">105:21</span> Wamenza inkosi yendlu yakhe, Umlawuli
wemfuyo yakhe yonke,

<span id="an_105:22">105:22</span> Ukuba abakhonkxe abathetheli bakhe
ngokuzithandela kwakhe, Amadoda akhe amakhulu awafundise ubulumko.

<span id="an_105:23">105:23</span> Waza uSirayeli waya eYiputa, UYakobi
waphambukela ezweni lakwaHam.

<span id="an_105:24">105:24</span> Wabaqhamisa kakhulu abantu bakhe,
Wabomeleza ngaphezu kwababandezeli babo.

<span id="an_105:25">105:25</span> Wazijika iintliziyo zabo, ukuba
babathiye abantu bakhe, Babaqhathanisele abakhonzi bakhe.

<span id="an_105:26">105:26</span> Wathuma uMoses, umkhonzi wakhe,
NoAron awamnyulayo.

<span id="an_105:27">105:27</span> Bazenza kubo iindawo zemiqondiso
yakhe, Nezimanga zakhe ezweni lakwaHam.

<span id="an_105:28">105:28</span> Wathumela ubumnyama, kwaba mnyama;
Ababa nakuwaphikisa amazwi akhe.

<span id="an_105:29">105:29</span> Wawaguqula amanzi abo, aba ligazi,
Wazibulala iintlanzi zabo.

<span id="an_105:30">105:30</span> Ilizwe labo lanyakazela amasele
Ezingontsini zookumkani babo.

<span id="an_105:31">105:31</span> Wathetha, zafika izibawu,
Iingcongconi, emideni yabo yonke.

<span id="an_105:32">105:32</span> Wabanika isichotho, saba yimvula;
Umlilo walenya ezweni labo.

<span id="an_105:33">105:33</span> Wayibetha imidiliya yabo nemikhiwane
yabo, Wayishwaqa imithi yemida yabo.

<span id="an_105:34">105:34</span> Wathetha, kwafika iinkumbi ezandayo,
Nezikhothululayo, into engenakubalwa;

<span id="an_105:35">105:35</span> Zayidla imifuno yonke ezweni labo,
Zazidla iziqhamo zomhlaba wabo.

<span id="an_105:36">105:36</span> Waza wababulala bonke abamazibulo
ezweni labo, Intlahlela yamandla abo onke.

<span id="an_105:37">105:37</span> Wabakhupha ke abakhe benesilivere
negolide, Akwabakho ukhubekayo ezizweni zakhe.

<span id="an_105:38">105:38</span> Lavuya iYiputa ekuphumeni kwabo,
Ngokuba lifikelwe kukunkwantyisa kwabo.

<span id="an_105:39">105:39</span> Waneka ilifu lokubasitha, Nomlilo
wokukhanyisa ebusuku.

<span id="an_105:40">105:40</span> Babiza, wazisa izagwityi,
Wabahluthisa nangesonka sasezulwini.

<span id="an_105:41">105:41</span> Wavula iliwa, abaleka amanzi, Ahamba
engumlambo emqwebedwini.

<span id="an_105:42">105:42</span> Ngokuba wakhumbula ilizwi lakhe
elingcwele, Wakhumbula uAbraham umkhonzi wakhe.

<span id="an_105:43">105:43</span> Wabakhupha abantu bakhe benemihlali,
Abanyulwa bakhe bememelela.

<span id="an_105:44">105:44</span> Wabanika amazwe eentlanga, Bayihlutha
inzuzo yokwaphuka kwezizwe,

<span id="an_105:45">105:45</span> Ukuze bayigcine imimiselo yakhe,
Bayibambe imiyalelo yakhe. Haleluya!

<span id="an_106:1">106:1</span> Haleluya! Bulelani kuYehova, ngokuba
elungile, Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_106:2">106:2</span> Ngubani na onokuzixela izenzo zobugorha
bukaYehova, Onokuyivakalisa yonke indumiso yakhe?

<span id="an_106:3">106:3</span> Hayi, uyolo lwabaligcinayo isiko,
Lwabenza ubulungisa ngamaxesha onke!

<span id="an_106:4">106:4</span> Ndikhumbule, Yehova, ekwenzeni kwakho
isisa kubantu bakho; Ndiyelele ngosindiso lwakho,

<span id="an_106:5">106:5</span> Ukuze ndibone inyhweba yabanyulwa
bakho, Ndivuye ekuvuyeni kohlanga lwakho, Ndiqhayise kunye nelifa lakho.

<span id="an_106:6">106:6</span> Sonile, thina noobawo; Senze ubugwenxa,
senze okungendawo.

<span id="an_106:7">106:7</span> Oobawo abayiqiqanga eYiputa imisebenzi
yakho ebalulekileyo; Ababukhumbulanga ubuninzi beenceba zakho; Baphika
elwandle, eLwandle oluBomvu.

<span id="an_106:8">106:8</span> Wabasindisa ngenxa yegama lakhe, Ukuze
abazise ubugorha bakhe.

<span id="an_106:9">106:9</span> Walukhalimela uLwandle oluBomvu, loma,
Wabahambisa emanzini anzongonzongo kwanga kusentlango.

<span id="an_106:10">106:10</span> Wabasindisa esandleni sobathiyayo,
Wabakhulula esandleni sotshaba.

<span id="an_106:11">106:11</span> Amanzi abagubungela ababandezeli
babo, Akwasala namnye kubo.

<span id="an_106:12">106:12</span> Bakholwa ke ngamazwi akhe, Bayivuma
indumiso yakhe.

<span id="an_106:13">106:13</span> Kanti bahle bazilibala izenzo zakhe,
Abalilinda icebo lakhe.

<span id="an_106:14">106:14</span> Bakhanukile entlango, Bamlinga uThixo
enkangala.

<span id="an_106:15">106:15</span> Wabanika abakubizayo; Wathumela
ukungcumbeka emphefumlweni wabo.

<span id="an_106:16">106:16</span> Bamenzela umona uMoses eminqubeni,
NoAron ongcwele kaYehova.

<span id="an_106:17">106:17</span> Wavuleka umhlaba, wamginya uDatan,
Waliselela ibandla lika-Abhiram;

<span id="an_106:18">106:18</span> Umlilo walitshisa ibandla labo,
Amalangatye abalenya abangendawo.

<span id="an_106:19">106:19</span> Benza ithole eHorebhe, Baqubuda
emfanekisweni otyhidiweyo.

<span id="an_106:20">106:20</span> Balwananisa uzuko lwabo Ngento
emilise okwenkomo edla utyani.

<span id="an_106:21">106:21</span> Bamlibala uThixo, umsindisi wabo,
Owenza imisebenzi emikhulu eYiputa;

<span id="an_106:22">106:22</span> Imisebenzi ebalulekileyo ezweni
lakwaHam, Imisebenzi eyoyikekayo eLwandle oluBomvu.

<span id="an_106:23">106:23</span> Wathi uya kubatshabalalisa, Koko
wesukayo uMoses, umnyulwa wakhe, Wema ethubeni phambi kwakhe, Ebuyisa
ubushushu bakhe, ukuba angatshabalalisi.

<span id="an_106:24">106:24</span> Balicekisa ilizwe elinqwenelekayo,
Abakholwa lilizwi lakhe,

<span id="an_106:25">106:25</span> Bakrokra ezintenteni zabo,
Abaliphulaphula izwi likaYehova.

<span id="an_106:26">106:26</span> Wabaphakamisela isandla sakhe,
Wafungela ukuba abawise entlango;

<span id="an_106:27">106:27</span> Ayiwise imbewu yabo phakathi
kweentlanga, Abachithachithe emazweni.

<span id="an_106:28">106:28</span> Bazibandakanya noBhahali-pehore,
Badla imibingelelo yabafileyo,

<span id="an_106:29">106:29</span> Bamqumbisa ngeentlondi zabo;
Sagaleleka phakathi kwabo isibetho.

<span id="an_106:30">106:30</span> Wesuka wema uPinehasi, walamla;
Sathintelwa isibetho.

<span id="an_106:31">106:31</span> Oko kwabalelwa kuye ekuthini
bubulungisa Izizukulwana ngezizukulwana kude kuse ephakadeni.

<span id="an_106:32">106:32</span> Bamqumbisa emanzini aseMeribha,
Kwehla ububi kuMoses ngenxa yabo;

<span id="an_106:33">106:33</span> Ngokuba bawuphikisa umoya wakhe,
Waphololoza ke ngomlomo wakhe.

<span id="an_106:34">106:34</span> Abazitshabalalisa izizwe, Awayethethe
ngazo kubo uYehova;

<span id="an_106:35">106:35</span> Baxubana neentlanga ezo, Bafunda
izenzo zazo;

<span id="an_106:36">106:36</span> Bakhonza izithixo zazo, Yaba
sisirhintyelo kubo.

<span id="an_106:37">106:37</span> Babingelela ngoonyana babo
nangeentombi zabo kwiidemon;

<span id="an_106:38">106:38</span> Baphalaza igazi elimsulwa, Igazi
loonyana babo neleentombi zabo, Ababingelela ngabo kwizithixo
zakwaKanan; Lahlanjelwa ilizwe ngamagazi.

<span id="an_106:39">106:39</span> Baba ziinqambi ngezenzo zabo,
Bahenyuza ngeentlondi zabo.

<span id="an_106:40">106:40</span> Wavutha ke umsindo kaYehova kubantu
bakhe, Laba lisikizi kuye ilifa lakhe.

<span id="an_106:41">106:41</span> Wabanikela ezandleni zeentlanga,
Balawulwa ngababathiyileyo.

<span id="an_106:42">106:42</span> Zabaxina iintshaba zabo, Bathotyelwa
phantsi kwezandla zazo.

<span id="an_106:43">106:43</span> Zibe zininzi izihlandlo ebahlangula;
Ke bona bamphikisa ngamaqhinga abo, Bonakala bubugwenxa babo.

<span id="an_106:44">106:44</span> Noko ke wakunonelela ukubandezelwa
kwabo, Akuva ukuhlahlamba kwabo.

<span id="an_106:45">106:45</span> Wawukhumbula ngenxa yabo umnqophiso
wakhe, Wazohlwaya ngenxa yobuninzi beenceba zakhe.

<span id="an_106:46">106:46</span> Wabafumanisa imfesane Phambi kwabo
bonke abaye bebathimbile.

<span id="an_106:47">106:47</span> Sisindise, Yehova, Thixo wethu,
Sibuthe ezintlangeni, Ukuze sibulele kwigama lakho elingcwele, Sizingce
ngendumiso yakho.

<span id="an_106:48">106:48</span> Makabongwe uYehova, uThixo
kaSirayeli, Kususela kwaphakade kude kuse ephakadeni. Mabathi bonke
abantu, Amen. Haleluya!

<span id="an_107:1">107:1</span> Bulelani kuYehova, ngokuba elungile,
Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_107:2">107:2</span> Mabatsho abakhululwa bakaYehova,
Awabakhululayo esandleni sombandezeli;

<span id="an_107:3">107:3</span> Wababutha emazweni, Empumalanga
nasentshonalanga, Entla naselwandle.

<span id="an_107:4">107:4</span> Badinga entlango, endleleni esenkanga,
la, Abafumana mzi wakuhlala.

<span id="an_107:5">107:5</span> Belambile, benxaniwe, Watyhafa phakathi
kwabo umphefumlo wabo.

<span id="an_107:6">107:6</span> Bakhala ke kuYehova embandezelweni
yabo, Wabahlangula ekucuthekeni kwabo;

<span id="an_107:7">107:7</span> Wabanyathelisa endleleni ethe tye,
Ukuba baye kumzi wokuhlala.

<span id="an_107:8">107:8</span> Mabayibulele kuYehova inceba yakhe,
Nemisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo koonyana babantu!

<span id="an_107:9">107:9</span> Kuba ewuhluthisile umphefumlo
otshobayo, Wawuzalisa ngokulungileyo umphefumlo olambileyo.

<span id="an_107:10">107:10</span> Behleli emnyameni nasethunzini
lokufa, Bekhonkxwe yimbandezelo nasisinyithi,

<span id="an_107:11">107:11</span> Ngokuba bephikise amazwi kaThixo,
Belitshitshisa icebo lOsenyangweni:

<span id="an_107:12">107:12</span> Wayithoba intliziyo yabo
ngokubasebenzisa kanzima; Bakhubeka, akwabakho mncedi.

<span id="an_107:13">107:13</span> Bakhala ke kuYehova embandezelweni
yabo; Wabasindisa ekucuthekeni kwabo.

<span id="an_107:14">107:14</span> Wabakhupha emnyameni nasethunzini
lokufa, Waziqhawula iimbophelelo zabo.

<span id="an_107:15">107:15</span> Mabayibulele kuYehova inceba yakhe,
Nemisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo koonyana babantu!

<span id="an_107:16">107:16</span> Kuba ezaphule iingcango zobhedu,
Wayixakaxa imivalo yesinyithi.

<span id="an_107:17">107:17</span> Abamathileyo, ngenxa yendlela
yokukreqa kwabo, Nangenxa yobugwenxa babo, bacinezelwa;

<span id="an_107:18">107:18</span> Konke ukudla kwaba lisikizi
kumphefumlo wabo, Bafika emasangweni okufa.

<span id="an_107:19">107:19</span> Bakhala ke kuYehova embandezelweni
yabo, Wabasindisa ekucuthekeni kwabo.

<span id="an_107:20">107:20</span> Wathumela ilizwi lakhe, wabaphilisa,
Wabasiza ezihogweni zabo.

<span id="an_107:21">107:21</span> Mabayibulele kuYehova inceba yakhe,
Nemisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo koonyana babantu!

<span id="an_107:22">107:22</span> Mababingelele imibingelelo yombulelo,
Bancokole ngezenzo zakhe bememelela.

<span id="an_107:23">107:23</span> Abaya elwandle ngeenqanawa, Benze
ishishini emanzini amaninzi,

<span id="an_107:24">107:24</span> Bazibona bona izenzo zikaYehova,
Nemisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo enzulwini.

<span id="an_107:25">107:25</span> Watsho, wavusa umoya ovuthuzayo,
Waphakamisa amaza ayo.

<span id="an_107:26">107:26</span> Banyuka basinga ezulwini, behla
basinga emanzini enzonzobila; Umphefumlo wabo uthe amandla bububi.

<span id="an_107:27">107:27</span> Bathendeleka, bahexa njengenxila,
Butshone bonke ubulumko babo.

<span id="an_107:28">107:28</span> Bakhala ke kuYehova embandezelweni
yabo Wabakhupha ekucuthekeni kwabo.

<span id="an_107:29">107:29</span> Ukumisile ukuvuthuza, kwathi cwaka,
Amaza ayo azola;

<span id="an_107:30">107:30</span> Bavuya ke, kuba edambile; Wabafikisa
echwebeni abalilangazelelayo.

<span id="an_107:31">107:31</span> Mabayibulele kuYehova inceba yakhe,
Nemisebenzi yakhe ebalulekileyo koonyana babantu!

<span id="an_107:32">107:32</span> Mabamphakamise ebandleni labantu,
Bamdumise embuthweni yamadoda amakhulu.

<span id="an_107:33">107:33</span> Uyenze imilambo yaba yintlango,
Namathende amanzi aba ngumhlaba onxaniweyo;

<span id="an_107:34">107:34</span> Ilizwe elineziqhamo laba leletyuwa,
Ngenxa yezinto ezimbi zabemi balo.

<span id="an_107:35">107:35</span> Uyenze intlango yaba lidike
elinamanzi, Ilizwe elingumqwebedu laba ngamathende amanzi.

<span id="an_107:36">107:36</span> Wabahlalisa khona abalambileyo,
Bamisa umzi wokuhlala.

<span id="an_107:37">107:37</span> Bahlwayela amasimi, batyala
izidiliya, Bavelisa iziqhamo, baba nongeniselo.

<span id="an_107:38">107:38</span> Wabasikelela, banda kunene, Iinkomo
zabo akazinciphisa.

<span id="an_107:39">107:39</span> Bancipha, basibekeka Ngokukhanyangwa
bububi nesingqala.

<span id="an_107:40">107:40</span> Uwagalele ngendelo amanene,
Wawadingisa enyanyeni, kungekho ndlela.

<span id="an_107:41">107:41</span> Walisa engxondeni ihlwempu, kude
nengcinezelo, Walenzela imizalwana yanjengomhlambi.

<span id="an_107:42">107:42</span> Baya kubona abathe tye, bavuye, Bonke
ubugqwetha buvale umlomo.

<span id="an_107:43">107:43</span> Lowo ulumkileyo makazigcine ezi
ndawo, Azigqale iinceba zikaYehova.

<span id="an_108:1">108:1</span> Ingoma. Umhobe kaDavide. Izimasekile
intliziyo yam, Thixo, Ndiya kuvuma, ndibethe uhadi, Kwanozuko lwam.

<span id="an_108:2">108:2</span> Vukani, mrhubhe nohadi; Ndiya
kusiphangela isifingo.

<span id="an_108:3">108:3</span> Ndiya kubulela kuwe phakathi kwezizwe,
Yehova, Ndikubethele uhadi phakathi kwezizwe.

<span id="an_108:4">108:4</span> Ngokuba inkulu ngaphezu kwezulu inceba
yakho, Yada yesa esibhakabhakeni inyaniso yakho.

<span id="an_108:5">108:5</span> Ziphakamise ngaphezu kwezulu, Thixo,
Bube phezu kwehlabathi lonke ubuqaqawuli bakho.

<span id="an_108:6">108:6</span> Ukuze zihlangulwe iintanda zakho,
Sindisa ngesandla sakho sokunene, undiphendule.

<span id="an_108:7">108:7</span> UThixo uthethe engcwele; mandivuyelele,
Ndimabe uShekem, ndiyilinganisele intili yaseSukoti.

<span id="an_108:8">108:8</span> Ngowam uGiliyadi, ngowam uManase,
UEfrayim sisigcina-ntloko sam, UYuda yintonga yam yommiselo;

<span id="an_108:9">108:9</span> UMowabhi sisitya sam sokuhlambela,
Ndiyiphosa kuEdom imbadada yam; Ndiduma ngelamaFilisti.

<span id="an_108:10">108:10</span> Ngubani na owondisa emzini
onqatyisiweyo, Ngubani na owondikhaphela kwaEdom?

<span id="an_108:11">108:11</span> Asinguwe na, Thixo, lo usihlambileyo?
Akwaphuma, Thixo, nemikhosi yethu.

<span id="an_108:12">108:12</span> Sincede kumbandezeli wethu; Alunto
yanto usindiso lomntu.

<span id="an_108:13">108:13</span> NgoThixo siya kweyisa, Abagqushe yena
ababandezeli bethu.

<span id="an_109:1">109:1</span> Kumongameli; ekaDavide. Umhobe. Thixo
wendumiso yam, musa ukuthi tu;

<span id="an_109:2">109:2</span> Ngokuba bandakhamisele umlomo
ongendawo, nomlomo onenkohliso; Bathetha ngam ngolwimi lobuxoki.

<span id="an_109:3">109:3</span> Bandijikele ngeentetho zentiyo; Balwa
nam ngelize.

<span id="an_109:4">109:4</span> Ekubeni mna ndibathanda, bona
bayandichasa, Ndibe mna ndithandaza.

<span id="an_109:5">109:5</span> Endaweni yobulungisa bandibuyekeza
ngobubi; Ekubeni mna ndibathanda, bona bayandithiya.

<span id="an_109:6">109:6</span> Misa ongendawo, abe ngumveleli wakhe,
Eme uSathana ngasekunene kwakhe.

<span id="an_109:7">109:7</span> Ekuthethweni kwetyala makaphume
engongendawo, Nomthandazo wakhe ube sisono.

<span id="an_109:8">109:8</span> Imihla yakhe mayibe mbalwa,
Mabuthatyathwe ngomnye ubuveleli bakhe.

<span id="an_109:9">109:9</span> Oonyana bakhe mababe ziinkedama,
Nomkakhe abe ngumhlolokazi;

<span id="an_109:10">109:10</span> Babhadule bebhadula oonyana bakhe,
becela, Bengqiba, bekude namanxuwa akowabo.

<span id="an_109:11">109:11</span> Umboleki-mali makakushwankathele
konke anako, Abasemzini baphange ukuxelenga kwakhe.

<span id="an_109:12">109:12</span> Makungabikho wolulela nceba kuye,
Kungabikho uzibabalayo iinkedama zakhe.

<span id="an_109:13">109:13</span> Izivela-mva zakhe mazibe
zezokunqunyulwa, Igama lazo licinywe esizukulwaneni esizayo.

<span id="an_109:14">109:14</span> Mabukhunjulwe nguYehova ubugwenxa
booyise, Singacinywa isono sonina.

<span id="an_109:15">109:15</span> Masibe phambi koYehova ngamaxesha
onke, Akunqumle ehlabathini ukukhunjulwa kwabo;

<span id="an_109:16">109:16</span> Ngenxa enokuba engakukhumbulanga
ukwenza inceba, Etshutshise indoda elusizana, Elihlwempu, enentliziyo
eyothukileyo, ukuba ayibulale.

<span id="an_109:17">109:17</span> Ewe, wathanda ukuqalekisa,
kwamfikela; Akakufuna ukusikelela, kwakhwelela kude kuye.

<span id="an_109:18">109:18</span> Wambatha ukuqalekisa kwanga yingubo
yakhe, Kwangena embilinini wakhe njengamanzi, Nanjengeoli emathanjeni
akhe.

<span id="an_109:19">109:19</span> Makube njengengubo kuye, azithe wambu
ngayo, Kube luqhwemesha, alunxibe amaxesha onke.

<span id="an_109:20">109:20</span> Nguwo lowo umvuzo wabandichasayo,
ophuma kuYehova, Wabathetha okubi ngomphefumlo wam.

<span id="an_109:21">109:21</span> Ke wena Yehova, Nkosi, ndenzele
ngenxa yegama lakho; Ngokokuba ilungile inceba yakho; ndihlangule.

<span id="an_109:22">109:22</span> Ngokuba ndilusizana, ndilihlwempu,
Intliziyo yam ihlatyiwe phakathi kwam.

<span id="an_109:23">109:23</span> Ndinjengethunzi xa lolukayo,
ndiyemka; Ndiphetshethwa njengenkumbi.

<span id="an_109:24">109:24</span> Amadolo am ayagexa kukuzila ukudla,
Nenyama yam ibhityile, tu ukutyeba.

<span id="an_109:25">109:25</span> Ndithe ndasisingcikivo kubo;
Bendibona, bahlunguzela intloko.

<span id="an_109:26">109:26</span> Ndincede, Yehova, Thixo wam,
Ndisindise ngokwenceba yakho;

<span id="an_109:27">109:27</span> Bazi ukuba sisandla sakho eso, Ukuba
kukwenza kwakho, Yehova.

<span id="an_109:28">109:28</span> Bayaqalekisa aba, uyasikelela wena;
Besukile bema, baya kudana; uya kubuya yena umkhonzi wakho.

<span id="an_109:29">109:29</span> Abandichasayo baya kwambatha ihlazo,
Bazithi wambu ukudana njengengubo yokwaleka.

<span id="an_109:30">109:30</span> Ndiya kubulela kakhulu kuYehova
ngomlomo wam, Ndimdumise phakathi kwabaninzi;

<span id="an_109:31">109:31</span> Kuba emi ekunene kolihlwempu, Ukuba
amsindise kwabawugwebayo umphefumlo wakhe.

<span id="an_110:1">110:1</span> EkaDavide. Umhobe. Utsho uYehova
eNkosini yam ukuthi, Hlala ngasekunene kwam, Ndide iintshaba zakho
ndizenze Isitulo seenyawo zakho.

<span id="an_110:2">110:2</span> Intonga yamandla akho uya kuyithumela
uYehova, ivela eZiyon, esithi, Yiba nobukhosi phakathi kweentshaba
zakho.

<span id="an_110:3">110:3</span> Abantu bakho baya kuzinikela
ngeentliziyo, ngemini yakho yokuphuma umkhosi; Bebethe ezingcwele,
ekuphumeni kwesifingo, Uza kuwe umbethe womlisela wakho.

<span id="an_110:4">110:4</span> Ufungile uYehova, akayi kuzohlwaya;
uthe, Ungumbingeleli ngonaphakade wena Ngokohlobo lukaMelkitsedeke.

<span id="an_110:5">110:5</span> INkosi ngasekunene kwakho Iya kuphalusa
ookumkani ngemini yomsindo wayo.

<span id="an_110:6">110:6</span> Iya kugweba phakathi kweentlanga,
kuzale zizidumbu; Iphaluse intloko ezweni elibanzi.

<span id="an_110:7">110:7</span> Endleleni iya kusela emlanjaneni;
Ngenxa yoko iya kuphakamisa intloko.

<span id="an_111:1">111:1</span> Haleluya! Ndiya kubulela kuYehova
ngentliziyo yonke, Elucweyweni lwabathe tye nasebandleni.

<span id="an_111:2">111:2</span> Zikhulu izenzo zikaYehova,
Zezokungxokwa iintsingiselo zazo zonke.

<span id="an_111:3">111:3</span> Unendili nobungangamela umsebenzi
wakhe, Ubulungisa bakhe bumi ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_111:4">111:4</span> Uyenzele ukuze ikhunjulwe imisebenzi
yakhe ebalulekileyo; Unobabalo nemfesane uYehova.

<span id="an_111:5">111:5</span> Ubaphe ukudla abamoyikayo; Uwukhumbule
ngonaphakade umnqophiso wakhe.

<span id="an_111:6">111:6</span> Ubabonise abantu bakhe amandla ezenzo
zakhe, Ebanika ilifa leentlanga.

<span id="an_111:7">111:7</span> Izenzo zezandla zakhe ziyinyaniso
nesiko; Zithembekile zonke iziyalezo zakhe.

<span id="an_111:8">111:8</span> Zizimasekile nanini nangonaphakade;
Zenziwe ngenyaniso, zithe tye.

<span id="an_111:9">111:9</span> Ubathumele abantu bakhe inkululeko;
Uwumisele ngonaphakade umnqophiso wakhe; Lingcwele, liyoyikeka, igama
lakhe.

<span id="an_111:10">111:10</span> Ingqalo yobulumko kukoyika uYehova,
Banengqiqo elungileyo bonke abenza ngako; Indumiso yakhe ihlala imi.

<span id="an_112:1">112:1</span> Haleluya! Hayi, uyolo lomntu omoyikayo
uYehova, Oyinoneleleyo kunene imithetho yakhe!

<span id="an_112:2">112:2</span> Iya kuba nobugorha ehlabathini imbewu
yakhe; Isizukulwana sabathe tye sisikelelwe.

<span id="an_112:3">112:3</span> Bubuncwane nobutyebi endlwini yakhe;
Ubulungisa bakhe buhlala bumi.

<span id="an_112:4">112:4</span> Baphunyelwa kukukhanya ebumnyameni
abathe tye, Benobabalo, nemfesane, nobulungisa.

<span id="an_112:5">112:5</span> Unoyolo umntu obabalayo, aboleke; Uya
kuyimisa intetho yakhe ematyaleni.

<span id="an_112:6">112:6</span> Ngokuba akayi kushukunyiswa naphakade;
Uya kuba lilungisa elikhunjulwa ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_112:7">112:7</span> Akoyikiswa ziindaba ezimbi; Iqinisekile
intliziyo yakhe, ikholose ngoYehova.

<span id="an_112:8">112:8</span> Izimasekile intliziyo yakhe, akoyiki;
Uya kuda ababonele ababandezeli bakhe.

<span id="an_112:9">112:9</span> Uyahlakaza, upha amahlwempu; Ubulungisa
bakhe buhlala bumi, Uphondo lwakhe luphakamile, lunozuko.

<span id="an_112:10">112:10</span> Ongendawo yena uya kukubona, aqumbe,
Atshixize amazinyo, anyibilike; Umnqweno wongendawo uyadaka.

<span id="an_113:1">113:1</span> Haleluya! Dumisani, bakhonzi
bakaYehova, Dumisani igama likaYehova.

<span id="an_113:2">113:2</span> Malibongwe igama likaYehova, Kususela
ngokunje, kude kuse ephakadeni.

<span id="an_113:3">113:3</span> Kwasekuphumeni kwelanga kuse
ekutshoneni kwalo, Malidunyiswe igama likaYehova.

<span id="an_113:4">113:4</span> Uphakamile ngaphezu kweentlanga zonke
uYehova, Bungaphezulu kwamazulu ubuqaqawuli bakhe.

<span id="an_113:5">113:5</span> Ngubani na onjengoYehova, uThixo wethu?
Ulohlala phezulu;

<span id="an_113:6">113:6</span> Uloqondela phantsi; Ezulwini
nasemhlabeni?

<span id="an_113:7">113:7</span> Ulomvusa eluthulini osweleyo,
Ulomphakamisa ezaleni olihlwempu,

<span id="an_113:8">113:8</span> Ukuba amhlalise namanene, Amanene
abantu bakhe;

<span id="an_113:9">113:9</span> Ulohlalisa endlwini umfazi ongazaliyo,
Abe ngunobantwana ovuyayo. Haleluya!

<span id="an_114:1">114:1</span> Ekuphumeni kukaSirayeli eYiputa,
Kwendlu kaYakobi ebantwini abantetho ingaziwayo,

<span id="an_114:2">114:2</span> UYuda waba yingcwele yakhe, USirayeli
waba sisikumkani sakhe.

<span id="an_114:3">114:3</span> Ulwandle lwabona, lwasaba, IYordan
yabuya umva.

<span id="an_114:4">114:4</span> Iintaba zadloba njengeenkunzi zeegusha;
Iinduli, njengamatakane omhlambi.

<span id="an_114:5">114:5</span> Ubunani na, lulwandlendini, ukuba
usabe? Wena Yordan, ukuba ubuye umva?

<span id="an_114:6">114:6</span> Nina zintaba, ukuba nidlobe
njengeenkunzi zeegusha? Nina zinduli, njengamatakane omhlambi?

<span id="an_114:7">114:7</span> Wena hlabathi, zibhijabhije ebusweni
beNkosi, Ebusweni boThixo kaYakobi;

<span id="an_114:8">114:8</span> Uloguqula iliwa libe lidike lamanzi,
Iqhwitha libe yimithombo yamanzi.

<span id="an_115:1">115:1</span> Ungazukisi thina, Yehova, ungazukisi
thina; Zukisa igama lakho, Ngenxa yenceba yakho, ngenxa yenyaniso yakho.

<span id="an_115:2">115:2</span> Yini na ukuba zithi iintlanga, Uphi na
kaloku uThixo wabo?

<span id="an_115:3">115:3</span> UThixo wethu ke usemazulwini, Konke
akuthandileyo uyakwenza.

<span id="an_115:4">115:4</span> Izithixo zazo yisilivere negolide,
Zizenzo zezandla zabantu.

<span id="an_115:5">115:5</span> Zinomlomo nje, azithethi; Zinamehlo nje
aziboni;

<span id="an_115:6">115:6</span> Zineendlebe nje, aziva; Zineempumlo
nje, azisezeli.

<span id="an_115:7">115:7</span> Izandla zazo aziphathi, Iinyawo zazo
azihambi; Azidumzeli ngomqala wazo.

<span id="an_115:8">115:8</span> Boba njengazo abenzi bazo, Bonke
abasukuba bekholose ngazo.

<span id="an_115:9">115:9</span> Wena Sirayeli, kholosa ngoYehova;
Uncedo lwabo nengweletshetshe yabo nguye.

<span id="an_115:10">115:10</span> Nani bendlu ka-Aron, kholosani
ngoYehova; Uncedo lwabo nengweletshetshe yabo nguye.

<span id="an_115:11">115:11</span> Nina boyiki bakaYehova, kholosani
ngoYehova; Uncedo lwabo nengweletshetshe yabo nguye.

<span id="an_115:12">115:12</span> UYehova usikhumbule, wosisikelela;
Woyisikelela indlu kaSirayeli, Woyisikelela indlu ka-Aron;

<span id="an_115:13">115:13</span> Wobasikelela aboyiki bakaYehova,
Abancinane kwanabakhulu.

<span id="an_115:14">115:14</span> UYehova wonandisa nina ngakumbi
nangakumbi, Abandise oonyana benu.

<span id="an_115:15">115:15</span> Nisikelelekile kuYehova, UMenzi
wamazulu nowehlabathi.

<span id="an_115:16">115:16</span> Amazulu ngamazulu kaYehova, Ihlabathi
ulinike oonyana babantu.

<span id="an_115:17">115:17</span> Asingabafileyo abamdumisayo uYehova,
Asingabo bonke abehlayo baye kwelokuzola.

<span id="an_115:18">115:18</span> Thina ke siya kumbonga uYehova,
Kususela koku kude kuse ephakadeni. Haleluya!

<span id="an_116:1">116:1</span> Ndiyamthanda, ngokuba uYehova eliva
Ilizwi lam, ukutarhuzisa kwam.

<span id="an_116:2">116:2</span> Ngokuba endithobele indlebe yakhe,
Ndiya kumnqula ngemihla yam yonke.

<span id="an_116:3">116:3</span> Izintya zokufa zandijikela,
Iingxingongo zelabafileyo zandifumana, Ndafunyanwa ziimbandezelo
nesingqa la.

<span id="an_116:4">116:4</span> Ndanqula ke igama likaYehova, ndathi,
Yehova, ndiya kukhunga, siza umphefumlo wam.

<span id="an_116:5">116:5</span> UYehova unobabalo, ulilungisa, UThixo
wethu unemfesane.

<span id="an_116:6">116:6</span> Ngumgcini wabazizidenge uYehova;
Ndandiswele, wandisindisa.

<span id="an_116:7">116:7</span> Buyela ekuphumleni kwakho, mphefumlo
wam, Ngokuba uYehova ukuphatha kakuhle;

<span id="an_116:8">116:8</span> Ngokuba ewuhlangule umphefumlo wam
ekufeni, Iliso lam ezinyembezini, Unyawo lwam ekungqulekeni.

<span id="an_116:9">116:9</span> Ndiya kuhamba-hamba phambi koYehova
Emazweni abaphilileyo.

<span id="an_116:10">116:10</span> Ndiyakholwa, xa ndithethayo; Mna
ndicinezelekile kunene.

<span id="an_116:11">116:11</span> Ndathi mna ekuphakuzeleni kwam, Bonke
abantu ngamaxoki.

<span id="an_116:12">116:12</span> Ndingambuyisela ngantoni na uYehova
Konke ukundiphatha kwakhe kakuhle?

<span id="an_116:13">116:13</span> Ndophakamisa indebe yosindiso,
Ndinqule igama likaYehova.

<span id="an_116:14">116:14</span> Ewe, ndozizalisa izibhambathiso zam
kuYehova, Phambi kwabantu bakhe bonke kalokunje.

<span id="an_116:15">116:15</span> Kunqabile emehlweni kaYehova Ukufa
kwakhakhe benceba.

<span id="an_116:16">116:16</span> Okunene, Yehova, ndingumkhonzi wakho,
Ndingumkhonzi wakho, unyana womkhonzazana wakho; Uzicombulule
iimbophelelo zam.

<span id="an_116:17">116:17</span> Ndiya kubingelela kuwe umbingelelo
wombulelo, Ndinqule igama likaYehova.

<span id="an_116:18">116:18</span> Ewe, ndiya kuzizalisa izibhambathiso
zam kuYehova, Phambi kwabantu bakhe bonke,

<span id="an_116:19">116:19</span> Ezintendelezweni zendlu kaYehova,
Esazulwini sakho, Yerusalem. Haleluya!

<span id="an_117:1">117:1</span> Mdumiseni uYehova, nonke zintlanga,
Mncomeni, nonke zizwe.

<span id="an_117:2">117:2</span> Ngokuba inamandla kuthi inceba yakhe,
Inyaniso kaYehova ingunaphakade. Haleluya!

<span id="an_118:1">118:1</span> Bulelani kuYehova, ngokuba elungile,
Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_118:2">118:2</span> Makathi uSirayeli, Ingunaphakade inceba
yakhe.

<span id="an_118:3">118:3</span> Mayithi indlu ka-Aron, Ingunaphakade
inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_118:4">118:4</span> Mabathi abamoyikayo uYehova,
Ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_118:5">118:5</span> Ndabiza uYehova ndisengxingongweni;
Wandiphendula uYehova, wandibeka endaweni ebanzi.

<span id="an_118:6">118:6</span> UYehova ungakum, andoyiki; Angandenza
ntoni na umntu?

<span id="an_118:7">118:7</span> UYehova ungakum ngokundinceda; Ndiya
kubona mna kwabandithiyayo.

<span id="an_118:8">118:8</span> Kulungile ukuzimela ngoYehova, Ngaphezu
kokukholosa ngomntu.

<span id="an_118:9">118:9</span> Kulungile ukuzimela ngoYehova Ngaphezu
kokukholosa ngamanene.

<span id="an_118:10">118:10</span> Zingafanelana zonke iintlanga
zindirhawule: Egameni likaYehova inene ndozinqumla.

<span id="an_118:11">118:11</span> Zingafanelana zindirhawule
zandirhawula: Egameni likaYehova inene ndozinqumla.

<span id="an_118:12">118:12</span> Zingafanelana zindirhawule
njengeenyosi: Zocinywa njengomlilo weentsasa; Egameni likaYehova inene
ndozinqumla.

<span id="an_118:13">118:13</span> Undityhale ngamandla wena ukuba
ndiwe; Kodwa uYehova wandinceda.

<span id="an_118:14">118:14</span> Iqhayiya lam nengoma yam nguYehova,
Waba lusindiso kum.

<span id="an_118:15">118:15</span> Izwi lokumemelela nelosindiso
lisezintenteni zamalungisa, lisithi, Isandla sokunene sikaYehova
siyeyisa;

<span id="an_118:16">118:16</span> Isandla sokunene sikaYehova
siphakamile; Isandla sokunene sikaYehova siyeyisa.

<span id="an_118:17">118:17</span> Andiyi kufa, ndiya kudla ubomi,
Ndibalise ngezenzo zikaYehova.

<span id="an_118:18">118:18</span> UYehova undithethise kakhulu, Ke
akandinikela ekufeni.

<span id="an_118:19">118:19</span> Ndivuleleni amasango obulungisa;
Ndiya kungena ngawo, ndiya kubulela kuYehova.

<span id="an_118:20">118:20</span> Nali isango likaYehova, Amalungisa
angena ngalo.

<span id="an_118:21">118:21</span> Ndiyabulela kuwe kuba undiphendule,
Waba lusindiso kum.

<span id="an_118:22">118:22</span> Ilitye abalilahlayo abakhi Laba
yintloko yembombo.

<span id="an_118:23">118:23</span> Kuvele kuYehova oku, Kungumsebenzi
obalulekileyo emehlweni ethu.

<span id="an_118:24">118:24</span> Le yimini ayenzileyo uYehova,
Masigcobe sivuye ngayo.

<span id="an_118:25">118:25</span> Yehova, camagu, khawusindise, Yehova,
camagu, khawuhlangule.

<span id="an_118:26">118:26</span> Makabongwe lo uzayo esegameni
likaYehova, Siyanisikelela nina basendlwini kaYehova.

<span id="an_118:27">118:27</span> UYehova nguThixo, usikhanyisela;
Bophelelani umbingelelo womthendeleko ngeentambo, Kude kuye ezimpondweni
zesibingelelo.

<span id="an_118:28">118:28</span> UnguThixo wam, ndiya kubulela kuwe;
UnguThixo wam, ndiya kukuphakamisa.

<span id="an_118:29">118:29</span> Bulelani kuYehova, ngokuba elungile,
Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_119:1">119:1</span> Hayi, uyolo lwabandlela igqibeleleyo,
Bona bahambayo ngomyalelo kaYehova!

<span id="an_119:2">119:2</span> Hayi, uyolo lwababambe izingqiniso
zakhe, Abamquqelayo ngentliziyo epheleleyo!

<span id="an_119:3">119:3</span> Abasebenzi nokusebenza bugqwetha,
Bayahamba ngeendlela zakhe.

<span id="an_119:4">119:4</span> Uzimisile iziyalezo zakho, Ukuba
zigcinwe kunene.

<span id="an_119:5">119:5</span> Azaba iindlela zam bezibhekiselwe
Ukugcina imimiselo yakho!

<span id="an_119:6">119:6</span> Bendingayi kudana ke Ekubhekeni kwam
kwimithetho yakho yonke.

<span id="an_119:7">119:7</span> Ndiya kubulela kuwe ngentliziyo ethe
tye, Ekuzifundeni kwam izigwebo zobulungisa bakho.

<span id="an_119:8">119:8</span> Ndiya kuyigcina imimiselo yakho, Musa
ukundishiya kuphele.

<span id="an_119:9">119:9</span> Umfana uya kuwuqaqambisa ngantoni na
umendo wakhe? Ngokuzigcina ngokwelizwi lakho.

<span id="an_119:10">119:10</span> Ndiya kuquqela kuwe ngentliziyo yam
yonke; Musa ukundilahlekanisa nemithetho yakho.

<span id="an_119:11">119:11</span> Ndiyibeke intetho yakho entliziyweni
yam, Ukuze ndingoni kuwe.

<span id="an_119:12">119:12</span> Ungowokubongwa, Yehova; Ndifundise
imimiselo yakho.

<span id="an_119:13">119:13</span> Ndiyawabalisa ngemilebe yomlomo wam
Onke amasiko omlomo wakho.

<span id="an_119:14">119:14</span> Ndinemihlali endleleni yezingqiniso
zakho, Ngathi kusebuncwaneni bonke.

<span id="an_119:15">119:15</span> Ndiya kucamngca ngeziyalezo zakho,
Ndibheke kumendo wakho.

<span id="an_119:16">119:16</span> Ndiyaziyolisa ngemimiselo yakho;
Andiyi kulilibala ilizwi lakho.

<span id="an_119:17">119:17</span> Mphathe kakuhle umkhonzi wakho,
ndidle ubomi, Ndigcine ilizwi lakho.

<span id="an_119:18">119:18</span> Vula amehlo am, ukuba ndiyibone
Imisebenzi ebalulekileyo yasemyalelweni wakho.

<span id="an_119:19">119:19</span> Ndingumphambukeli ehlabathini, Musa
ukuyisithelisa kum imithetho yakho.

<span id="an_119:20">119:20</span> Umphefumlo wam ucumkile
ngokulangazelela Amasiko akho ngamaxesha onke.

<span id="an_119:21">119:21</span> Ubakhalimele abakhukhumali,
Abaqalekiswa abo, balahlekeneyo nemithetho yakho.

<span id="an_119:22">119:22</span> Shenxisa imke kum ingcikivo nendelo,
Ngokuba ndizibambile izingqiniso zakho.

<span id="an_119:23">119:23</span> Nangona abathetheli behlala bathethe
ngam, Umkhonzi wakho yena ucamngca ngemimiselo yakho.

<span id="an_119:24">119:24</span> Izingqiniso zakho ziziyoliso zam
noko, Zingamaphakathi am.

<span id="an_119:25">119:25</span> Umphefumlo wam unamathele eluthulini:
Ndiphilise ngokwelizwi lakho.

<span id="an_119:26">119:26</span> Ndizicacisile iindlela zam,
wandiphendula; Ndifundise imimisela yakho.

<span id="an_119:27">119:27</span> Ndiqondise iindlela zeziyalezo zakho,
Ndicamngce ngemisebenzi yakho ebalulekileyo.

<span id="an_119:28">119:28</span> Umphefumlo wam uvuza iinyembezi
sisingqala, Ndimise ngokwelizwi lakho.

<span id="an_119:29">119:29</span> Indlela yobuxoki yisuse kum;
Ndibabale umyalelo wakho.

<span id="an_119:30">119:30</span> Ndiyinyule indlela yokuthembeka;
Amasiko akho ndijolise kuwo.

<span id="an_119:31">119:31</span> Ndinamathele ezingqinisweni zakho;
Musa ukundidanisa, Yehova.

<span id="an_119:32">119:32</span> Ndigidima ngendlela yemithetho yakho,
Ngokuba uyenze banzi intliziyo yam.

<span id="an_119:33">119:33</span> Ndiyalele, Yehova, indlela yemimiselo
yakho, Ndiyibambe kuphele.

<span id="an_119:34">119:34</span> Ndiqondise, ndibambe umyalelo wakho,
Ndiwugcine ngentliziyo yonke.

<span id="an_119:35">119:35</span> Ndinyathelise endleleni yemithetho
yakho, Ngokuba ndiyithandile.

<span id="an_119:36">119:36</span> Intliziyo yam yithobele
ezingqinisweni zakho, Ungayithobeli ekubaweni.

<span id="an_119:37">119:37</span> Dlulisa amehlo am angakhangeli
