inkohlakalo, Ndiphilise ngeendlela zakho.

<span id="an_119:38">119:38</span> Zalisa kumkhonzi wakho intetho yakho,
Eyokuba bakoyike.

<span id="an_119:39">119:39</span> Yidlulise ingcikivo yam
endinxunguphala yiyo, Ngokuba amasiko akho alungile.

<span id="an_119:40">119:40</span> Nanku ndilangazelela iziyalezo zakho,
Ndiphilise ngobulungisa bakho.

<span id="an_119:41">119:41</span> Mazize kum iinceba zakho, Yehova,
Nosindiso lwakho ngokwentetho yakho;

<span id="an_119:42">119:42</span> Ndimphendule ngelizwi ondingcikivayo,
Ngokuba ndikholose ngelizwi lakho.

<span id="an_119:43">119:43</span> Musa ukuda ulihluthe emlonyeni wam
ilizwi lenyaniso, Ngokuba ndilindele izigwebo zakho;

<span id="an_119:44">119:44</span> Ndowugcina umyalelo wakho ngamaxesha
onke, Ngonaphakade kanaphakade;

<span id="an_119:45">119:45</span> Ndihamba-hambe endaweni ebanzi,
Ngokuba ndifuna iziyalezo zakho.

<span id="an_119:46">119:46</span> Ndothetha ngezingqiniso zakho phambi
kokumkani, Ndingabi nakudana.

<span id="an_119:47">119:47</span> Ndoziyolisa ngemithetho yakho
Endiyithandayo;

<span id="an_119:48">119:48</span> Ndiziphakamise izandla zam
emithethweni yakho endiyithandayo, Ndicamngce ngemimiselo yakho.

<span id="an_119:49">119:49</span> Khumbula ilizwi lakho kumkhonzi
wakho, Ngenxa enokuba undithembise lona.

<span id="an_119:50">119:50</span> Yiyo le intuthuzelo yam
ekucinezelekeni kwam, Yokuba intetho yakho indiphilisile.

<span id="an_119:51">119:51</span> Abakhukhumali bada bandigxeka
kakhulu; Kanti andithi gu bucala emyalelweni wakho.

<span id="an_119:52">119:52</span> Ndawakhumbula amasiko akho kususela
kwanaphakade, Yehova, Ndathuthuzeleka.

<span id="an_119:53">119:53</span> Ndingenwe ngumsindo oshushu,
Ndisenziwa ngabangendawo abalahla umyalelo wakho.

<span id="an_119:54">119:54</span> Iziingoma kum imimiselo yakho,
Endlwini yokuphambukela kwam.

<span id="an_119:55">119:55</span> Ndilikhumbule ebusuku igama lakho,
Yehova, Ndawugcina umyalelo wakho.

<span id="an_119:56">119:56</span> Ndinikwe oku, Ukuba ndibambe
iziyalezo zakho.

<span id="an_119:57">119:57</span> Isabelo sam, Yehova, ndithi, Sesokuba
ndigcine amazwi akho.

<span id="an_119:58">119:58</span> Ndiya kubongoza ngentliziyo yonke,
Ndibabale ngokwentetho yakho.

<span id="an_119:59">119:59</span> Ndazicingela iindlela zam,
Ndazibuyisela iinyawo zam ezingqinisweni zakho.

<span id="an_119:60">119:60</span> Ndikhawulezile andazila-zila Ukugcina
imithetho yakho.

<span id="an_119:61">119:61</span> Izintya zabangendawo zindithandele,
Andiwulibele umyalelo wakhe noko.

<span id="an_119:62">119:62</span> Ndivuka phakathi kobusuku, ndibulele
kuwe, Ngenxa yezigwebo zobulungisa bakho.

<span id="an_119:63">119:63</span> Ndilidlelane labo bonke abakoyikayo,
Nelabazigcinayo iziyalezo zakho.

<span id="an_119:64">119:64</span> Inceba yakho, Yehova, izalise
ihlabathi; Ndifundise imimiselo yakho.

<span id="an_119:65">119:65</span> Umenzele okulungileyo umkhonzi wakho,
Yehova, ngokwelizwi lakho.

<span id="an_119:66">119:66</span> Ndifundise, ndibe nemvo nokwazi
okulungileyo, Ngokuba ndikholwa yimithetho yakho.

<span id="an_119:67">119:67</span> Ndingekacinezelwa, ndaye ndilahleka;
Kungoku ndiyigcinile intetho yakho.

<span id="an_119:68">119:68</span> Ulungile wena, ulungisa; Ndifundise
imimiselo yakho.

<span id="an_119:69">119:69</span> Abakhukhumali bathungele ubuxoki
ngam; Mna ndizibamba ngentliziyo yonke iziyalezo zakho.

<span id="an_119:70">119:70</span> Ithe fithi kukutyeba intliziyo yabo;
Ke mna ndiziyolisa ngomyalelo wakho.

<span id="an_119:71">119:71</span> Kundilungele okokuba ndacinezelwayo,
Ukuze ndiyifunde imimiselo yakho.

<span id="an_119:72">119:72</span> Ulungile kum umyalelo womlomo wakho,
Ngaphezu kwamawaka egolide nesilivere.

<span id="an_119:73">119:73</span> Izandla zakho zindenzile,
zandilungisa; Ndiqondise, ndifunde imithetho yakho.

<span id="an_119:74">119:74</span> Abakoyikayo bondibona, bavuye,
Ngokuba ndilindele elizwini lakho.

<span id="an_119:75">119:75</span> Ndiyazi, Yehova, ukuba zinobulungisa
izigwebo zakho; Undicinezele, phofu uthembekile.

<span id="an_119:76">119:76</span> Ngamana inceba yakho yaba
yeyokundithuthuzela, Njengokwentetho yakho kumkhonzi wakho.

<span id="an_119:77">119:77</span> Mazize kum iimfesane zakho, ndiphile,
Ngokuba umyalelo wakho undiyolisa.

<span id="an_119:78">119:78</span> Mabadane abakhukhumali, ngokuba
bendigobele phantsi ngobuxoki, Mna ndicamngca ngeziyalezo zakho.

<span id="an_119:79">119:79</span> Mabandibuyele abakoyikayo, Nabazaziyo
izingqiniso zakho.

<span id="an_119:80">119:80</span> Mayigqibelele intliziyo yam
emimiselweni yakho, Ukuze ndingadani.

<span id="an_119:81">119:81</span> Umphefumlo wam uyaphela
kukululangazelela usindiso lwakho, Ndilindele elizwini lakho.

<span id="an_119:82">119:82</span> Amehlo am ayaphela kukulangazelela
intetho yakho, Ndisithi, Uya kundithuthuzela nini na?

<span id="an_119:83">119:83</span> Noko ndithe ndaba njengentsuba
emsini; Andiyilibali imimiselo yakho.

<span id="an_119:84">119:84</span> Zingaphi na iintsuku zomkhonzi wakho?
Uya kuda ubagwebe nini na abandisukelayo?

<span id="an_119:85">119:85</span> Abakhukhumali bandimbele izihogo,
Abangenamyalelo wakho.

<span id="an_119:86">119:86</span> Yonke imithetho yakho ithembekile:
Bandisukela ngobuxoki; ndincede.

<span id="an_119:87">119:87</span> Baphantse ukundigqibela emhlabeni, Ke
mna andizilahli iziyalezo zakho.

<span id="an_119:88">119:88</span> Ndiphilise ngokwenceba yakho,
Ndizigcine izingqiniso zomlomo wakho.

<span id="an_119:89">119:89</span> Lingunaphakade, Yehova, Limi
emazulwini ilizwi lakho.

<span id="an_119:90">119:90</span> Ukuthembeka kwakho kukwizizukulwana
ngezizukulwana; Ulizinzisile ihlabathi, lema.

<span id="an_119:91">119:91</span> Ezo zinto zimele izigwebo zakho
nanamhla, Ngokuba iinto zonke zingabakhonzi bakho.

<span id="an_119:92">119:92</span> Koko umyalelo wakho wandiyolisayo,
Ndinge ndaphelayo ekucinezelekeni kwam.

<span id="an_119:93">119:93</span> Andiyi kuzilibala naphakade iziyalezo
zakho, Ngokuba undiphilisile ngazo.

<span id="an_119:94">119:94</span> Ndingowakho mna, ndisindise, Kuba
ndicamanga ngeziyalezo zakho.

<span id="an_119:95">119:95</span> Abangendawo bandilindile ukuze
banditshabalalise; Mna ndigqale izingqiniso zakho.

<span id="an_119:96">119:96</span> Yonke inzaliseko ndiyibonile apho
iphela khona; Ke wona umthetho wakho ngumphangalala omkhulu.

<span id="an_119:97">119:97</span> Hayi, ukuwuthanda kwam umyalelo
wakho! Imini le yonke ndiyacamngca ngawo.

<span id="an_119:98">119:98</span> Indifundisa ubulumko ngaphezu
kweentshaba zam imithetho yakho, Ngokuba yeyam ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_119:99">119:99</span> Ndinokuqiqa ngaphezu kwabafundisi bam
bonke, Ngokuba ngezingqiniso zakho ndiyacamngca.

<span id="an_119:100">119:100</span> Ndinokuqonda ngaphezu kwamadoda
amakhulu, Ngokuba ndizibamba iziyalezo zakho.

<span id="an_119:101">119:101</span> Ndizinqandile iinyawo zam
kwiindlela zonke ezimbi, Ukuze ndiligcine ilizwi lakho.

<span id="an_119:102">119:102</span> Andisuki emasikweni akho, Ngokuba
undiyalile wena.

<span id="an_119:103">119:103</span> Hayi, ukuba mnandi kwentetho yakho
ekhuhlangubeni lam! Igqithe nobusi emlonyeni wam.

<span id="an_119:104">119:104</span> Ngeziyalezo zakho ndinokuqonda,
Ngenxa yoko ndiwuthiyile wonke umendo wobuxoki.

<span id="an_119:105">119:105</span> Lisisibane seenyawo zam ilizwi
lakho, Likukukhanya emendweni wam.

<span id="an_119:106">119:106</span> Ndikufungele, ndikumisile,
Ukuzigcina izigwebo zobulungisa bakho.

<span id="an_119:107">119:107</span> Ndide ndacinezeleka kakhulu;
Yehova, ndiphilise ngokwelizwi lakho.

<span id="an_119:108">119:108</span> Ngamana wakholeka kuwe, Yehova,
umbingelelo wesisa womlomo wam; Ndifundise amasiko akho.

<span id="an_119:109">119:109</span> Umphefumlo wam uhlala usesandleni
sam, Ndingawulibali umyalelo wakho.

<span id="an_119:110">119:110</span> Abangendawo bandenzele umgibe,
Andiphambukanga eziyalezweni zakho.

<span id="an_119:111">119:111</span> Ndizidle ilifa izingqiniso zakho
ngonaphakade, Ngokuba ziyimihlali yentliziyo yam;

<span id="an_119:112">119:112</span> Intliziyo yam ndiyithobele
ekwenzeni imimiselo yakho Ngonaphakade, kuphele.

<span id="an_119:113">119:113</span> Abambaxa ndiyabathiya, Wona
umyalelo wakho ndiyawuthanda.

<span id="an_119:114">119:114</span> Isithe lam nengweletshetshe yam
nguwe, Ndilindele elizwini lakho.

<span id="an_119:115">119:115</span> Sukani kum, nina benzi beento
ezimbi, Ndibambe imithetho yoThixo wam.

<span id="an_119:116">119:116</span> Ndizimase ngokwelizwi lakho,
ndiphile, Ungandidanisi ekulindeni kwam.

<span id="an_119:117">119:117</span> Ndixhase ndisinde, Ndihlale
ndibheke emimiselweni yakho.

<span id="an_119:118">119:118</span> Ubacukucezile bonke abalahlekana
nemimiselo yakho, Ngokuba inkohliso yabo ibubuxoki.

<span id="an_119:119">119:119</span> Wena ususa bonke abangendawo
behlabathi njengentlenga, Ngoko ndiyazithanda izingqiniso zakho.

<span id="an_119:120">119:120</span> Inyama yam isuka ihambe
kukunkwantyiswa nguwe, Ndizoyike izigwebo zakho.

<span id="an_119:121">119:121</span> Ndenza ngesiko nangobulungisa,
Ungandinikeli kwabandicudisayo.

<span id="an_119:122">119:122</span> Mmele umkhonzi wakho, kulunge;
Mabangandicudisi abakhukhumali.

<span id="an_119:123">119:123</span> Amehlo am ayaphela
kukululangazelela usindiso lwakho, Nentetho yobulungisa bakho.

<span id="an_119:124">119:124</span> Umkhonzi wakho menzele ngokwenceba
yakho Undifundise imimiselo yakho.

<span id="an_119:125">119:125</span> Ndingumkhonzi wakho, ndiqondise,
Ndizazi izingqiniso zakho.

<span id="an_119:126">119:126</span> Lilixa lokuba uYehova enze, Kuba
bawaphule umyalelo wakho.

<span id="an_119:127">119:127</span> Ngenxa yoko ndiyithanda imithetho
yakho Ngaphezu kwegolide, nakwengcwengiweyo.

<span id="an_119:128">119:128</span> Ngenxa yoko ndithi, Zonke iziyalezo
zakho zithe tye ngezinto zonke; Wonke umendo wobuxoki ndiwuthiyile.

<span id="an_119:129">119:129</span> Ziyimisebenzi ebalulekileyo
izingqiniso zakho, Ngenxa yoko uzibambile umphefumlo wam.

<span id="an_119:130">119:130</span> Ukutyhila kwamazwi akho
kuyakhanyisa, Kuqondisa abazizidenge.

<span id="an_119:131">119:131</span> Ndakhamisa umlomo wam, ndakhefuza,
Ngokuba ndiyilangazelela imithetho yakho.

<span id="an_119:132">119:132</span> Ndibheke, undibabale, Ngokwesiko
lakho kubathandi begama lakho.

<span id="an_119:133">119:133</span> Qinisa ukunyathela kwam ngentetho
yakho, Mabungabi nagunya kum ubutshinga, nabuphi na.

<span id="an_119:134">119:134</span> Ndikhulule ekucudiseni komntu,
Ndizigcine iziyalezo zakho.

<span id="an_119:135">119:135</span> Khanyisa ubuso bakho kumkhonzi
wakho, Undifundise imimiselo yakho.

<span id="an_119:136">119:136</span> Ahla imijelo yamanzi amehlo am,
Ngenxa yokuba bengawugcini umyalelo wakho.

<span id="an_119:137">119:137</span> Ulilungisa wena, Yehova, Zithe tye
izigwebo zakho.

<span id="an_119:138">119:138</span> Uzimisile izingqiniso zakho,
zanobulungisa, Zaba nokuthembeka kakhulu.

<span id="an_119:139">119:139</span> Ikhwele lam lindibhangisile,
Ngokuba abandibandezelayo bewalibele amazwi akho.

<span id="an_119:140">119:140</span> Ilizwi lakho linyibilikisiwe
njengegolide kunene, Umkhonzi wakho uyalithanda.

<span id="an_119:141">119:141</span> Ndimncinane, ndideliwe, Noko
andizilibali iziyalezo zakho.

<span id="an_119:142">119:142</span> Ubulungisa bakho bubulungisa
obungunaphakade, Umyalelo wakho uyinyaniso.

<span id="an_119:143">119:143</span> Imbandezelo nengcutheko indifumene,
Imithetho yakho iyandiyolisa.

<span id="an_119:144">119:144</span> Zinobulungisa ngonaphakade
izingqiniso zakho, Ndiqondise, ndiphile.

<span id="an_119:145">119:145</span> Ndikhala ngentliziyo yonke,
ndiphendule; Yehova, imimiselo yakho ndiya kuyibamba.

<span id="an_119:146">119:146</span> Ndikhala kuwe, ndisindise, Ndigcine
izingqiniso zakho.

<span id="an_119:147">119:147</span> Ndakuphangela ukusa, ndazibika,
Ndalindela emazwini akho.

<span id="an_119:148">119:148</span> Amehlo am aphengela imilindo
yasebusuku, Ukuze ndicamngce ngentetho yakho.

<span id="an_119:149">119:149</span> Live ilizwi lam ngokwenceba yakho,
Yehova, ndiphilise ngokwamasiko akho.

<span id="an_119:150">119:150</span> Bayasondela abaphuthuma amanyala,
Banyawuka emyalelweni wakho;

<span id="an_119:151">119:151</span> Usondele wena, Yehova, Yonke
imithetho yakho iyinyaniso.

<span id="an_119:152">119:152</span> Kudala ndisazi ngokwezingqiniso
zakho, Ukuba uzisekile ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_119:153">119:153</span> Khangela ukucinezeleka kwam,
undihlangule, Ngokuba ndingawulibali umyalelo wakho.

<span id="an_119:154">119:154</span> Bambana nobambene nam, undikhulule,
Ndiphilise ngokwelizwi lakho.

<span id="an_119:155">119:155</span> Lunyawukile kwabangendawo usindiso,
Ngokuba abayifuni imimiselo yakho.

<span id="an_119:156">119:156</span> Iimfesane zakho zininzi, Yehova;
Ndiphilise ngokwamasiko akho.

<span id="an_119:157">119:157</span> Baninzi abandisukelayo
nabandibandezelayo; Andithi gu bucala ezingqinisweni zakho.

<span id="an_119:158">119:158</span> Ndababona abatshinizi, ndakruquka,
Abo bangayigciniyo intetho yakho.

<span id="an_119:159">119:159</span> Bona ukuthanda kwam iziyalezo
zakho, Yehova, ndiphilise ngokwenceba yakho.

<span id="an_119:160">119:160</span> Isimbuku selizwi lakho siyinyaniso
iphela, Zingunaphakade zonke izigwebo zobulungisa bakho.

<span id="an_119:161">119:161</span> Abathetheli bandisukela ngelize,
Intliziyo yam iyankwantyiswa ngamazwi akho.

<span id="an_119:162">119:162</span> Ndinemihlali ngentetho yakho,
Njengofumene ixhoba elininzi.

<span id="an_119:163">119:163</span> Ndikuthiyile ukuxoka, lisikizi kum;
Ndiyawuthanda umyalelo wakho.

<span id="an_119:164">119:164</span> Ndikudumisa kasixhenxe ngemini,
Ngenxa yezigwebo zobulungisa bakho.

<span id="an_119:165">119:165</span> Banoxolo olukhulu abawuthandayo
umyalelo wakho; Akukho sikhubekiso kubo.

<span id="an_119:166">119:166</span> Ndikhangela usindiso lwakho,
Yehova; Ndenza imithetho yakho.

<span id="an_119:167">119:167</span> Umphefumlo wam uyazigcina
izingqiniso zakho, Ndizithanda kunene.

<span id="an_119:168">119:168</span> Ndiyazigcina iziyalezo zakho
nezingqiniso zakho, Ngokuba zonke iindlela zam ziphambi kwakho.

<span id="an_119:169">119:169</span> Makusondele phambi kwakho
ukuhlahlamba kwam; Yehova, ndiqondise ngokwelizwi lakho.

<span id="an_119:170">119:170</span> Masifike isikhungo sam phambi
kwakho; Ndihlangule ngokwentetho yakho.

<span id="an_119:171">119:171</span> Umlomo wam mawumpompoze indumiso,
Kuba undifundisile imimiselo yakho.

<span id="an_119:172">119:172</span> Ulwimi lwam luya kuyiphendula
intetho yakho, Ngokuba yonke imithetho yakho inobulungisa.

<span id="an_119:173">119:173</span> Isandla sakho masibe
sesokundinceda, Ngokuba ndizinyulele iziyalezo zakho.

<span id="an_119:174">119:174</span> Ndilangazelela usindiso lwakho,
Yehova; Umyalelo wakho uyandiyolisa.

<span id="an_119:175">119:175</span> Mawuphile umphefumlo wam,
ukudumise, Andincede amasiko akho.

<span id="an_119:176">119:176</span> Ndiya ndimka njengemvu
elahlekileyo; mfune umkhonzi wakho, Ngokuba andiyilibali imithetho
yakho.

<span id="an_120:1">120:1</span> Ingoma yezinyuko. Engxingongweni yam
ndakhala kuYehova, Wandiphendula.

<span id="an_120:2">120:2</span> Ndathi, Wuhlangule, Yehova, umphefumlo
wam emlonyeni oxokayo, Elulwimini olunenkohliso.

<span id="an_120:3">120:3</span> Makakunike ntoni na, akongeze ntoni na,
Lulwimindini lunenkohliso?

<span id="an_120:4">120:4</span> Iintolo zegorha ezitsolo, Kunye
namalahle avuthayo onwele.

<span id="an_120:5">120:5</span> Athi ke mna! Kuba ndingumphambukeli
kwaMesheki, Ndihleli ngasezintenteni zakwaKedare.

<span id="an_120:6">120:6</span> Umphefumlo wam kade uhleli
Nabaluthiyileyo uxolo.

<span id="an_120:7">120:7</span> Mna ndingowoxolo; Ke ndithi
ndakuthetha, bona babe yimfazwe.

<span id="an_121:1">121:1</span> Ingoma yezinyuko. Ndiwaphakamisele
ezintabeni na amehlo am? Luya kuvela phi na uncedo lwam?

<span id="an_121:2">121:2</span> Uncedo lwam luvela kuYehova, UMenzi
wezulu nehlabathi.

<span id="an_121:3">121:3</span> Akayi kukha alunikele unyawo lwakho
ekutyibilikeni; Akayi kukha ozele umgcini wakho.

<span id="an_121:4">121:4</span> Uyabona, akozeli, akalali, UMgcini
kaSirayeli.

<span id="an_121:5">121:5</span> NguYehova umgcini wakho, NguYehova
umthunzi wakho ekunene kwakho.

<span id="an_121:6">121:6</span> Emini ilanga aliyi kukwenzakalisa,
Nenyanga ebusuku.

<span id="an_121:7">121:7</span> UYehova uya kukugcina ebubini bonke,
Uya kuwugcina umphefumlo wakho.

<span id="an_121:8">121:8</span> UYehova uya kukugcina ukuphuma kwakho
nokungena kwakho, Kususela ngoku kude kuse ephakadeni.

<span id="an_122:1">122:1</span> Ingoma yezinyuko. KaDavide. Ndavuya
bakuthi kum, Masiye endlwini kaYehova.

<span id="an_122:2">122:2</span> Iinyawo zethu zifike zema Emasangweni
akho, Yerusalem;

<span id="an_122:3">122:3</span> Yerusalem, wena wakhiweyo Ngokomzi
ohlangeneyo wamnye;

<span id="an_122:4">122:4</span> Apho zinyuka ziye khona izizwe, Izizwe
zikaYehova; Ibubungqina ke loo nto kwaSirayeli, Ukuba kubulelwe kwigama
likaYehova.

<span id="an_122:5">122:5</span> Kuba khona apho kumiswe iitrone
zokugweba, Iitrone zendlu kaDavide.

<span id="an_122:6">122:6</span> Celelani iYerusalem uxolo; Mababe
nokuchulumacha abakuthandayo,

<span id="an_122:7">122:7</span> Malube luxolo eludongeni lwakho
olurhaqileyo, Nokuchulumacha ezingxandeni zakho ezinde.

<span id="an_122:8">122:8</span> Ngenxa yabazalwana bam nowethu, Makhe
ndithethe uxolo ngawe.

<span id="an_122:9">122:9</span> Ngenxa yendlu kaYehova, uThixo wethu,
Ndiya kufuna okukulungeleyo.

<span id="an_123:1">123:1</span> Ingoma yezinyuko. Ulohlala emazulwini,
Ndiwaphakamisela kuwe amehlo am.

<span id="an_123:2">123:2</span> Uyabona, njengokuba amehlo abakhonzi
Emi kwisandla seenkosi zabo; Njengokuba amehlo omkhonzazana Emi
kwisandla senkosikazi yakhe: Ngokunjalo amehlo ethu akuYehova, uThixo
wethu, Ade asibabale.

<span id="an_123:3">123:3</span> Sibabale, Yehova, sibabale, Ngokuba
sanele kakhulu kukudelwa.

<span id="an_123:4">123:4</span> Umphefumlo wethu wanele kakhulu
Kukugculela kwabangakhathalele bani, Nokudela kwabanekratshi.

<span id="an_124:1">124:1</span> Ingoma yezinyuko. KaDavide. Koko
uYehova ebengakuthi, Makatsho uSirayeli,

<span id="an_124:2">124:2</span> Koko uYehova ebengakuthi Ekusukeleni
kwabantu phezulu kuthi,

<span id="an_124:3">124:3</span> Bange beba basiginya sihleli,
Ekuvutheni komsindo wabo kuthi;

<span id="an_124:4">124:4</span> Ange esintywilisele amanzi, Wadlula
phezu komphefumlo wethu umsinga;

<span id="an_124:5">124:5</span> Ange edlule phezu komphefumlo wethu
Amanzi akhukumeleyo.

<span id="an_124:6">124:6</span> Ungowokubongwa uYehova, Ongasinikelanga
emazinyweni abo, ukuba siqwengwe.

<span id="an_124:7">124:7</span> Umphefumlo wethu usindile, njengentaka
emgibeni wababambisi; Umgibe uqhawukile, sasinda ke thina.

<span id="an_124:8">124:8</span> Uncedo lwethu lusegameni likaYehova,
UMenzi wezulu nehlabathi.

<span id="an_125:1">125:1</span> Ingoma yezinyuko. Abo bakholosa
ngoYehova banjengentaba yaseZiyon: Ayishukumi, ihleli ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_125:2">125:2</span> IYerusalem ijikelezwe ziintaba; Ke
uYehova ubajikelezile naye abantu bakhe, Kususela ngoku kude kuse
ephakadeni.

<span id="an_125:3">125:3</span> Ngokuba ayiyi kuhlala intonga
yokungendawo elifeni lamalungisa, Ukuze amalungisa angazisi ebugqwetheni
izandla zawo.

<span id="an_125:4">125:4</span> Yehova, yenza okulungileyo
kwabalungileyo, Kwabathe tye ezintliziyweni zabo.

<span id="an_125:5">125:5</span> Ke bona abathi gu bucala ngeendlela
zabo ezimagoso-goso, UYehova makabemkise, kunye nabasebenzi bobutshinga.
Malube luxolo kuSirayeli.

<span id="an_126:1">126:1</span> Ingoma yezinyuko. Ekubabuyiseni
kukaYehova ababuyayo baseZiyon, Saba njengabaphuphayo;

<span id="an_126:2">126:2</span> Waza wazala kukuhleka umlomo wethu,
Lwazala kukumemelela ulwimi lwethu. Baza bathi phakathi kweentlanga,
UYehova ubenzele izinto ezinkulu aba.

<span id="an_126:3">126:3</span> UYehova usenzele izinto ezinkulu, Saba
ngabavuyayo.

<span id="an_126:4">126:4</span> Buyisa, Yehova, abathinjiweyo bakuthi,
Njengemilambo yamanzi yelasezantsi.

<span id="an_126:5">126:5</span> Abahlwayelayo beneenyembezi Baya kuvuna
benokumemelela.

<span id="an_126:6">126:6</span> Ohamba ahambe elila, Ephethe
intlwayelelo, Uyabuya eze ememelela, Ethwele izithungu zakhe.

<span id="an_127:1">127:1</span> Ingoma yezinyuko. KaSolomon. Ukuba
akayakhi uYehova indlu, Bafumana besaphuka yiyo abakhi bayo. Ukuba umzi
akawugcini uYehova, Ufumana ephaphama owugcinayo.

<span id="an_127:2">127:2</span> Nifumana nivuka kusasa, Nihlale
nisebenza kude kube sebusuku, Nikudla ukudla kokubulaleka; Uyipha
intanda yakhe, ilele ubuthongo.

<span id="an_127:3">127:3</span> Uyabona, ilifa likaYehova ngoonyana,
Umvuzo sisiqhamo sesizalo.

<span id="an_127:4">127:4</span> Njengeentolo esandleni segorha, Banjalo
oonyana bobutsha.

<span id="an_127:5">127:5</span> Hayi, uyolo lomfo ozalise umphongolo
wakhe ngabo! Abayi kudana, Xa bathetha neentshaba esangweni.

<span id="an_128:1">128:1</span> Ingoma yezinyuko. Hayi, uyolo lwabantu
bonke abamoyikayo uYehova, Abahamba ngeendlela zakhe!

<span id="an_128:2">128:2</span> Ukuxelenga kwezandla zakho inene uya
kukudla, Uya kuba noyolo wena, kulunge kuwe.

<span id="an_128:3">128:3</span> Umkakho woba njengomdiliya oqhamayo
Endlwini yakho ngaphakathi; Oonyana bakho babe njengezithole zomnquma
Ngeenxa zonke esithebeni sakho.

<span id="an_128:4">128:4</span> Yabona, unjalo ukusikelelwa umfo
Omoyikayo uYehova.

<span id="an_128:5">128:5</span> Makakusikelele uYehova eZiyon. Uyibone
iYerusalem inenyhweba Yonke imihla yobomi bakho;

<span id="an_128:6">128:6</span> Ubone abantwana babantwana bakho.
Malube luxolo kuSirayeli.

<span id="an_129:1">129:1</span> Ingoma yezinyuko. Kukaninzi
bendibandezela kwasebuncinaneni bam, Makatsho uSirayeli;

<span id="an_129:2">129:2</span> Kukaninzi bendibandezela
kwasebuncinaneni bam: Ababanga nakundithini noko.

<span id="an_129:3">129:3</span> Abalimi balima emhlana kum, Bayolula
indima yabo.

<span id="an_129:4">129:4</span> UYehova ulilungisa, Uzinqumle izintya
zabangendawo.

<span id="an_129:5">129:5</span> Mabadane babuye umva Bonke abayithiyayo
iZiyon.

<span id="an_129:6">129:6</span> Mababe njengengca ephuma phezu
kwezindlu, Eyomayo ingekahlumi,

<span id="an_129:7">129:7</span> Engekasizalisi nesandla sakhe umvuni,
Engekalizalisi nesondo lengubo yakhe umbophi wezithungu;

<span id="an_129:8">129:8</span> Bengekathi nabadlulayo, Intsikelelo
kaYehova mayibe kuni; Siyanisikelela egameni likaYehova.

<span id="an_130:1">130:1</span> Ingoma yezinyuko. Ezinzulwini ndinqula
wena, Yehova,

<span id="an_130:2">130:2</span> Nkosi, yiva ilizwi lam. Iindlebe zakho
mazilibazele Ilizwi lokutarhuzisa kwam.

<span id="an_130:3">130:3</span> Ukuba uthe wabunqala ubugwenxa, Yehova,
Ngubani na ongaba nokuma, Nkosi?

<span id="an_130:4">130:4</span> Ngokuba kunawe ukuxolela, Ukuze
woyikwe.

<span id="an_130:5">130:5</span> Ndithembele kuYehova, uthembile
umphefumlo wam; Ndilinde ilizwi lakhe.

<span id="an_130:6">130:6</span> Umphefumlo wam ulindele eNkosini
Ngaphezu kwabalinde ukusa, Ewe, abalinde ukusa.

<span id="an_130:7">130:7</span> Lindela kuYehova, Sirayeli, Ngokuba
inceba ikuYehova; Ikuye inkululeko eninzi.

<span id="an_130:8">130:8</span> Yena ke wowakhulula amaSirayeli
Ebugwenxeni bawo bonke.

<span id="an_131:1">131:1</span> Ingoma yezinyuko; kaDavide. Yehova,
intliziyo yam ayiphakamile, amehlo am akaqwayingile; Andihambi ezintweni
ezinkulu, Eziyimisebenzi ebalulekileyo kum.

<span id="an_131:2">131:2</span> Inene, ndiwuzolise ndawuthozamisa
umphefumlo wam; Unjengomntwana olunyulweyo, ehleli kunina;
Unjengomntwana olunyulweyo umphefumlo wam kum.

<span id="an_131:3">131:3</span> Wena Sirayeli, lindela kuYehova
Kususela ngoku kude kuse ephakadeni.

<span id="an_132:1">132:1</span> Ingoma yezinyuko. Yehova, mkhumbulele
uDavide Ukucinezeleka kwakhe konke;

<span id="an_132:2">132:2</span> Yena wamfungelayo uYehova,
Wabhambathisa kwimbalasane enguThixo kaYakobi,

<span id="an_132:3">132:3</span> Esithi, Andiyi kungena ententeni
eyindlu yam, Andiyi kunyuka ndiye esililini, emandlalweni wam;

<span id="an_132:4">132:4</span> Andiyi kuwanika amehlo am ubuthongo,
Neenkophe zam ukozela:

<span id="an_132:5">132:5</span> Ndide ndimfumanele indawo uYehova,
Ndiyifumanele umnquba imbalasane kaYakobi.

<span id="an_132:6">132:6</span> Khangela, sawuva e-Efrata, Sawufumana
ezintilini zaseKiriyati-yeharim.

<span id="an_132:7">132:7</span> Masingene emnqubeni wakhe, Siqubude
esihlalweni seenyawo zakhe.

<span id="an_132:8">132:8</span> Khawusuk’ ume, Yehova, uze ekuphumleni
kwakho, Wena netyeya yamandla akho.

<span id="an_132:9">132:9</span> Ababingeleli bakho mabambathe
ubulungisa, Bamemelele abakho benceba.

<span id="an_132:10">132:10</span> Ngenxa kaDavide umkhonzi wakho, Musa
ukubutyhala ubuso bomthanjiswa wakho.

<span id="an_132:11">132:11</span> UYehova wamfungela uDavide; Inyaniso,
akayi kubuya kuloo nto, Esithi, Esiqhameni sezibilini zakho Ndimisa oya
kuba setroneni yakho.

<span id="an_132:12">132:12</span> Ukuba bathe oonyana bakho bawugcina
umnqophiso wam, Nesingqiniso sam endibafundisayo: Oonyana babo bothi
nabo bahlale Etroneni yakho nanini.

<span id="an_132:13">132:13</span> Ngokuba uYehova uyinyule iZiyon,
Uyinqwenele ukuba ibe likhaya lakhe;

<span id="an_132:14">132:14</span> Esithi, Nantsi indawo yam yokuphumla
kwam nanini; Ndiya kuhlala apha, ngokuba oko ndikunqwenele.

<span id="an_132:15">132:15</span> Umphako wayo ndiya kuwusikelela
kunene; Amahlwempu ayo ndiya kuwahluthisa ngesonka,

<span id="an_132:16">132:16</span> Ndibambathise ngosindiso ababingeleli
bayo, Abenceba bayo bamemelele bememelela.

<span id="an_132:17">132:17</span> Apho ndiya kumhlumisela uphondo
uDavide, Ndiya kumlungisela isibane umthanjiswa wam.

<span id="an_132:18">132:18</span> Iintshaba zakhe ndiya kuzambathisa
udano; Ke phezu kwakhe yena siya kutyatyamba isithsaba sakhe.

<span id="an_133:1">133:1</span> Ingoma yezinyuko; kaDavide. Yabonani,
ukuba kuhle, ukuba mnandi, Ukuthi abazalwana bahlale bemxhelo mnye!

<span id="an_133:2">133:2</span> Kunjengeoli elungileyo entloko, Isihla
ezindevini, Ezindevini zika-Aron, Isihla iye emqukumbelweni weengubo
zakhe.

<span id="an_133:3">133:3</span> Kunjengombethe waseHermon, Ohla phezu
kweentaba zaseZiyon; Ngokuba uYehova wayimisela khona apho intsikelelo,
Ubomi, kude kuse ephakadeni.

<span id="an_134:1">134:1</span> Ingoma yezinyuko. Yabonani, mbongeni
uYehova, nonke bakhonzi bakaYehova, Nimiyo endlwini kaYehova ebusuku.

<span id="an_134:2">134:2</span> Phakamiselani engcweleni izandla zenu,
Nimbonge uYehova.

<span id="an_134:3">134:3</span> Makakusikelele eZiyon uYehova, UMenzi
wezulu nehlabathi.

<span id="an_135:1">135:1</span> Haleluya. Dumisani igama likaYehova;
Dumisani, nina bakhonzi bakaYehova,

<span id="an_135:2">135:2</span> Nimiyo endlwini kaYehova,
Ezintendelezweni zendlu yoThixo wethu.

<span id="an_135:3">135:3</span> Dumisani uYehova, ngokuba elungile
uYehova; Libetheleni uhadi igama lakhe, ngokuba kumnandi.

<span id="an_135:4">135:4</span> Ngokuba uYehova unyule uYakobi ukuba
abe ngowakhe, Wanyula uSirayeli ukuba abe yinqobo kuye.

<span id="an_135:5">135:5</span> Ngokuba ndiyazi mna ukuba mkhulu
uYehova, INkosi yethu ingaphezu koothixo bonke.

<span id="an_135:6">135:6</span> Konke akuthandileyo uYehova uya kwenza,
Ezulwini nasemhlabeni, Ezilwandle nasemanzini onke enzonzobila.

<span id="an_135:7">135:7</span> Ulonyusa amafu eziphelweni zehlabathi,
Imvula wayenzela imibane; Ulorhola umoya koovimba bakhe.

<span id="an_135:8">135:8</span> Owawabulalayo amazibulo aseYiputa,
Ethabathele ebantwini wesa ezinkomeni;

<span id="an_135:9">135:9</span> Wathumela imiqondiso nezimanga Phakathi
kwakho, Yiputa, KuFaro nakubakhonzi bakhe bonke;

<span id="an_135:10">135:10</span> Owabulala iintlanga ezinkulu,
Wabulala ookumkani abanamandla;

<span id="an_135:11">135:11</span> OoSihon, ukumkani wama-Amori, No-Ogi,
ukumkani waseBhashan, Nezikumkani zonke zakwaKanan;

<span id="an_135:12">135:12</span> Walinikela ilizwe labo lalilifa,
Lalilifa kumaSirayeli, abantu bakhe,

<span id="an_135:13">135:13</span> Yehova, igama lakho lingunaphakade,
Inkumbuzo yakho, Yehova, ikwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana.

<span id="an_135:14">135:14</span> Ngokuba uYehova uya kugweba phakathi
kwabantu bakhe, Azohlwaye ngenxa yabakhonzi bakhe.

<span id="an_135:15">135:15</span> Izithixo zeentlanga yisilivere
negolide, Umsebenzi wezandla zabantu.

<span id="an_135:16">135:16</span> Zinomlomo nje, azithethi; Zinamehlo
nje, aziboni;

<span id="an_135:17">135:17</span> Zineendlebe nje, aziva; Akukho nento
engumoya emlonyeni wazo.

<span id="an_135:18">135:18</span> Baya kuba njengazo abenzi bazo, Bonke
abasukuba bekholose ngazo.

<span id="an_135:19">135:19</span> Nina ndlu kaSirayeli, bongani
uYehova; Nani ndlu ka-Aron, bongani uYehova.

<span id="an_135:20">135:20</span> Nina ndlu kaLevi, bongani uYehova;
Nani boyika uYehova, bongani uYehova.

<span id="an_135:21">135:21</span> Ngowokubongwa uYehova eZiyon,
Ulohlala eYerusalem. Haleluya!

<span id="an_136:1">136:1</span> Bulelani kuYehova, ngokuba elungile:
Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_136:2">136:2</span> Bulelani kuThixo woothixo: Ngokuba
ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_136:3">136:3</span> Bulelani kuNkosi kankosi: Ngokuba
ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_136:4">136:4</span> KuloMenzi wemisebenzi ebalulekileyo
emikhulu yedwa: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_136:5">136:5</span> KuloMenzi wezulu ngengqondo: Ngokuba
ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_136:6">136:6</span> KuloMtwabululi wehlabathi phezu
kwamanzi: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_136:7">136:7</span> KuloMenzi wezikhanyiso ezikhulu:
Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe;

<span id="an_136:8">136:8</span> Ilanga lilawule emini: Ngokuba
ingunaphakade inceba yakhe;

<span id="an_136:9">136:9</span> Inyanga neenkwenkwezi zilawule ebusuku:
Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_136:10">136:10</span> Kulowabulala amaYiputa kumazibulo
awo: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_136:11">136:11</span> Wawakhupha amaSirayeli phakathi
kwawo: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_136:12">136:12</span> Ngesandla esithe nkqi, nangengalo
eyolukileyo: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_136:13">136:13</span> KuloMgabuli woLwandle oluBomvu,
lwagabuka: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_136:14">136:14</span> Wawaweza amaSirayeli esazulwini salo:
Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_136:15">136:15</span> Wamvuthululela uFaro nempi yakhe
eLwandle oluBomvu: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_136:16">136:16</span> Kulohambisa abantu bakhe entlango:
Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_136:17">136:17</span> Kulowaxabela ookumkani abakhulu:
Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_136:18">136:18</span> Wabulala ookumkani abaziingangamsha:
Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe;

<span id="an_136:19">136:19</span> USihon, ukumkani wama-Amori: Ngokuba
ingunaphakade inceba yakhe;

<span id="an_136:20">136:20</span> No-Ogi, ukumkani waseBhashan: Ngokuba
ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_136:21">136:21</span> Walinikela ilizwe labo laba lilifa:
Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe,

<span id="an_136:22">136:22</span> Laba lilifa kuSirayeli umkhonzi
wakhe: Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_136:23">136:23</span> Owasikhumbulayo ebuphantsini bethu:
Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_136:24">136:24</span> Wasihlangula kwabasibandezelayo:
Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_136:25">136:25</span> Ulonika into yonke ephilileyo ukudla:
Ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_136:26">136:26</span> Bulelani kuThixo wamazulu: Ngokuba
ingunaphakade inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_137:1">137:1</span> NgaseMilanjeni yaseBhabheli Sahlala
phantsi khona, salila, Sakuyikhumbula iZiyon.

<span id="an_137:2">137:2</span> Emingculubeni phakathi kwayo Sazixhoma
khona iihadi zethu.

<span id="an_137:3">137:3</span> Ngokuba khona apho abathimbi bethu
basibiza Izango zengoma; Abathuthumbisi bethu basibiza uvuyo, Besithi,
Sivumeleni ingoma yaseZiyon.

<span id="an_137:4">137:4</span> Singathini na ukuvuma ingoma kaYehova
Emhlabeni wolunye uhlanga?

<span id="an_137:5">137:5</span> Ukuba ndithe ndakulibala, Yerusalem,
Masinyele isandla sam sokunene.

<span id="an_137:6">137:6</span> Ulwimi lwam malunamathele
ekhuhlangubeni lam, Ukuba andithanga ndikukhumbule; Ukuba andithanga
ndiyinyuse iYerusalem Ngaphezu kwemivuyo yam yonke.

<span id="an_137:7">137:7</span> Bakhumbule, Yehova, oonyana bakaEdom,
Umhla weYerusalem, Abo bathi, Yidilizeni, yidilizeni Kuse elusekweni
lwayo.

<span id="an_137:8">137:8</span> Ntombi inguBhabheli, wena unyashiweyo;
Hayi, uyolo lwalowo ukubuyekezayo ukuphatha kwakho Osiphethe ngako!

<span id="an_137:9">137:9</span> Hayi, uyolo lwalowo ubabambayo
abahlekeze abantwana bakho Engxondorheni!

<span id="an_138:1">138:1</span> EkaDavide. Ndiya kubulela kuwe
ngentliziyo yam yonke; Phambi koothixo ndiya kukubethela uhadi.

<span id="an_138:2">138:2</span> Ndiya kuqubuda ndibhekise etempileni
yakho engcwele, Ndibulele kwigama lakho, ngenxa yenceba yakho, nangenxa
yenyaniso yakho; Kuba ulikhulisile ilizwi lakho ngaphezu kwegama lakho
lonke.

<span id="an_138:3">138:3</span> Ngomhla wokubiza kwam wandiphendula,
Wandikhaliphisa, yangamandla emphefumlweni wam.

<span id="an_138:4">138:4</span> Baya kubulela kuwe, Yehova, bonke
ookumkani behlabathi, Bakuweva amazwi omlomo wakho;

<span id="an_138:5">138:5</span> Bavume ngeendlela zikaYehova, Ukuba
lukhulu uzuko lukaYehova:

<span id="an_138:6">138:6</span> Ngokuba noko uYehova aphakamileyo,
uyambona othobekileyo; Ke yena oziphakamisayo umazi nakude.

<span id="an_138:7">138:7</span> Ukuba ndithe ndahamba-hamba phakathi
kweembandezelo, uyandiphilisa; Wosolulela emsindweni weentshaba zam
isandla sakho, Sindisindise isandla sakho sokunene.

<span id="an_138:8">138:8</span> UYehova uya kundifezela. Yehova, inceba
yakho ingunaphakade, Izenzo zezandla zakho musa ukuziyekela.

<span id="an_139:1">139:1</span> Kumongameli; ekaDavide. Umhobe. Yehova,
undigocagocile, wandazi.

<span id="an_139:2">139:2</span> Wena uyakwazi ukuhlala kwam nokusuka
kwam; Uyaziqonda izicamango zam nakude.

<span id="an_139:3">139:3</span> Ukuhamba kwam nokulala kwam, uyakwela;
Uqhelene neendlela zam zonke.

<span id="an_139:4">139:4</span> Ngokuba akukho lizwi elulwimini lwam
Ongalaziyo ke, Yehova, kanye.

<span id="an_139:5">139:5</span> Ngasemva nangaphambili undingqingile,
Wasibeka phezu kwam isandla sakho.

<span id="an_139:6">139:6</span> Kubalulekile kum oko kwazi, Kuphezulu,
kundinqabele.

<span id="an_139:7">139:7</span> Ndingahambela phi na ukumka emoyeni
wakho? Ndingabalekela phi na ukumka ebusweni bakho?

<span id="an_139:8">139:8</span> Ukuba ndithe ndenyuka ndaya emazulwini,
ulapho wena; Ukuba ndithe ndazandlalela kwelabafileyo, nanko ukho.

<span id="an_139:9">139:9</span> Ukuba ndithe ndaphakamisa amaphiko
esifingo, Ndaya ndahlala ekupheleni kolwandle,

<span id="an_139:10">139:10</span> Besingandikhaphayo kwanalapho isandla
sakho, Sindibambe isandla sakho sokunene.

<span id="an_139:11">139:11</span> Ukuba ndithe, Mabundisongele
ubumnyama bona bodwa, Nokukhanya kube bubusuku ngeenxa zonke kum:

<span id="an_139:12">139:12</span> Kwanobumnyama obo abungebi bubumnyama
kuwe; Ubusuku bungaba mhlophe njengemini, Ubumnyama bungaba
njengokukhanya

<span id="an_139:13">139:13</span> Ngokuba wena wazibumba izintso zam,
Wandibiyela esizalweni sikama.

<span id="an_139:14">139:14</span> Ndiyabulela kuwe ngenxa enokuba
ndenziwe ngokoyikekayo, ngokubalulekileyo; Zibalulekile izenzo zakho,
Umphefumlo wam uyazi kakuhle.

<span id="an_139:15">139:15</span> Ayengagushekile kuwe amathambo am,
Mna ndenzelwayo entsithelweni, Ndalukwa ndayimfakamfele ezinzulwini
zomhlaba.

<span id="an_139:16">139:16</span> Amehlo akho andibona ndiseyimbumba,
Zazibhalwe encwadini yakho iimini zonke ziphela; Ziyiliwe ngenxa
engaphambili, Kungekabikho ke nanye kuzo.

<span id="an_139:17">139:17</span> Kum ke zinjani na ukunqaba izicamango
zakho, Thixo! Asingangani isimbuku sazo!

<span id="an_139:18">139:18</span> Zingathi, ndizibalile, zibe ninzi
ngaphezu kwentlabathi; Ndakuvuka ndoba ndisenawe.

<span id="an_139:19">139:19</span> Ngamana wambulala ongendawo, Thixo!
Nina madoda amagazi, sukani kum.

<span id="an_139:20">139:20</span> Abo bakukhankanyela amayelenqe,
Balibizela inkohlakalo igama lakho abazondi bakho.

<span id="an_139:21">139:21</span> Andinakubathiya na abakuthiyayo,
Yehova, Ndikruquke ngabasukela phezulu kuwe?

<span id="an_139:22">139:22</span> Ndibathiya ngentiyo ephelelisileyo,
Kum mna baziintshaba.

<span id="an_139:23">139:23</span> Ndigocagoce, Thixo, uyazi intliziyo
yam; Ndicikide, uzazi iingcinga-ngcinga zam;

<span id="an_139:24">139:24</span> Ubone ukuba kukho ndlela yobubi na
kum, Undikhaphele kwindlela engunaphakade.

<span id="an_140:1">140:1</span> Kumongameli. Umhobe kaDavide.
Ndihlangule, Yehova, esintwini esinobubi, Ndilondoloze emntwini
ogonyamelayo,

<span id="an_140:2">140:2</span> Abacinga okubi entliziyweni. Imihla
yonke baxhaya imfazwe.

<span id="an_140:3">140:3</span> Balola ulwimi lwabo njengenyoka;
Ubuhlungu berhamba busemlonyeni wabo (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_140:4">140:4</span> Ndigcine, Yehova, ezandleni zongendawo,
Ndilondoloze emntwini ogonyamelayo, Abacinga ukuzikhubekisa iinyawo zam.

<span id="an_140:5">140:5</span> Abanekratshi bandiqhushekele isibatha
nezintya, Baneke umnatha ecaleni kwendlela, Bandithiyele ngemigibe.
(Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_140:6">140:6</span> Ndithi kuYehova, UnguThixo wam; Beka
indlebe, Yehova, elizwini lesikhungo sam.

<span id="an_140:7">140:7</span> Yehova, Nkosi yam, nqaba endisindisayo,
Uyigqubuthele intloko yam ngemini yeduli.

<span id="an_140:8">140:8</span> Musa ukumnika, Yehova, ongendawo
iminqweno yakhe; Musa ukuwuphumelelisa umnkqangiyelo wakhe, Hleze
aziphakamise. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_140:9">140:9</span> Yona intloko yabandingqingayo, Ububi
bomlomo wabo mabubagubungele.

<span id="an_140:10">140:10</span> Mabathotyelwe amalahle avuthayo;
Makabawise emlilweni, emimbithini, bangabi saphuma.

<span id="an_140:11">140:11</span> Indoda enolwimi mayingazinzi
ehlabathini; Indoda enokugonyamela, ububi mabuyizingele ngembembetshane.

<span id="an_140:12">140:12</span> Ndiyazi ukuba uYehova uya kulifeza
Ityala losizana, ibango lamahlwempu.

<span id="an_140:13">140:13</span> Inene, amalungisa aya kubulela
kwigama lakho; Baya kuhlala ebusweni bakho abathe tye.

<span id="an_141:1">141:1</span> Umhobe kaDavide. Yehova, ndiyakunqula,
khawuleza uze kum; Libekele indlebe izwi lam ekudandulukeni kwam kuwe.

<span id="an_141:2">141:2</span> Umthandazo wam mawuhlale uhleli phambi
kwakho usisiqhumiso, Nokuphakamisa kwam izandla kube ngumnikelo
wangokuhlwa.

<span id="an_141:3">141:3</span> Umlomo wam wumisele umlindi, Yehova;
Misa umgcini emnyango womlomo wam.

<span id="an_141:4">141:4</span> Intliziyo yam musa ukuyithobela entweni
embi, Ukuba isebenze intlondi yokungendawo Namadoda asebenza ubutshinga;
Mandingazidli izimnandi zawo.

<span id="an_141:5">141:5</span> Malindibethe ilungisa linenceba,
lindohlwaye; Ioli enjalo yentloko ayingeyali intloko yam: Ngokuba usekho
nomthandazo wam ebubini bawo.

<span id="an_141:6">141:6</span> Bakhahlelwa emacaleni engxondorha
abagwebi bawo, Beve amazwi am ukuba amnandi.

<span id="an_141:7">141:7</span> Njengolimayo enqika umhlaba, Anjalo
ukuthi saa amathambo ethu emlonyeni wengcwaba.

<span id="an_141:8">141:8</span> Ngokuba akuwe, Yehova, Nkosi yam,
amehlo am; Ndizimela ngawe; musa ukuwuphalaza umphefumlo wam.

<span id="an_141:9">141:9</span> Ndigcine esangweni lomgibe
wabandithiyelayo, Nasezirhintyelweni zabasebenza ubutshinga.

<span id="an_141:10">141:10</span> Mabeyele ezintanjeni zabo
abangendawo, Ndide ndidlule mna okukanye.

<span id="an_142:1">142:1</span> Eyokuqiqa kaDavide; oko
ebesemqolombeni. Umthandazo. Ndikhala kuYehova ngezwi lam, Ndikhunga
uYehova ngezwi lam,

<span id="an_142:2">142:2</span> Ndiphalaza inkalazo yam phambi kwakhe,
Ndixela imbandezelo yam phambi kwakhe.

<span id="an_142:3">142:3</span> Ekutyhafeni komoya phakathi kwam,
Uyayazi wena ingqushu yam. Emendweni endihamba ngawo Bandiqhushekela
isibatha.

<span id="an_142:4">142:4</span> Bheka ngasekunene ubone, Akukho
undibukayo; Andinandawo ndingasabela kuyo, Akukho uwukhathaleleyo
umphefumlo wam.

<span id="an_142:5">142:5</span> Ndikhala kuwe, Yehova, Ndithi, Nguwe
ihlathi lam, Isabelo sam ezweni labahleliyo.

<span id="an_142:6">142:6</span> Kubazele indlebe ukuhlahlamba kwam,
Ngokuba ndiswele kakhulu: Ndihlangule kwabandisukelayo, Ngokuba bomelele
kunam.

<span id="an_142:7">142:7</span> Wukhuphe entolongweni umphefumlo wam,
Ndibulele kwigama lakho. Amalungisa aya kuzithi jize ngesithsaba ngenxa
yam, Ngokuba undiphethe kakuhle.

<span id="an_143:1">143:1</span> Umhobe kaDavide. Yehova, yiva
umthandazo wam, kubekele indlebe ukutarhuzisa kwam; Ndiphendule
ngokunyaniseka kwakho, ngobulungisa bakho.

<span id="an_143:2">143:2</span> Musa ukumsa ematyaleni umkhonzi wakho:
Ngokuba phambi kwakho akukho namnye uhleliyo olilungisa.

<span id="an_143:3">143:3</span> Ngokuba utshaba luwusukele umphefumlo
wam, Lubutyumzele emhlabeni ubomi bam; Lundihlalise ezindaweni
ezimnyama, njengabafe ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_143:4">143:4</span> Utyhafile phakathi kwam umoya wam;
Imangalisiwe phakathi kwam intliziyo yam.

<span id="an_143:5">143:5</span> Ndikhumbula imihla yamandulo;
Ndicamngca ngemisebenzi yakho yonke, Ndicamngca ngesenzo sezandla zakho.

<span id="an_143:6">143:6</span> Ndizolulela kuwe izandla zam,
Umphefumlo wam ukungxamele njengelizwe elibharhileyo. (Phakamisani.)

<span id="an_143:7">143:7</span> Khawuleza undiphendule, Yehova;
uyaphela umoya wam. Musa ukubusithelisa kum ubuso bakho, Ndifane nabahla
baye emhadini.

<span id="an_143:8">143:8</span> Ndivise kwakusasa inceba yakho, Ngokuba
ndikholose ngawe. Ndazise indlela endiya kuhamba ngayo: Ngokuba
ndiwuphakamisela kuwe umphefumlo wam.

<span id="an_143:9">143:9</span> Ndihlangule ezintshabeni zam, Yehova.
Ndizimela ngawe.

<span id="an_143:10">143:10</span> Ndifundise ukwenza ikholo lakho,
ngokuba unguThixo wam. UMoya wakho olungileyo makandikhaphele ezweni
elisithabazi.

<span id="an_143:11">143:11</span> Ngenxa yegama lakho, Yehova,
ndiphilise; Wukhuphe embandezelweni umphefumlo wam ngobulungisa bakho.

<span id="an_143:12">143:12</span> Ngenceba yakho zibhangise iintshaba
zam, Ubatshabalalise bonke abawubandezelayo umphefumlo wam, Ngokuba
ndingumkhonzi wakho.

<span id="an_144:1">144:1</span> EkaDavide. Makabongwe uYehova, uliwa
lam, Ulofundisa izandla zam ukulwa, Iminwe yam imfazwe.

<span id="an_144:2">144:2</span> Unceba yam, umboniselo yam, Ungxonde
yam, umsindisi wam, mna lo; Ungweletshetshe yam, undizimela ngaye;
Ulonyathelela abantu bam phantsi kwam.

<span id="an_144:3">144:3</span> Yehova, uyintoni na umntu, le nto
umaziyo? Unyana womfo, le nto umnyamekelayo?

<span id="an_144:4">144:4</span> Umntu lo ufana nomphunga, Imihla yakhe
injengethunzi elidlulayo.

<span id="an_144:5">144:5</span> Yehova, thoba amazulu akho, uhle;
Phatha ezintabeni, ziqhume.

<span id="an_144:6">144:6</span> Banekisa imibane, uziphangalalise;
Thuma iintolo zakho, uziduba-dube.

<span id="an_144:7">144:7</span> Thuma izandla zakho, zivele phezulu;
Ndirhole, ndihlangule emanzini amakhulu. Esandleni soonyana bolunye
uhlanga;

<span id="an_144:8">144:8</span> Abamlomo uthetha inkohlakalo, Abasandla
sokunene sisesokunene sobuxoki.

<span id="an_144:9">144:9</span> Thixo, ndokuvumela ingoma entsha,
Ndikubethele umrhubhe ontambo zilishumi;

<span id="an_144:10">144:10</span> Ulonika ookumkani usindiso,
Ulohlangula uDavide umkhonzi wakhe ekreleni elinobubi.

<span id="an_144:11">144:11</span> Ndirhole, ndihlangule esandleni
soonyana bolunye uhlanga, Abamlomo uthetha inkohlakalo, Abasandla
sokunene sisesokunene sobuxoki;

<span id="an_144:12">144:12</span> Baze oonyana bethu babe njengezityalo
ezikhulileyo ebutsheni babo; Iintombi zethu zibe njengeembombo
ezivathisiweyo ngeemfakamfele ngokokwakhiwa kwebhotwe;

<span id="an_144:13">144:13</span> Oovimba bethu bazale, bavelise
iintlobo ngeentlobo; Iigusha zethu zizale amawaka, zande ngezigidi
emaphandleni ethu;

<span id="an_144:14">144:14</span> Iinkomo zethu zizale, Kungabikho
kungenelwa, kungabikho kuthinjwa, Kungabikho kuhlahlamba ezitratweni
zethu.

<span id="an_144:15">144:15</span> Hayi, uyolo lwabantu ekunjalo kubo!
Hayi, uyolo lwabantu abaThixo unguYehova!

<span id="an_145:1">145:1</span> Eyokudumisa kaDavide. Ndiya
kukuphakamisa, Thixo wam, wena Kumkani, Ndilibonge igama lakho
ngonaphakade kanaphakade.

<span id="an_145:2">145:2</span> Imihla yonke ndiya kukubonga,
Ndilidumise igama lakho ngonaphakade kanaphakade.

<span id="an_145:3">145:3</span> Mkhulu uYehova, ngowokudunyiswa
kakhulu; Ubukhulu bakhe abunakugocwagocwa.

<span id="an_145:4">145:4</span> Izizukulwana ngezizukulwana, kunconywa
izenzo zakho, Kuxelwe ubugorha bakho.

<span id="an_145:5">145:5</span> Bunobungangamela ubuqaqawuli bendili
yakho; Ngeendawo zakho ezibalulekileyo ndiya kucamngca.

<span id="an_145:6">145:6</span> Bothetha ngamandla ezenzo zakho
ezoyikekayo, Ndibalise ngobukhulu bakho.

<span id="an_145:7">145:7</span> Bompompoza isikhumbuzo sokulunga kwakho
okukhulu, Bamemelele ngobulungisa bakho.

<span id="an_145:8">145:8</span> Unobabalo nemfesane uYehova, Uzeka kade
umsindo, mkhulu ngenceba.

<span id="an_145:9">145:9</span> Ulungile uYehova kubo bonke, Imfesane
yakhe ikuzo zonke izenzo zakhe.

<span id="an_145:10">145:10</span> Ziyabulela kuwe, Yehova, zonke izenzo
zakho, Bakubonge abakho benceba;

<span id="an_145:11">145:11</span> Uzuko lobukumkani bakho balutsho,
Bathethe ngobugorha bakho.

<span id="an_145:12">145:12</span> Ukuba babazise oonyana babantu
ubugorha bakhe, Ubuqaqawuli obuhle bobukumkani bakhe.

<span id="an_145:13">145:13</span> Ubukumkani bakho bubukumkani
bamaphakade onke, Nolawulo lwakho lukwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana.

<span id="an_145:14">145:14</span> UYehova ungumxhasi wabo bonke
abawayo, Ngumphakamisi wabo bonke abagobileyo.

<span id="an_145:15">145:15</span> Amehlo eento zonke akhangele kuwe,
Wena ke uzinika ukudla kwazo ngexesha elililo;

<span id="an_145:16">145:16</span> Uyasivula isandla sakho, Uzihluthise
iinto zonke eziphilileyo ngeento ezikholekileyo.

<span id="an_145:17">145:17</span> Ulilungisa uYehova ngeendlela zakhe
zonke, Unenceba ngezenzo zakhe zonke.

<span id="an_145:18">145:18</span> Usondele uYehova kubo bonke
abamnqulayo, Kubo bonke abamnqulayo ngenyaniso.

<span id="an_145:19">145:19</span> Uyayenza into ekholekileyo
kwabamoyikayo, Akuve ukuzibika kwabo, abasindise.

<span id="an_145:20">145:20</span> UYehova ungumgcini wabo bonke
abamthandayo, Abatshabalalise bonke abangendawo.

<span id="an_145:21">145:21</span> Umlomo wam mawuthethe indumiso
kaYehova, Inyama yonke ilibonge igama lakhe elingcwele ngonaphakade
kanaphakade.

<span id="an_146:1">146:1</span> Haleluya! Mdumise uYehova, mphefumlo
wam.

<span id="an_146:2">146:2</span> Ndiya kumdumisa uYehova lo gama ndidla
ubomi; Ndiya kumbethela uhadi uThixo wam ekubeni ndingosekhoyo.

<span id="an_146:3">146:3</span> Musani ukukholosa ngamanene, Ngonyana
womntu, yena ungenalo usindiso.

<span id="an_146:4">146:4</span> Uyaphuma umoya wakhe, abuyele yena
emhlabeni wakhe; Ngaloo mini ayatshitsha amabhongo akhe.

<span id="an_146:5">146:5</span> Hayi, uyolo lwalowo uluncedo lunguThixo
kaYakobi, Lwalowo ulinde kuYehova uThixo wakhe:

<span id="an_146:6">146:6</span> KuMenzi wezulu nomhlaba, Nolwandle
neento zonke ezikulo; Kulogcina inyaniso ngonaphakade;

<span id="an_146:7">146:7</span> Kogweba ityala labacudiswayo; Kopha
abalambileyo ukudla; KuYehova okhulula ababanjwa;

<span id="an_146:8">146:8</span> KuYehova ovula amehlo eemfama; KuYehova
ophakamisa abagobileyo; KuYehova othanda amalungisa;

<span id="an_146:9">146:9</span> KuYehova ogcina abaphambukeli;
Kulophakamisa inkedama nomhlolokazi, Ayiphethule indlela yabangendawo.

<span id="an_146:10">146:10</span> UYehova ungukumkani ngonaphakade,
UThixo wakho, Ziyon, kwizizukulwana ngezizukulwana. Haleluya!

<span id="an_147:1">147:1</span> Haleluya! Ngokuba kulungile ukuvuma
ngoThixo wethu; Ngokuba kumnandi, ifanelekile indumiso.

<span id="an_147:2">147:2</span> Umakhi weYerusalem nguYehova;
Abagxothwa bakwaSirayeli ubabuthela khona.

<span id="an_147:3">147:3</span> Ulophilisa abaphuke intliziyo, Abophe
amanxeba abo;

<span id="an_147:4">147:4</span> Ulobala inani leenkwenkwezi, Ezibiza
zonke ngamagama.

<span id="an_147:5">147:5</span> Inkulu iNkosi yethu, inamandla
amakhulu; Ingqondo yayo ayiphele ndawo.

<span id="an_147:6">147:6</span> Ulophakamisa abalulamileyo nguYehova,
Uthobela abangendawo emhlabeni.

<span id="an_147:7">147:7</span> Hlabelani kuYehova eyokubulela,
Mbetheleni uhadi uThixo wethu.

<span id="an_147:8">147:8</span> Ulosibekelisa izulu ngamafu,
Ulolungisela umhlaba imvula; Ulontshulisa utyani ezintabeni;

<span id="an_147:9">147:9</span> Ulonika inkomo ukudla, Namathole
ehlungulu alilayo.

<span id="an_147:10">147:10</span> Akabunanze nganto ubugorha behashe,
Akakholiswa zizitho zendoda;

<span id="an_147:11">147:11</span> UYehova ukholiswa ngabamoyikayo,
Abalinde inceba yakhe.

<span id="an_147:12">147:12</span> Mncome uYehova, Yerusalem. Mdumise
uThixo wakho, Ziyon:

<span id="an_147:13">147:13</span> Ngokuba eyomelezile imivalo yamasango
akho, Ebasikelele abantwana bakho phakathi kwakho.

<span id="an_147:14">147:14</span> Ngulomisa uxolo emideni yakho,
Wakuhluthisa ngengqolowa etyebileyo.

<span id="an_147:15">147:15</span> Ulothumela intetho yakhe ehlabathini,
Ilizwi lakhe ligidima ngokukhawuleza;

<span id="an_147:16">147:16</span> Ulonika ikhephu njengoboya bezimvu,
Ugcwayela iqabaka njengothuthu,

<span id="an_147:17">147:17</span> Ephosa umkhenkce wakhe
njengamaqhekeza; Ngubani na onokuma phambi kwengqele yakhe?

<span id="an_147:18">147:18</span> Uthumela ilizwi lakhe, ezo nto
azinyibilikise; Uvuthuzisa umoya wakhe, aqukuqele amanzi.

<span id="an_147:19">147:19</span> Uloxelela uYakobi ilizwi lakhe,
USirayeli imimiselo yakhe namasiko akhe.

<span id="an_147:20">147:20</span> Akenjanga ngalo kolunye uhlanga,
Namasiko aluwazi. Haleluya!

<span id="an_148:1">148:1</span> Haleluya! Dumisani uYehova emazulwini;
Mdumiseni ezindaweni eziphezulu.

<span id="an_148:2">148:2</span> Mdumiseni, nonke zithunywa zakhe;
Mdumiseni, nonke mikhosi yakhe;

<span id="an_148:3">148:3</span> Mdumiseni, wena langa, nawe nyanga;
Mdumiseni, nonke zinkwenkwezi zinokukhanya;

<span id="an_148:4">148:4</span> Mdumiseni, mazulu awo amazulu, Nani,
manzi angaphezu kwezulu.

<span id="an_148:5">148:5</span> Mazilidumise ezo nto igama likaYehova;
Ngokuba wawisa umthetho, zadalwa.

<span id="an_148:6">148:6</span> Wazimisa ngonaphakade kanaphakade,
Wazimisela ummiselo ezingayi kuwugqitha.

<span id="an_148:7">148:7</span> Dumisani uYehova ehlabathini, Nina
bominenga, nani nonke, manzi enzonzobila:

<span id="an_148:8">148:8</span> Wena mlilo, nawe sichotho; wena khephu,
nawe msi; Moya uvuthuzayo, ulenzayo ilizwi lakhe;

<span id="an_148:9">148:9</span> Nina zintaba, nani zinduli nonke, Nina
mithi eneziqhamo, nani misedare nonke;

<span id="an_148:10">148:10</span> Nina marhamncwa, nani zinkomo nonke,
Nina zinambuzane, nani zintaka zinamaphiko;

<span id="an_148:11">148:11</span> Ookumkani behlabathi, nezizwe zonke,
Abathetheli nabagwebi behlabathi lonke;

<span id="an_148:12">148:12</span> Umlisela kwanomthinjana, Amadoda
amakhulu kunye nabafana:

<span id="an_148:13">148:13</span> Mabalidumise igama likaYehova,
Ngokuba liyingxonde igama lakhe yena yedwa; Indili yakhe ingaphezu
komhlaba nezulu.

<span id="an_148:14">148:14</span> Wabaphakamisela abantu bakhe uphondo,
Lwayindumiso kwabakhe benceba bonke, Koonyana bakaSirayeli, abantu
abasondeleyo kuye. Haleluya!

<span id="an_149:1">149:1</span> Haleluya! Mvumeleni uYehova ingoma
entsha, Indumiso yakhe ebandleni labenceba.

<span id="an_149:2">149:2</span> USirayeli makavuye ngoMenzi wakhe;
Usapho lwaseZiyon malugcobe ngoKumkani walo.

<span id="an_149:3">149:3</span> Mabalidumise igama lakhe beqamba,
Bembethela ingqongqo nohadi.

<span id="an_149:4">149:4</span> Ngokuba uYehova uyakholiswa ngabantu
bakhe, Uyabahombisa abalulamileyo ngoloyiso.

<span id="an_149:5">149:5</span> Mabadlamke benozuko abenceba,
Mabamemelele besezililini zabo.

<span id="an_149:6">149:6</span> Yimibongo kaThixo emqaleni wabo,
Likrele elintlangothi mbini esandleni sabo;

<span id="an_149:7">149:7</span> Ukuze benze impindezelo ezintlangeni,
Izohlwayo ezizweni;

<span id="an_149:8">149:8</span> Bakhonkxe ookumkani bazo
ngemixokelelwane, Nabazukileyo kuzo ngamakhamandela esinyithi;

<span id="an_149:9">149:9</span> Benze kubo isiko elibhaliweyo. Luzuko
olo lwabakhe benceba bonke. Haleluya!

<span id="an_150:1">150:1</span> Haleluya! Dumisani uThixo engcweleni
yakhe, Mdumiseni esibhakabhakeni samandla akhe.

<span id="an_150:2">150:2</span> Mdumiseni ngenxa yobugorha bakhe,
Mdumiseni ngokobuninzi bobukhulu bakhe.

<span id="an_150:3">150:3</span> Mdumiseni ngokuvuthela isigodlo,
Mdumiseni ngomrhubhe nohadi.

<span id="an_150:4">150:4</span> Mdumiseni ngengqongqo nengqungqo,
Mdumiseni ngeento ezineentambo nogwali.

<span id="an_150:5">150:5</span> Mdumiseni ngamacangci akhenkcezayo,
Mdumiseni ngamacangci adumayo.

<span id="an_150:6">150:6</span> Yonke into ephefumlayo mayimdumise
uYehova. Haleluya!

------------------------------------------------------------------------
